   160	def _get_routing_allowlist() -> set[str]:
   161	    """Return the set of environment variable names allowed for export."""
   162	    return {
   163	        # Dopemux Identity
   164	        "DOPEMUX_INSTANCE_ID",
   165	        "DOPEMUX_WORKSPACE_ID",
   166	        "DOPEMUX_CLAUDE_VIA_LITELLM",
   167	        "DOPEMUX_DEFAULT_LITELLM",
   168	        
   169	        # Anthropic / LiteLLM Auth
   170	        "ANTHROPIC_BASE_URL",
   171	        "ANTHROPIC_API_BASE",
   172	        "ANTHROPIC_API_KEY",
   173	        "LITELLM_MASTER_KEY",
   174	        "DOPEMUX_LITELLM_MASTER_KEY",
   175	        
   176	        # Database (if needed for metrics)
   177	        "DOPEMUX_LITELLM_DB_URL",
   178	        "LITELLM_DATABASE_URL",
   179	        "DATABASE_URL",
   180	        
   181	        # Claude Code Router (CCR)
   182	        "CLAUDE_CODE_ROUTER_PORT",
   183	        "CLAUDE_CODE_ROUTER_HOME",
   184	        "CLAUDE_CODE_ROUTER_CONFIG",
   185	        "CLAUDE_CODE_ROUTER_LOG",
   186	        "CLAUDE_CODE_ROUTER_PROVIDER",
   187	        "CLAUDE_CODE_ROUTER_MODELS",
   188	        "CLAUDE_CODE_ROUTER_UPSTREAM_URL",
   189	        "CLAUDE_CODE_ROUTER_UPSTREAM_KEY_VAR",
   190	        "CLAUDE_CODE_ROUTER_UPSTREAM_KEY",
   191	    }

   194	def _persist_instance_env_exports(
   195	    project_root: Path, instance_id: str, env_vars: Dict[str, str]
   196	) -> None:
   197	    """
   198	    Persist instance environment variables for use outside Dopemux processes.
   199	
   200	    Writes both `export`-style and `.env`-style files with a strict allowlist
   201	    of routing and identity variables.
   202	    """
   203	    try:
   204	        target_dir = project_root / ".dopemux" / "env"
   205	        target_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
   206	
   207	        slug = instance_id or "A"
   208	        export_path = target_dir / f"instance_{slug}.sh"
   209	        env_path = target_dir / f"instance_{slug}.env"
   210	
   211	        allowlist = _get_routing_allowlist()
   212	        export_secrets = os.environ.get("DOPEMUX_EXPORT_SECRETS") == "1"
   213	        
   214	        filtered_vars = {}
   215	        for k, v in env_vars.items():
   216	            if k not in allowlist:
   217	                continue
   218	                
   219	            # Pattern-based secret detection
   220	            is_secret = any(p in k for p in ("API_KEY", "TOKEN", "SECRET", "PASSWORD", "MASTER_KEY"))
   221	            if is_secret and not export_secrets:
   222	                continue
   223	                
   224	            filtered_vars[k] = v
   225	            
   226	        sorted_items = sorted(filtered_vars.items())
   227	
   228	        with export_path.open("w", encoding="utf-8") as export_file:
   229	            export_file.write("#!/usr/bin/env bash\n")
   230	            export_file.write("# Autogenerated by Dopemux – current instance environment\n")
   231	            export_file.write("# Source this file in your shell to mirror Dopemux routing context.\n\n")
   232	            for key, value in sorted_items:
   233	                value_str = "" if value is None else str(value)
   234	                export_file.write(f"export {key}={shlex.quote(value_str)}\n")
   235	
   236	        with env_path.open("w", encoding="utf-8") as env_file:
   237	            env_file.write("# Autogenerated by Dopemux – docker-compose compatible env file\n")
   238	            for key, value in sorted_items:
   239	                value_str = "" if value is None else str(value)
   240	                safe_value = value_str.replace("\\", "\\\\").replace('"', '\\"')
   241	                env_file.write(f'{key}="{safe_value}"\n')
   242	
   243	        # Refresh convenience pointers for the active instance
   244	        shutil.copyfile(export_path, target_dir / "current.sh")
   245	        shutil.copyfile(env_path, target_dir / "current.env")
   246	
   247	        relative_export = export_path.relative_to(project_root)
   248	        console.print(
   249	            f"[dim]✓ Instance environment exported to {relative_export} "
   250	            f"(source .dopemux/env/current.sh to mirror in this shell)[/dim]"
   251	        )
   252	    except Exception as exc:  # pragma: no cover - best effort persistence
   253	        console.print(
   254	            f"[yellow]⚠️  Could not persist instance environment: {exc}[/yellow]"
   255	        )
   256	
   257	
   258	def _ensure_role_profile(spec) -> Optional[object]:  # returns DopemuxProfile when available
   259	    """Ensure a profile file exists for the given role spec."""
   260	
   261	    profile_name = getattr(spec, "profile_name", None)
   262	    if not profile_name:
   263	        return None
   264	
   265	    manager = ProfileManager()
   266	    existing = manager.get_profile(profile_name)
   267	    if existing:
   268	        return existing
   269	
   270	    profiles_dir = manager.profiles_dir
   271	    profiles_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
   272	
   273	    required = sorted({"conport", * (spec.required_servers or [])})
   274	    optional = sorted(set(spec.optional_servers or []))
   275	
   276	    attention_cfg = ATTENTION_PROFILE_DEFAULTS.get(spec.attention_state, ATTENTION_PROFILE_DEFAULTS["variable"])
   277	
   278	    profile_data = {
   279	        "name": profile_name,
   280	        "display_name": spec.label,
   281	        "description": spec.description,
   282	        "mcp_servers": {
   283	            "required": required,
   284	            "enabled": optional,
   285	            "disabled": [],
   286	        },
   287	        "adhd_config": {
   288	            "session_duration_minutes": attention_cfg["session_duration_minutes"],
   289	            "energy_preference": attention_cfg["energy_preference"],
   290	            "attention_mode": attention_cfg["attention_mode"],
   291	        },
   292	        "markers": {
   293	            "required_files": [],
   294	            "optional_files": [],
   295	        },
   296	    }
   297	
   298	    profile_path = profiles_dir / f"{profile_name}.yaml"
   299	    with open(profile_path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
   300	        yaml.safe_dump(profile_data, f, sort_keys=False)
   301	
   302	    return manager.get_profile(profile_name)
   303	
   304	
   305	def _load_litellm_models(config_path: Path) -> List[str]:
   306	    """Load model names from a LiteLLM YAML configuration file."""
   307	    try:
   308	        data = yaml.safe_load(config_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
   309	    except FileNotFoundError:
   310	        return []
   311	    except yaml.YAMLError:
   312	        return []
   313	
   314	    models: List[str] = []
   315	    for entry in data.get("model_list", []) if isinstance(data, dict) else []:
   316	        if isinstance(entry, dict):
   317	            name = entry.get("model_name")
   318	            if isinstance(name, str) and name.strip():
   319	                models.append(name.strip())
   320	    return models
   321	
   322	
   323	def _select_model_by_priority(models: Sequence[str], candidates: Sequence[str]) -> Optional[str]:
   324	    """Choose the first model matching any candidate (exact or substring) from a list."""
   325	    if not models:
   326	        return None
   327	
   328	    normalized = [(model, model.lower()) for model in models]
   329	    for candidate in candidates:
   330	        candidate_lower = candidate.lower()
   331	        for original, lower in normalized:
   332	            if lower == candidate_lower:
   333	                return original
   334	        for original, lower in normalized:
   335	            if candidate_lower in lower:
   336	                return original
   337	
   338	    return models[0]
   339	
   340	
   341	def _build_router_overrides(provider_name: str, models: Sequence[str]) -> Dict[str, str]:
   342	    """Generate CCR router overrides based on available LiteLLM models."""
   343	    overrides: Dict[str, str] = {}
   344	
   345	    def _assign(key: str, candidates: Sequence[str]) -> None:
   346	        chosen = _select_model_by_priority(models, candidates)
   347	        if chosen:
   348	            overrides[key] = f"{provider_name},{chosen}"
   349	
   350	    _assign(
   351	        "default",
   352	        (
   353	            "gpt-5",
   354	            "gpt-5-pro",
   355	            "openrouter-openai-gpt-5",
   356	            "grok-4-fast",
   357	            "grok-4",
   358	            "grok-code-fast-1",
   359	            "xai-grok-4-fast",
   360	            "xai-grok-code-fast-1",
   361	        ),
   362	    )
   363	    _assign(
   364	        "background",
   365	        (
   366	            "grok-4-fast",
   367	            "grok-code-fast-1",
   368	            "xai-grok-4-fast",
   369	            "xai-grok-code-fast-1",
   370	            "openrouter-xai-grok-code-fast",
   371	        ),
   372	    )
   373	    _assign(
   374	        "think",
   375	        (
   376	            "gpt-5-codex",
   377	            "openrouter-openai-gpt-5-codex",
   378	            "codex",
   379	        ),
   380	    )
   381	    _assign(
   382	        "webSearch",
   383	        (
   384	            "gpt-5-mini",
   385	            "openrouter-openai-gpt-5-mini",
   386	            "glm-4.6",
   387	            "grok-code-fast-1",
   388	            "xai-grok-code-fast-1",
   389	            "openrouter-google-gemini-2-flash",
   390	        ),
   391	    )
   392	
   393	    return overrides
   394	
   395	
   396	def _suggest_server_start(missing_servers: Iterable[str]) -> None:
   397	    """Suggest commands to start missing MCP services."""
   398	
   399	    services = sorted({ROLE_SERVER_SERVICE_MAP.get(name, name) for name in missing_servers})
   400	    if not services:
   401	        return
   402	    service_arg = ",".join(services)
   403	    console.print(
   404	        f"[yellow]💡 Start required services: dopemux mcp up --services {service_arg}[/yellow]"
   405	    )
   406	    console.print(
   407	        "[dim]   or bring up the full stack: dopemux mcp start-all --verify[/dim]"
   408	    )
   409	
   410	
   411	def _invoke_switch_role_script(role_key: str) -> None:
   412	    if os.getenv("DOPEMUX_SKIP_SWITCH_ROLE_SCRIPT", "0").lower() in {"1", "true", "yes"}:
   413	        return
   414	
   415	    script_path = Path.home() / ".claude" / "switch-role.sh"
   416	    if not script_path.exists():
   417	        return
   418	
   419	    try:
   420	        subprocess.run([str(script_path), role_key], check=True)
   421	        console.print(
   422	            f"[dim]✓ Synced MetaMCP role via {script_path} {role_key}[/dim]"
   423	        )
   424	    except subprocess.CalledProcessError as exc:
   425	        console.print(
   426	            f"[yellow]⚠ switch-role.sh failed (exit {exc.returncode}); continuing[/yellow]"
   427	        )
   428	
   429	
   430	def show_version(ctx, param, value):
   431	    """Show version and exit."""
   432	    if not value or ctx.resilient_parsing:
   433	        return
   434	    click.echo(f"Dopemux {__version__}")
   435	    ctx.exit()

   437	
   438	def _start_minimal_session(
   439	    config_manager: ConfigManager,
   440	    project_path: Path,
   441	    session: Optional[str],
   442	    background: bool,
   443	    debug: bool,
   444	):
   445	    """Fallback start routine for non-real workspaces (test/mocked environments)."""
   446	    context_manager = ContextManager(project_path)
   447	    context = None
   448	    if session:
   449	        context = context_manager.restore_session(session)
   450	    else:
   451	        context = context_manager.restore_latest()
   452	
   453	    launcher = ClaudeLauncher(config_manager)
   454	    try:
   455	        launcher.launch(
   456	            project_path=project_path,
   457	            background=background,
   458	            debug=debug,
   459	            context=context,
   460	        )
   461	    except Exception as e:
   462	        pass
   463	
   464	        logger.error(f"Error: {e}")
   465	    if not background:
   466	        console.logger.info("[green]✨ Claude Code is running (minimal mode)\n[/green]")
   467	
   468	
   469	@click.group()
   470	@click.option(
   471	    "--version", is_flag=True, expose_value=False, is_eager=True, callback=show_version
   472	)
   473	@click.option("--config", "-c", help="Configuration file path")
   474	@click.option("--verbose", "-v", is_flag=True, help="Verbose output")
   475	@click.option("--debug-log", type=click.Path(path_type=Path, dir_okay=False), help="Write debug logs to file")
   476	@click.pass_context
   477	def cli(ctx, config: Optional[str], verbose: bool, debug_log: Optional[Path]):
   478	    """
   479	    🧠 Dopemux - ADHD-optimized development platform
   480	
   481	    Provides context preservation, attention monitoring, and task decomposition
   482	    for enhanced productivity in software development.
   483	    """
   484	    ctx.ensure_object(dict)
   485	    ctx.obj["verbose"] = verbose
   486	    ctx.obj["config_manager"] = ConfigManager(config_path=config)
   487	
   488	    # Optional debug file logging
   489	    log_path_env = os.getenv("DOPEMUX_DEBUG_LOG")
   490	    if not debug_log and log_path_env:
   491	        debug_log = Path(log_path_env)
   492	    if debug_log:
   493	        try:
   494	            log_path = Path(debug_log).expanduser().resolve()
   495	            log_path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
   496	            logging.basicConfig(
   497	                level=logging.DEBUG,
   498	                format="%(asctime)s %(levelname)s %(name)s: %(message)s",
   499	                handlers=[logging.FileHandler(log_path, encoding="utf-8")],
   500	            )
   501	            ctx.obj["debug_log"] = str(log_path)
   502	            os.environ["DOPEMUX_DEBUG_LOG"] = str(log_path)
   503	            logging.debug("dopemux invoked: argv=%s", sys.argv)
   504	        except (OSError, PermissionError) as e:
   505	            logger.error(f"Failed to initialize debug logging file: {e}")
   506	        except Exception:
   507	            logger.error("Unexpected debug logging setup error", exc_info=True)
   508	@cli.command()
   509	@click.argument(
   510	    "directory",
   511	    type=click.Path(path_type=Path, file_okay=False, dir_okay=True),
   512	    required=False,
   513	)
   514	@click.option("--profile", "-p", help="Profile to use (auto-detects if not specified)")
   515	@click.option("--force", "-f", is_flag=True, help="Overwrite existing .dopemux/ directory")
   516	@click.option("--template", "-t", help="Claude configuration template")
   517	@click.pass_context
   518	def init(ctx, directory: Optional[Path], profile: Optional[str], force: bool, template: Optional[str]):
   519	    """
   520	    🚀 Initialize dopemux in current project
   521	
   522	    Creates .dopemux/ directory with profile-based configuration.
   523	    Auto-detects project type and suggests appropriate profile.
   524	
   525	    \b
   526	    Examples:
   527	        dopemux init                    # Auto-detect and prompt
   528	        dopemux init -p python-ml       # Use specific profile
   529	        dopemux init --force            # Reinitialize existing project
   530	        dopemux init ../project-2       # Initialize specific directory
   531	    """
   532	    config_manager = ctx.obj["config_manager"]
   533	
   534	    workspace = (directory or Path.cwd()).expanduser().resolve()
   535	    dopemux_dir = workspace / ".dopemux"
   536	
   537	    workspace_exists = False
   538	    dopemux_exists = False
   539	    try:
   540	        workspace_exists = Path.exists(workspace)
   541	        dopemux_exists = Path.exists(dopemux_dir)
   542	    except TypeError:
   543	        pass
   544	
   545	    if directory and not workspace_exists and not dopemux_exists:
   546	        console.logger.info(f"[red]Directory does not exist: {workspace}[/red]")
   547	        sys.exit(1)
   548	
   549	    if not force and not workspace_exists and dopemux_exists:
   550	        console.logger.info(f"[yellow]⚠️  Project already initialized (.dopemux/ exists)[/yellow]")
   551	        sys.exit(1)
   552	
   553	    try:
   554	        workspace.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
   555	    except (OSError, FileNotFoundError) as e:
   556	        logger.error(f"Workspace directory creation failed: {e}")
   557	    except Exception:
   558	        logger.error("Unexpected error creating workspace directory", exc_info=True)
   559	    success = init_project(workspace, profile, force)
   560	
   561	    if not success:
   562	        console.logger.info("[yellow]Initialization cancelled.[/yellow]")
   563	        sys.exit(1)
   564	
   565	    click.echo("Project Initialized")
   566	
   567	    try:
   568	        configurator = ClaudeConfigurator(config_manager)
   569	        configurator.setup_project_config(workspace, template or "python", force=force)
   570	    except (ClaudeConfigError, ProfileValidationError) as e:
   571	        logger.error(f"Project configuration setup failed: {e}")
   572	    except Exception:
   573	        logger.error("Unexpected configurator error", exc_info=True)
   574	    # Install git hook for automatic ConPort wiring
   575	    try:
   576	        hooks_dir = workspace / ".git" / "hooks"
   577	        if hooks_dir.exists():
   578	            src = Path(__file__).resolve().parents[2] / "scripts" / "git_post_worktree_hook.sh"
   579	            dst = hooks_dir / "post-checkout"
   580	            if not dst.exists():
   581	                import shutil
   582	                shutil.copy2(src, dst)
   583	                dst.chmod(0o755)
   584	                click.echo("🔗 Installed git post-checkout hook for ConPort wiring")
   585	            else:
   586	                click.echo("✅ Git post-checkout hook present")
   587	    except (OSError, shutil.Error) as e:
   588	        logger.error(f"Git hook installation failed: {e}")
   589	    except Exception:
   590	        logger.error("Unexpected git hook install error", exc_info=True)
   591	@cli.command()
   592	@click.option("--instance", "-i", help="Instance id (feature branch name)")
   593	@click.option("--project", "-p", help="Project root (defaults to CWD)")
   594	def wire_conport(instance: Optional[str], project: Optional[str]):
   595	    """
   596	    Wire project-level ConPort MCP config for the current worktree.
   597	
   598	    Writes .claude/claude_config.json with a `conport` stdio server that
   599	    docker-execs into the correct container (mcp-conport[_<instance>]).
   600	    """
   601	    try:
   602	        script = Path(__file__).resolve().parents[2] / "scripts" / "wire_conport_project.py"
   603	        args = [sys.executable, str(script)]
   604	        if instance:
   605	            args.extend(["--instance", instance])
   606	        if project:
   607	            args.extend(["--project", project])
   608	        subprocess.check_call(args)
   609	        click.echo("✅ ConPort wired for this project/worktree")
   610	    except CalledProcessError as e:
   611	        click.echo(f"❌ Failed to wire ConPort: {e}", err=True)
   612	        sys.exit(1)
   613	
   614	@cli.command()
   615	@click.option("--session", "-s", help="Restore specific session ID")
   616	@click.option("--background", "-b", is_flag=True, help="Launch in background")
   617	@click.option("--debug", is_flag=True, help="Launch with debug output")
   618	@click.option(
   619	    "--dangerous",
   620	    is_flag=True,
   621	    help="⚠️  Enable dangerous mode (no approvals, all tools)",
   622	)
   623	@click.option(
   624	    "--dangerously-skip-permissions",
   625	    is_flag=True,
   626	    help="⚠️  Skip all permission checks (same as --dangerous)",
   627	)
   628	@click.option(
   629	    "--no-mcp",
   630	    is_flag=True,
   631	    help="Skip starting MCP servers (not recommended for ADHD experience)",
   632	)
   633	@click.option(
   634	    "--no-recovery",
   635	    is_flag=True,
   636	    help="Skip orphan worktree recovery menu and continue in current location",
   637	)
   638	@click.option(
   639	    "--litellm",
   640	    "use_litellm",
   641	    is_flag=True,
   642	    help="Route Claude Code traffic through LiteLLM proxy",
   643	)
   644	@click.option(
   645	    "--alt-routing",
   646	    "use_alt_routing",
   647	    is_flag=True,
   648	    help="🚀 Automatic alternative provider routing (OpenRouter, XAI, Minimax) - starts LiteLLM automatically",
   649	)
   650	@click.option(
   651	    "--claude-router/--no-claude-router",
   652	    "use_claude_router",
   653	    default=False,  # Changed to False - OAuth-first design (no routing needed)
   654	    help="Start Claude Code Router per instance (requires global `ccr`)",
   655	)
   656	@click.option(
   657	    "--role",
   658	    "-r",
   659	    help="Run Claude with a specific role/persona (e.g. quickfix, act, plan, research, all, orchestrator).",
   660	)
   661	@click.option(
   662	    "--dry-run",
   663	    is_flag=True,
   664	    help="Preview role/profile effects without launching Claude Code.",
   665	)
   666	@click.option(
   667	    "--grok",
   668	    "use_grok",
   669	    is_flag=True,
   670	    help="🎯 Route ALL requests to xAI Grok Code Fast 1 (requires XAI_API_KEY)",
   671	)
   672	@click.option(
   673	    "--codex",
   674	    "use_codex",
   675	    is_flag=True,
   676	    help="🎯 Route ALL requests to OpenAI GPT-5 Codex via OpenRouter (requires OPENROUTER_API_KEY)",
   677	)
   678	@click.option(
   679	    "--altp",
   680	    "use_altp",
   681	    is_flag=True,
   682	    help="🎯 Tier-matched routing: opus→GPT-5.2-Codex, sonnet→GPT-5-Mini, haiku→Grok Code Fast 1",
   683	)
   684	@click.pass_context
   685	def start(
   686	    ctx,
   687	    session: Optional[str],
   688	    background: bool,
   689	    debug: bool,
   690	    dangerous: bool,
   691	    dangerously_skip_permissions: bool,
   692	    no_mcp: bool,
   693	    no_recovery: bool,
   694	    use_litellm: bool,
   695	    use_alt_routing: bool,
   696	    use_claude_router: bool,
   697	    role: Optional[str],
   698	    dry_run: bool,
   699	    use_grok: bool,
   700	    use_codex: bool,
   701	    use_altp: bool,
   702	    **legacy_kwargs,
   703	):
   704	    """
   705	    🚀 Start Claude Code with ADHD-optimized configuration
   706	
   707	    Launches Claude Code with custom MCP servers, restores previous context,
   708	    and activates attention monitoring for the current project.
   709	
   710	    Multi-Instance Support:
   711	        Automatically detects running instances and creates isolated worktrees
   712	        for parallel ADHD-optimized development workflows.
   713	    """
   714	    legacy_value = legacy_kwargs.get("claude_router")
   715	    if legacy_value is not None:
   716	        use_claude_router = legacy_value
   717	
   718	    from .workspace_utils import get_workspace_root
   719	    from .agent_validator import validate_agents_in_workspace
   720	
   721	    # Preflight: Validate and fix agents
   722	    try:
   723	        workspace_root = get_workspace_root()
   724	        if workspace_root:
   725	            validate_agents_in_workspace(workspace_root)
   726	    except Exception as e:
   727	        console.logger.warning(f"Agent validation warning: {e}")
   728	
   729	    # ── Handle --grok / --codex / --altp provider routing ───────────────
   730	    provider_proxy_started = False
   731	    _provider_flags = sum([use_grok, use_codex, use_altp])
   732	    if _provider_flags > 0:
   733	        if _provider_flags > 1:
   734	            raise click.ClickException("Cannot combine --grok, --codex, and --altp. Pick one.")
   735	        if use_alt_routing:
   736	            raise click.ClickException("Cannot combine provider flags with --alt-routing.")
   737	
   738	        if use_grok or use_codex:
   739	            # ── Single-target routing ───────────────────────────────────
   740	            provider = GROK_PROVIDER if use_grok else CODEX_PROVIDER
   741	            flag_name = "--grok" if use_grok else "--codex"
   742	
   743	            if not os.getenv(provider["api_key_env"]):
   744	                raise click.ClickException(
   745	                    f"${provider['api_key_env']} is required for {flag_name}. "
   746	                    f"Set it in your environment or .env file."
   747	                )
   748	
   749	            console.logger.info(
   750	                f"[cyan]🎯 {flag_name}: Routing ALL requests → {provider['label']}[/cyan]"
   751	            )
   752	
   753	            config_data = generate_single_target_config(
   754	                target_name=provider["name"],
   755	                litellm_model=provider["model"],
   756	                api_key_env=provider["api_key_env"],
   757	                max_tokens=provider.get("max_tokens", 131072),
   758	                extra_litellm_params=provider.get("extra_params"),
   759	            )
   760	            _routing_summary = f"Claude Code → LiteLLM → {provider['label']}"
   761	
   762	        else:
   763	            # ── Multi-target tier-matched routing (--altp) ──────────────
   764	            missing_keys = [
   765	                k for k in ALTP_PROVIDER["required_keys"] if not os.getenv(k)
   766	            ]
   767	            if missing_keys:
   768	                raise click.ClickException(
   769	                    f"--altp requires: {', '.join('$' + k for k in missing_keys)}. "
   770	                    f"Set them in your environment or .env file."
   771	                )
   772	
   773	            console.logger.info("[cyan]🎯 --altp: Tier-matched alternative provider routing[/cyan]")
   774	            for t in ALTP_PROVIDER["targets"]:
   775	                tier = t["name"].replace("altp-", "")
   776	                console.logger.info(f"[dim]   {tier:>6s} → {t['label']} ({t['model']})[/dim]")
   777	
   778	            config_data = generate_multi_target_config(ALTP_PROVIDER["targets"])
   779	            
   780	            # Auto-enable Claude Code Router for API translation
   781	            use_claude_router = True
   782	            console.logger.info("[dim]   Enabling Claude Code Router for API translation (responses → completions)[/dim]")
   783	            
   784	            _routing_summary = "Claude Code → CCR → LiteLLM → tier-matched providers"
   785	
   786	        console.logger.info("[blue]🔄 Starting LiteLLM proxy (no DB required)...[/blue]")
   787	        try:
   788	            litellm_port, litellm_master_key = start_simple_proxy(
   789	                project_root=Path.cwd(),
   790	                config_data=config_data,
   791	            )
   792	            provider_proxy_started = True
   793	        except LiteLLMProxyError as exc:
   794	            raise click.ClickException(str(exc))
   795	
   796	        console.logger.info(f"[green]✅ LiteLLM proxy ready on port {litellm_port}[/green]")
   797	
   798	        # Wire Claude Code to use the proxy
   799	        os.environ["DOPEMUX_CLAUDE_VIA_LITELLM"] = "true"
   800	        os.environ["DOPEMUX_DEFAULT_LITELLM"] = "1"
   801	        os.environ["ANTHROPIC_BASE_URL"] = f"http://127.0.0.1:{litellm_port}"
   802	        os.environ["LITELLM_MASTER_KEY"] = litellm_master_key
   803	        os.environ["DOPEMUX_LITELLM_MASTER_KEY"] = litellm_master_key
   804	        os.environ["ANTHROPIC_API_KEY"] = litellm_master_key
   805	
   806	        # Export CCR upstream env vars so Claude Code Router uses the new proxy
   807	        os.environ["CLAUDE_CODE_ROUTER_PROVIDER"] = "litellm"
   808	        os.environ["CLAUDE_CODE_ROUTER_UPSTREAM_URL"] = f"http://127.0.0.1:{litellm_port}/v1/chat/completions"
   809	        os.environ["CLAUDE_CODE_ROUTER_UPSTREAM_KEY_VAR"] = "DOPEMUX_LITELLM_MASTER_KEY"
   810	        
   811	        if use_altp:
   812	            # For --altp, we map to the tier names defined in generate_multi_target_config
   813	            # CCR will expose these exact model names to Claude Code
   814	            os.environ["CLAUDE_CODE_ROUTER_MODELS"] = "altp-opus,altp-sonnet,altp-haiku"
   815	        else:
   816	            os.environ["CLAUDE_CODE_ROUTER_MODELS"] = provider["name"]
   817	
   818	        use_litellm = True
   819	        use_alt_routing = False  # Skip the full alt-routing block below
   820	
   821	        console.logger.info(f"[dim]✓ {_routing_summary} (:{litellm_port})[/dim]")
   822	        console.logger.info("")
   823	
   824	    # Handle --alt-routing flag (automatic LiteLLM setup)
   825	    if use_alt_routing:
   826	        use_litellm = True
   827	        console.logger.info("[cyan]🚀 Alternative routing enabled - starting LiteLLM automatically...[/cyan]")
   828	
   829	        from pathlib import Path as EnvPath
   830	        from dotenv import load_dotenv
   831	
   832	        routing_env = EnvPath.cwd() / ".env.routing"
   833	        if routing_env.exists():
   834	            load_dotenv(routing_env)
   835	            console.logger.info("[dim]✓ Loaded .env.routing[/dim]")
   836	        else:
   837	            console.logger.info("[yellow]⚠️  .env.routing not found - using defaults[/yellow]")
   838	
   839	        instance_dir = Path.cwd() / ".dopemux" / "litellm" / "A"
   840	        instance_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
   841	        litellm_log = instance_dir / "litellm.log"
   842	        master_key_path = instance_dir / "master.key"
   843	        db_url_path = instance_dir / "database.url"
   844	
   845	        remember_raw = os.getenv("DOPEMUX_LITELLM_REMEMBER_DB", "").strip().lower()
   846	        remember_db = remember_raw not in {"0", "false", "no"}
   847	        db_url = (
   848	            os.getenv("DOPEMUX_LITELLM_DB_URL")
   849	            or os.getenv("LITELLM_DATABASE_URL")
   850	            or os.getenv("DATABASE_URL")
   851	        )
   852	        if not db_url and remember_db and db_url_path.exists():
   853	            try:
   854	                loaded = db_url_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8").strip()
   855	                if loaded:
   856	                    db_url = loaded
   857	            except (OSError, UnicodeDecodeError) as e:
   858	                logger.error(f"Failed to read stored LiteLLM DB URL: {e}")
   859	            except Exception:
   860	                logger.error("Unexpected DB URL load error", exc_info=True)
   861	        if not db_url:
   862	            console.logger.info("[red]❌ LiteLLM metrics database is required for alternative routing.[/red]")
   863	            console.logger.info("[yellow]   Set DOPEMUX_LITELLM_DB_URL in .env.routing and ensure the database is reachable.[/yellow]")
   864	            console.logger.info("\n[cyan]Example:[/cyan]")
   865	            console.logger.info("  DOPEMUX_LITELLM_DB_URL=postgresql://user:password@localhost:5432/litellm")  # pragma: allowlist secret
   866	            raise click.ClickException("LiteLLM metrics database not configured.")
   867	
   868	        stored_master_key: Optional[str] = None
   869	        if master_key_path.exists():
   870	            try:
   871	                stored_master_key = master_key_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8").strip()
   872	            except (OSError, UnicodeDecodeError) as e:
   873	                stored_master_key = None
   874	                logger.error(f"Failed to read stored master key: {e}")
   875	            except (OSError, UnicodeDecodeError) as e:
   876	                stored_master_key = None
   877	                logger.error(f"Failed to read stored master key: {e}")
   878	            except Exception:
   879	                stored_master_key = None
   880	                logger.exception("Unexpected master key read error")
   881	        env_master_key_raw = (os.getenv("LITELLM_MASTER_KEY") or "").strip()
   882	        candidate_keys: List[str] = []
   883	        for key in (stored_master_key, env_master_key_raw):
   884	            if key and key not in candidate_keys:
   885	                candidate_keys.append(key)
   886	
   887	        import httpx
   888	
   889	        # Check if port 4000 is available, otherwise use an alternative
   890	        def is_port_available(port: int) -> bool:
   891	            """Check if a port is available for binding."""
   892	            with socket.socket(socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_STREAM) as s:
   893	                try:
   894	                    s.bind(('127.0.0.1', port))
   895	                    return True
   896	                except OSError:
   897	                    return False
   898	
   899	        litellm_port = 4000
   900	        if not is_port_available(litellm_port):
   901	            # Port 4000 is taken, try 4001
   902	            litellm_port = 4001
   903	            if not is_port_available(litellm_port):
   904	                # Port 4001 is also taken, try 4002
   905	                litellm_port = 4002
   906	                if not is_port_available(litellm_port):
   907	                    console.logger.info("[red]❌ Ports 4000-4002 are all in use.[/red]")
   908	                    console.logger.info("[yellow]   Free up a port or stop an existing LiteLLM instance.[/yellow]")
   909	                    raise click.ClickException("No available ports for LiteLLM proxy.")
   910	            console.logger.info(f"[yellow]⚠️  Port 4000 is in use, using port {litellm_port} instead[/yellow]")
   911	
   912	        litellm_master_key = ""
   913	        regenerated_master_key = False
   914	        litellm_running = False
   915	
   916	        # Check if LiteLLM is already running on the determined port
   917	        try:
   918	            resp = httpx.get(
   919	                f"http://localhost:{litellm_port}/health/readiness",
   920	                timeout=2,
   921	            )
   922	            if resp.status_code == 200:
   923	                litellm_running = True
   924	                # Use stored key if available, otherwise use env var
   925	                litellm_master_key = stored_master_key or env_master_key_raw or ""
   926	        except httpx.HTTPError as exc:
   927	            cause = getattr(exc, "__cause__", None)
   928	            if isinstance(cause, OSError) and getattr(cause, "errno", None) == 1:
   929	                console.print(
   930	                    "[yellow]⚠️ LiteLLM health probe blocked by OS (operation not permitted); proceeding without inline check.[/yellow]"
   931	                )
   932	        except Exception as e:
   933	            pass
   934	
   935	            logger.error(f"Error: {e}")
   936	        if not litellm_master_key:
   937	            base_candidate = env_master_key_raw or stored_master_key
   938	            litellm_master_key, regenerated_master_key = ensure_master_key(base_candidate)
   939	            if regenerated_master_key:
   940	                console.logger.info("[yellow]⚠️  Generated LiteLLM master key with sk- prefix for proxy auth[/yellow]")
   941	        else:
   942	            regenerated_master_key = False
   943	
   944	        os.environ["LITELLM_MASTER_KEY"] = litellm_master_key
   945	
   946	        if not stored_master_key or stored_master_key != litellm_master_key:
   947	            try:
   948	                master_key_path.write_text(litellm_master_key, encoding="utf-8")
   949	            except (OSError, IOError) as e:
   950	                logger.error(f"Master key write failed: {e}")
   951	            except Exception:
   952	                logger.error("Unexpected master key write error", exc_info=True)
   953	        config_source: Optional[Path] = None
   954	        if (instance_dir / "litellm.config.yaml").exists():
   955	            config_source = instance_dir / "litellm.config.yaml"
   956	
   957	        if config_source and config_source.exists():
   958	            try:
   959	                config_data = yaml.safe_load(config_source.read_text(encoding="utf-8")) or {}
   960	            except yaml.YAMLError:
   961	                config_data = {}
   962	        else:
   963	            try:
   964	                config_data = yaml.safe_load(DEFAULT_LITELLM_CONFIG) or {}
   965	            except yaml.YAMLError:
   966	                config_data = {}
   967	
   968	        general_settings = config_data.setdefault("general_settings", {})
   969	        general_settings["master_key"] = litellm_master_key
   970	
   971	        if dry_run:
   972	            console.print("[dim]⚡ Dry-run: Skipping LiteLLM DB sync[/dim]")
   973	            db_status_msg = "Dry-run: DB sync skipped"
   974	            db_enabled = True
   975	        else:
   976	            try:
   977	                db_status_msg, db_enabled = sync_litellm_database(instance_dir, db_url)
   978	            except LiteLLMProxyError as exc:
   979	                console.logger.error(f"[red]❌ LiteLLM database setup failed: {exc}[/red]")
   980	                console.logger.info("[yellow]   Fix the database connection (is Postgres running? credentials valid?) and retry.[/yellow]")
   981	                console.logger.info("\n[cyan]Troubleshooting:[/cyan]")
   982	                console.logger.info("  1. Check if PostgreSQL is running: lsof -i :5432 (or your port)")
   983	                console.logger.info("  2. Verify database credentials in .env.routing")
   984	                console.logger.info("  3. Ensure the 'litellm' database exists")
   985	                console.logger.info("  4. Test connection: psql <your_database_url>")
   986	                raise click.ClickException(str(exc))
   987	
   988	        if not db_enabled:
   989	            console.logger.info(f"[red]❌ {db_status_msg}[/red]")
   990	            console.logger.info("[yellow]   LiteLLM metrics must be available. Resolve the database issue and retry.")
   991	            raise click.ClickException("LiteLLM metrics database not ready.")
   992	
   993	        console.logger.info(f"[dim]{db_status_msg}[/dim]")
   994	        general_settings["database_url"] = db_url
   995	
   996	        config_path = instance_dir / "litellm.config.yaml"
   997	        try:
   998	            config_path.write_text(
   999	                yaml.safe_dump(config_data, sort_keys=False, default_flow_style=False),
  1000	                encoding="utf-8",
  1001	            )
  1002	        except Exception as e:
  1003	            pass
  1004	
  1005	            logger.error(f"Error: {e}")
  1006	        if litellm_running:
  1007	            console.logger.info(f"[green]✓ LiteLLM proxy already running on port {litellm_port}[/green]")
  1008	        else:
  1009	            console.logger.info("[blue]🔄 Starting LiteLLM proxy...[/blue]")
  1010	            kill_result = subprocess.run(
  1011	                ["pkill", "-f", "litellm"],
  1012	                stdout=subprocess.DEVNULL,
  1013	                stderr=subprocess.DEVNULL,
  1014	            )
  1015	            if kill_result.returncode not in (0, 1):
  1016	                console.logger.info("[red]❌ Unable to manage existing LiteLLM processes automatically (permission denied).")
  1017	                console.logger.info(f"[yellow]   Stop the existing LiteLLM proxy on port {litellm_port} manually and rerun the command.")
  1018	                raise click.ClickException("LiteLLM proxy still running.")
  1019	
  1020	            time.sleep(1)
  1021	            litellm_log.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
  1022	            with open(litellm_log, "w", encoding="utf-8") as log_file:
  1023	                subprocess.Popen(
  1024	                    ["litellm", "--config", str(config_path), "--port", str(litellm_port), "--host", "0.0.0.0"],
  1025	                    stdout=log_file,
  1026	                    stderr=subprocess.STDOUT,
  1027	                    start_new_session=True,
  1028	                )
  1029	
  1030	            console.logger.info("[dim]⏳ Waiting for LiteLLM to start...[/dim]")
  1031	            ready = False
  1032	            for _ in range(20):
  1033	                try:
  1034	                    resp = httpx.get(
  1035	                        f"http://127.0.0.1:{litellm_port}/health/readiness",
  1036	                        timeout=2,
  1037	                    )
  1038	                    if resp.status_code == 200:
  1039	                        ready = True
  1040	                        break
  1041	                except httpx.HTTPError as exc:
  1042	                    cause = getattr(exc, "__cause__", None)
  1043	                    if isinstance(cause, OSError) and getattr(cause, "errno", None) == 1:
  1044	                        console.print(
  1045	                            "[yellow]⚠️ LiteLLM health probe blocked by OS (operation not permitted); assuming proxy is running.[/yellow]"
  1046	                        )
  1047	                        ready = True
  1048	                        break
  1049	                time.sleep(1)
  1050	
  1051	            if not ready:

  1513	            else:
  1514	                console.print(
  1515	                    f"[green]✅ LiteLLM proxy ready at {litellm_proxy_info.base_url}[/green]"
  1516	                )
  1517	                console.print(
  1518	                    f"[dim]   Config: {litellm_proxy_info.config_path}[/dim]"
  1519	                )
  1520	                console.print(
  1521	                    f"[dim]   Logs: {litellm_proxy_info.log_path}[/dim]"
  1522	                )
  1523	            if litellm_proxy_info.db_status:
  1524	                prisma_log = litellm_proxy_info.log_path.parent / "prisma.log"
  1525	                color = "dim" if litellm_proxy_info.db_enabled else "yellow"
  1526	                console.logger.info(f"[{color}]   {litellm_proxy_info.db_status}[/{color}]")
  1527	                if prisma_log.exists():
  1528	                    console.logger.info(f"[dim]   Prisma log: {prisma_log}[/dim]")
  1529	
  1530	        except LiteLLMProxyError as exc:
  1531	            console.logger.error(f"[red]❌ LiteLLM proxy failed: {exc}[/red]")
  1532	            sys.exit(1)
  1533	
  1534	    router_info = None
  1535	    if use_claude_router and not _direct_provider_routing:
  1536	        provider_url = None
  1537	        provider_models: List[str] = []
  1538	        provider_name = os.environ.get("CLAUDE_CODE_ROUTER_PROVIDER")
  1539	        provider_key_env = os.environ.get(
  1540	            "CLAUDE_CODE_ROUTER_UPSTREAM_KEY_VAR",
  1541	            "DOPEMUX_LITELLM_MASTER_KEY" if litellm_proxy_info else None,
  1542	        )
  1543	        provider_key: Optional[str] = None
  1544	        router_overrides: Dict[str, str] = {}
  1545	
  1546	        if litellm_proxy_info:
  1547	            provider_url = f"{litellm_proxy_info.base_url}/v1/chat/completions"
  1548	            provider_name = provider_name or "litellm"
  1549	            provider_models = _load_litellm_models(litellm_proxy_info.config_path)
  1550	
  1551	            extra_models_env = os.environ.get("CLAUDE_CODE_ROUTER_MODELS", "")
  1552	            if extra_models_env:
  1553	                provider_models.extend(
  1554	                    [
  1555	                        model.strip()
  1556	                        for model in extra_models_env.split(",")
  1557	                        if model.strip()
  1558	                    ]
  1559	                )
  1560	
  1561	            if provider_models:
  1562	                deduped: List[str] = []
  1563	                seen_lower = set()
  1564	                for model in provider_models:
  1565	                    lower = model.lower()
  1566	                    if lower in seen_lower:
  1567	                        continue
  1568	                    seen_lower.add(lower)
  1569	                    deduped.append(model)
  1570	                provider_models = deduped
  1571	
  1572	                router_overrides = _build_router_overrides(provider_name, provider_models)
  1573	        else:
  1574	            provider_url = os.environ.get("CLAUDE_CODE_ROUTER_UPSTREAM_URL")
  1575	            models_env = os.environ.get("CLAUDE_CODE_ROUTER_MODELS", "")
  1576	            provider_models = [m.strip() for m in models_env.split(",") if m.strip()]
  1577	            if not provider_name:
  1578	                provider_name = os.environ.get("CLAUDE_CODE_ROUTER_PROVIDER", "custom")
  1579	            provider_key = os.environ.get("CLAUDE_CODE_ROUTER_UPSTREAM_KEY")
  1580	
  1581	        if not provider_url:
  1582	            console.print(
  1583	                "[red]❌ Claude Code Router upstream URL is not configured.[/red]"
  1584	            )
  1585	            console.print(
  1586	                "[dim]Set CLAUDE_CODE_ROUTER_UPSTREAM_URL or enable --litellm.[/dim]"
  1587	            )
  1588	            sys.exit(1)
  1589	
  1590	        if not provider_models:
  1591	            console.print(
  1592	                "[red]❌ No models configured for Claude Code Router upstream.[/red]"
  1593	            )
  1594	            console.print(
  1595	                "[dim]Set CLAUDE_CODE_ROUTER_MODELS or rely on --litellm defaults.[/dim]"
  1596	            )
  1597	            sys.exit(1)
  1598	
  1599	        # Print DopeBrainzRouterManager class info before usage.
  1600	        console.print("   Enabling Claude Code Router for API translation (responses → completions)")
  1601	
  1602	
  1603	
  1604	        router_manager = DopeBrainzRouterManager(project_path, instance_id, port_base)
  1605	
  1606	        try:
  1607	            router_info = router_manager.ensure_started(
  1608	                provider_url=provider_url,
  1609	                provider_models=provider_models,
  1610	                provider_name=provider_name or "litellm",
  1611	                provider_key=provider_key,
  1612	                provider_key_env_var=provider_key_env,
  1613	                router_overrides=router_overrides if router_overrides else None,
  1614	            )
  1615	        except DopeBrainzRouterError as exc:
  1616	            console.logger.error(f"[red]❌ DopeBrainz Router failed: {exc}[/red]")
  1617	            sys.exit(1)
  1618	
  1619	        router_env = router_manager.build_client_env(router_info)
  1620	        # Use router-provided base URL + API key for Claude Code and MCPs.
  1621	        # Do not restore original ANTHROPIC_API_KEY here — in API-key proxy mode,
  1622	        # the router (or LiteLLM) master key must be used by Claude to avoid login/API errors.
  1623	        os.environ.update(router_env)
  1624	        
  1625	        os.environ.update(router_env)
  1626	        
  1627	        # Re-export env with router variables so Claude Code can pick them up
  1628	        # We explicitly filter here for clarity, though _persist_instance_env_exports has a builtin allowlist.
  1629	        allowlist = _get_routing_allowlist()
  1630	        export_env = {k: os.environ[k] for k in allowlist if k in os.environ}
  1631	        _persist_instance_env_exports(project_path, instance_id, export_env)
  1632	
  1633	        if router_info.already_running:
  1634	            console.print(
  1635	                f"[green]✅ Reusing Claude Code Router at {router_info.base_url}[/green]"
  1636	            )
  1637	        else:
  1638	            console.print(
  1639	                f"[green]✅ Claude Code Router ready at {router_info.base_url}[/green]"
  1640	            )
  1641	            console.logger.info(f"[dim]   Config: {router_info.config_path}[/dim]")
  1642	            console.logger.info(f"[dim]   Logs: {router_info.log_path}[/dim]")
  1643	
  1644	    with Progress(
  1645	        SpinnerColumn(),
  1646	        TextColumn("[progress.description]{task.description}"),
  1647	        console=console,
  1648	    ) as progress:
  1649	        # Restore context
  1650	        task = progress.add_task("Restoring context...", total=None)
  1651	
  1652	        # Use worktree path for context if in multi-instance mode
  1653	        context_path = worktree_path if worktree_path else project_path
  1654	        context_manager = ContextManager(context_path)
  1655	
  1656	        if session:
  1657	            context = context_manager.restore_session(session)
  1658	        else:
  1659	            context = context_manager.restore_latest()
  1660	
  1661	        if context:
  1662	            progress.update(
  1663	                task,
  1664	                description=f"Restored session from {context.get('timestamp', 'unknown')}",
  1665	            )
  1666	            console.print(
  1667	                f"[green]📍 Welcome back! You were working on: {context.get('current_goal', 'Unknown task')}[/green]"
  1668	            )
  1669	        else:
  1670	            progress.update(task, description="Starting fresh session")
  1671	            console.logger.info("[blue]🆕 Starting new session[/blue]")
  1672	
  1673	        # Check if dangerous mode has expired
  1674	        _check_dangerous_mode_expiry()
  1675	
  1676	        # Handle dangerous mode activation
  1677	        is_dangerous_mode = dangerous or dangerously_skip_permissions
  1678	        if is_dangerous_mode:
  1679	            progress.update(task, description="⚠️  Activating dangerous mode...")
  1680	            _activate_dangerous_mode()
  1681	
  1682	        # Auto-configure MCP servers for current worktree (Phase 2: Zero manual steps)
  1683	        skip_auto_config = os.getenv("DOPEMUX_SKIP_MCP_AUTOCONFIG", "0").lower() in {"1", "true", "yes"}
  1684	        if skip_auto_config:
  1685	            progress.update(task, description="⏭️ Skipping MCP auto-configuration (DOPEMUX_SKIP_MCP_AUTOCONFIG)")
  1686	        else:
  1687	            progress.update(task, description="Auto-configuring MCP servers...")
  1688	            from .auto_configurator import WorktreeAutoConfigurator
  1689	
  1690	            auto_config = WorktreeAutoConfigurator()
  1691	            workspace_to_configure = worktree_path or project_path
  1692	            success, message = auto_config.configure_workspace(workspace_to_configure)
  1693	
  1694	            if success:
  1695	                progress.update(task, description="✅ MCP auto-configuration complete")
  1696	            else:
  1697	                progress.update(task, description="⚠️ MCP auto-configuration skipped")
  1698	                console.logger.info(f"[dim]{message}[/dim]")
  1699	
  1700	        # Start MCP servers by default (ADHD-optimized experience)
  1701	        if not no_mcp:
  1702	            # CRITICAL FIX: Pass instance_env_vars so MCP servers get workspace isolation
  1703	            _start_mcp_servers_with_progress(project_path, instance_env=instance_env_vars)
  1704	        else:
  1705	            console.logger.info("[yellow]⚠️  Skipping MCP servers (reduced ADHD experience)[/yellow]")
  1706	
  1707	        # Launch Claude Code
  1708	        progress.update(task, description="Launching Claude Code...")
  1709	        launcher = ClaudeLauncher(config_manager)
  1710	        claude_process = launcher.launch(
  1711	            project_path=project_path,
  1712	            background=background,
  1713	            debug=debug,
  1714	            context=context,
  1715	        )
  1716	
  1717	        # Start attention monitoring
  1718	        progress.update(task, description="Starting attention monitoring...")
  1719	        attention_monitor = AttentionMonitor(project_path)
  1720	        attention_monitor.start_monitoring()
  1721	
  1722	        progress.update(task, description="Ready! 🎯", completed=True)
  1723	
  1724	    # Save instance state to ConPort for crash recovery
  1725	    if instance_id and port_base:
  1726	        from .instance_state import save_instance_state_sync, InstanceState
  1727	        from datetime import datetime, timezone
  1728	
  1729	        # Get current git branch
  1730	        try:
  1731	            git_branch = subprocess.run(
  1732	                ["git", "rev-parse", "--abbrev-ref", "HEAD"],
  1733	                cwd=str(worktree_path or project_path),
  1734	                capture_output=True,
  1735	                text=True,
  1736	                check=True
  1737	            ).stdout.strip()
  1738	        except (subprocess.SubprocessError, OSError) as e:
  1739	            git_branch = "unknown"
  1740	            logger.error(f"Git branch detection failed: {e}")
  1741	        except Exception:
  1742	            git_branch = "unknown"
  1743	            logger.error("Unexpected git branch detection error", exc_info=True)
  1744	        state = InstanceState(
  1745	            instance_id=instance_id,
  1746	            port_base=port_base,
  1747	            worktree_path=str(worktree_path or project_path),
  1748	            git_branch=git_branch,
  1749	            created_at=datetime.now(timezone.utc),
  1750	            last_active=datetime.now(timezone.utc),
  1751	            status="active",
  1752	            last_working_directory=str(worktree_path or project_path),
  1753	            last_focus_context=context.get('current_goal', 'New session') if context else 'New session'
  1754	        )
  1755	
  1756	        save_instance_state_sync(
  1757	            state,
  1758	            workspace_id=str(project_path.resolve()),
  1759	            conport_port=3004  # Always save via instance A's ConPort
  1760	        )
  1761	        console.logger.info("[dim]✅ Instance state saved for crash recovery[/dim]")
  1762	
  1763	    if not background:
  1764	        console.print(
  1765	            "[green]✨ Claude Code is running with ADHD optimizations[/green]"
  1766	        )
  1767	        console.logger.info("Press Ctrl+C to stop monitoring and save context")
  1768	
  1769	        try:
  1770	            claude_process.wait()
  1771	        except KeyboardInterrupt:
  1772	            console.logger.info("\n[yellow]⏸️ Saving context and stopping...[/yellow]")
  1773	
  1774	            # Mark instance as stopped in ConPort
  1775	            if instance_id:
  1776	                from .instance_state import load_instance_state_sync, save_instance_state_sync
  1777	                from datetime import datetime, timezone
  1778	
  1779	                workspace_id = str(project_path.resolve())
  1780	                state = load_instance_state_sync(instance_id, workspace_id, conport_port=3004)
  1781	                if state:
  1782	                    state.status = 'stopped'
  1783	                    state.last_active = datetime.now(timezone.utc)
  1784	                    save_instance_state_sync(state, workspace_id, conport_port=3004)
  1785	                    console.logger.info("[dim]✅ Instance marked as stopped[/dim]")
  1786	
  1787	            ctx.invoke(save)
  1788	            attention_monitor.stop_monitoring()
  1789

  1791	@cli.command()
  1792	@click.option("--message", "-m", help="Save message/note")
  1793	@click.option("--force", "-f", is_flag=True, help="Force save even if no changes")
  1794	@click.pass_context
  1795	def save(ctx, message: Optional[str], force: bool):
  1796	    """
  1797	    💾 Save current development context
  1798	
  1799	    Captures open files, cursor positions, mental model, and recent decisions
  1800	    for seamless restoration later.
  1801	    """
  1802	    project_path = Path.cwd()
  1803	
  1804	    if not (project_path / ".dopemux").exists():
  1805	        console.logger.info("[red]No Dopemux project found in current directory[/red]")
  1806	        sys.exit(1)
  1807	
  1808	    with Progress(
  1809	        SpinnerColumn(),
  1810	        TextColumn("[progress.description]{task.description}"),
  1811	        console=console,
  1812	    ) as progress:
  1813	        task = progress.add_task("Saving context...", total=None)
  1814	
  1815	        context_manager = ContextManager(project_path)
  1816	        session_id = context_manager.save_context(message=message, force=force)
  1817	
  1818	        progress.update(task, description="Context saved!", completed=True)
  1819	
  1820	    console.logger.info(f"[green]✅ Context saved (session: {session_id[:8]})[/green]")
  1821	    if message:
  1822	        console.logger.info(f"[dim]Note: {message}[/dim]")
  1823	
  1824	
  1825	@cli.command()
  1826	@click.option("--session", "-s", help="Specific session ID to restore")
  1827	@click.option(
  1828	    "--list", "-l", "list_sessions", is_flag=True, help="List available sessions"
  1829	)
  1830	@click.pass_context
  1831	def restore(ctx, session: Optional[str], list_sessions: bool):
  1832	    """
  1833	    🔄 Restore previous development context
  1834	
  1835	    Restores files, cursor positions, and mental model from a previous session.
  1836	    """
  1837	    project_path = Path.cwd()
  1838	
  1839	    if not (project_path / ".dopemux").exists():
  1840	        console.logger.info("[red]No Dopemux project found in current directory[/red]")
  1841	        sys.exit(1)
  1842	
  1843	    context_manager = ContextManager(project_path)
  1844	
  1845	    if list_sessions:
  1846	        sessions = context_manager.list_sessions()
  1847	        if not sessions:
  1848	            console.logger.info("[yellow]No saved sessions found[/yellow]")
  1849	            return
  1850	
  1851	        table = Table(title="Available Sessions")
  1852	        table.add_column("ID", style="cyan")
  1853	        table.add_column("Timestamp", style="green")
  1854	        table.add_column("Goal", style="yellow")
  1855	        table.add_column("Files", justify="right", style="blue")
  1856	
  1857	        for s in sessions:
  1858	            table.add_row(
  1859	                s["id"],
  1860	                s["timestamp"],
  1861	                s.get("current_goal", "No goal set")[:50],
  1862	                str(len(s.get("open_files", []))),
  1863	            )
  1864	
  1865	        console.logger.info(table)
  1866	        for s in sessions:
  1867	            console.logger.info(f"- {s['id']} :: {s.get('current_goal', 'No goal set')}")
  1868	        return
  1869	
  1870	    with Progress(
  1871	        SpinnerColumn(),
  1872	        TextColumn("[progress.description]{task.description}"),
  1873	        console=console,
  1874	    ) as progress:
  1875	        task = progress.add_task("Restoring context...", total=None)
  1876	
  1877	        if session:
  1878	            context = context_manager.restore_session(session)
  1879	        else:
  1880	            context = context_manager.restore_latest()
  1881	
  1882	        progress.update(task, description="Context restored!", completed=True)
  1883	
  1884	    if context:
  1885	        console.print(
  1886	            f"[green]✅ Restored session from {context.get('timestamp', 'unknown')}[/green]"
  1887	        )
  1888	        console.print(
  1889	            f"[blue]🎯 Goal: {context.get('current_goal', 'No goal set')}[/blue]"
  1890	        )
  1891	        console.print(
  1892	            f"[yellow]📁 Files: {len(context.get('open_files', []))} files restored[/yellow]"
  1893	        )
  1894	    else:
  1895	        console.logger.info("[red]❌ No context found to restore[/red]")
  1896	
  1897	
  1898	@cli.group()
  1899	def instances():
  1900	    """
  1901	    🏗️  Manage multiple Dopemux instances and worktrees
  1902	
  1903	    Commands for managing parallel ADHD-optimized development workflows
  1904	    with isolated worktrees and shared database.
  1905	    """
  1906	    pass
  1907	
  1908	
  1909	@instances.command("list")
  1910	@click.pass_context
  1911	def instances_list(ctx):
  1912	    """
  1913	    📋 List all running instances and worktrees
  1914	
  1915	    Shows currently active instances with their ports, branches, and paths.
  1916	    Automatically detects and reports orphaned instances (crashed).
  1917	    """
  1918	    project_path = Path.cwd()
  1919	    workspace_id = str(project_path.resolve())
  1920	
  1921	    instance_manager = InstanceManager(project_path)
  1922	    running_instances = detect_instances_sync(project_path)
  1923	
  1924	    # Detect orphaned instances (automatic crash detection)
  1925	    orphaned_instances = detect_orphaned_instances_sync(
  1926	        project_path,
  1927	        workspace_id,
  1928	        conport_port=3004  # Always query via instance A's ConPort
  1929	    )
  1930	
  1931	    # Show running instances
  1932	    if running_instances:
  1933	        console.logger.info(f"\n[green]✅ Found {len(running_instances)} running instance(s)[/green]\n")
  1934	
  1935	        table = Table(title="Running Instances")
  1936	        table.add_column("Instance", style="cyan", no_wrap=True)
  1937	        table.add_column("Port", style="magenta", no_wrap=True)
  1938	        table.add_column("Branch", style="green")
  1939	        table.add_column("Current Worktree", style="blue")
  1940	        table.add_column("Status", style="green")
  1941	
  1942	        for inst in running_instances:
  1943	            status = "✅ Healthy" if inst.is_healthy else "⚠️  Unknown"
  1944	            table.add_row(
  1945	                inst.instance_id,
  1946	                str(inst.port_base),
  1947	                inst.git_branch or "unknown",
  1948	                str(inst.worktree_path) if inst.worktree_path else "main",
  1949	                status
  1950	            )
  1951	
  1952	        console.logger.info(table)
  1953	    else:
  1954	        console.logger.info("[yellow]No running instances found[/yellow]")
  1955	
  1956	    # Show orphaned instances (automatic crash detection)
  1957	    if orphaned_instances:
  1958	        console.logger.info(f"\n[red]⚠️  Found {len(orphaned_instances)} orphaned instance(s)[/red]")
  1959	        console.logger.info("[dim]Orphaned instances have crashed but their worktrees still exist[/dim]\n")
  1960	
  1961	        orphan_table = Table(title="Orphaned Instances (Crashed)")
  1962	        orphan_table.add_column("Instance", style="red", no_wrap=True)
  1963	        orphan_table.add_column("Branch", style="yellow")
  1964	        orphan_table.add_column("Last Active", style="dim")
  1965	        orphan_table.add_column("Last Focus", style="cyan")
  1966	        orphan_table.add_column("Action", style="green")
  1967	
  1968	        from datetime import datetime
  1969	        for orphan in orphaned_instances:
  1970	            # Calculate time since last active
  1971	            if isinstance(orphan['last_active'], str):
  1972	                last_active = datetime.fromisoformat(orphan['last_active'])
  1973	            else:
  1974	                last_active = orphan['last_active']
  1975	
  1976	            time_diff = datetime.now() - last_active
  1977	            if time_diff.days > 0:
  1978	                time_ago = f"{time_diff.days}d ago"
  1979	            elif time_diff.seconds > 3600:
  1980	                time_ago = f"{time_diff.seconds // 3600}h ago"
  1981	            else:
  1982	                time_ago = f"{time_diff.seconds // 60}m ago"
  1983	
  1984	            orphan_table.add_row(
  1985	                orphan['instance_id'],
  1986	                orphan['git_branch'],
  1987	                time_ago,
  1988	                orphan.get('last_focus_context', 'N/A')[:40] or "N/A",
  1989	                f"dopemux instances resume {orphan['instance_id']}"
  1990	            )
  1991	
  1992	        console.logger.info(orphan_table)
  1993	        console.logger.info("\n[dim]💡 Tip: Use 'dopemux instances resume <id>' to restart an orphaned instance[/dim]")
  1994	        console.logger.info("[dim]     Or use 'dopemux instances cleanup <id>' to remove the worktree[/dim]")
  1995	
  1996	    # Show git worktrees
  1997	    console.logger.info("\n[bold]Git Worktrees:[/bold]")
  1998	    worktrees = instance_manager.list_worktrees()
  1999	
  2000	    if worktrees:
  2001	        worktree_table = Table()
  2002	        worktree_table.add_column("ID", style="cyan")
  2003	        worktree_table.add_column("Path", style="dim")
  2004	        worktree_table.add_column("Branch", style="green")
  2005	
  2006	        for wt_id, wt_path, wt_branch in worktrees:
  2007	            worktree_table.add_row(wt_id, str(wt_path), wt_branch)
  2008	
  2009	        console.logger.info(worktree_table)
  2010	    else:
  2011	        console.logger.info("[dim]No worktrees found[/dim]")
  2012	
  2013	
  2014	@instances.command("resume")
  2015	@click.argument("instance_id")
  2016	@click.option("--restore-context", "-r", is_flag=True, help="Restore working directory and focus context")
  2017	@click.pass_context
  2018	def instances_resume(ctx, instance_id: str, restore_context: bool):
  2019	    """
  2020	    🔄 Resume an orphaned instance (one-click crash recovery)
  2021	
  2022	    Restarts services for an orphaned instance, optionally restoring
  2023	    the last working directory and focus context.
  2024	
  2025	    \b
  2026	    Examples:
  2027	        dopemux instances resume B              # Restart instance B
  2028	        dopemux instances resume B --restore-context  # Restart and restore context
  2029	
  2030	    \b
  2031	    ADHD Benefit:
  2032	        Zero-friction recovery from crashes. Resume exactly where you left off
  2033	        with preserved mental model and context continuity.
  2034	    """
  2035	    project_path = Path.cwd()
  2036	    workspace_id = str(project_path.resolve())
  2037	
  2038	    # Load orphaned instance state
  2039	    from .instance_state import load_instance_state_sync
  2040	
  2041	    state = load_instance_state_sync(instance_id, workspace_id, conport_port=3004)
  2042	
  2043	    if not state:
  2044	        console.logger.info(f"[red]❌ No saved state found for instance {instance_id}[/red]")
  2045	        console.logger.info("[dim]Tip: Use 'dopemux instances list' to see available instances[/dim]")
  2046	        sys.exit(1)
  2047	
  2048	    if state.status != 'orphaned':
  2049	        console.logger.info(f"[yellow]⚠️  Instance {instance_id} is not orphaned (status: {state.status})[/yellow]")
  2050	        if state.status == 'active':
  2051	            console.logger.info(f"[dim]Instance is already running on port {state.port_base}[/dim]")
  2052	        sys.exit(1)
  2053	
  2054	    # Check if worktree still exists
  2055	    worktree_path = Path(state.worktree_path)
  2056	    if not worktree_path.exists():
  2057	        console.logger.info(f"[red]❌ Worktree not found at {worktree_path}[/red]")
  2058	        console.logger.info("[dim]The worktree may have been deleted. Use 'dopemux instances cleanup' to remove state[/dim]")
  2059	        sys.exit(1)
  2060	
  2061	    console.logger.info(f"\n[cyan]🔄 Resuming instance {instance_id}...[/cyan]")
  2062	    console.logger.info(f"   Branch: {state.git_branch}")
  2063	    console.logger.info(f"   Worktree: {worktree_path}")
  2064	    console.logger.info(f"   Port base: {state.port_base}")
  2065	
  2066	    if state.last_focus_context:
  2067	        console.logger.info(f"   Last focus: [dim]{state.last_focus_context}[/dim]")
  2068	
  2069	    # Show context restoration info
  2070	    if restore_context and state.last_working_directory:
  2071	        console.logger.info(f"\n[green]✨ Context restoration enabled:[/green]")
  2072	        console.logger.info(f"   Working directory: {state.last_working_directory}")
  2073	        if state.last_focus_context:
  2074	            console.logger.info(f"   Focus context: {state.last_focus_context}")
  2075	
  2076	    # Start instance
  2077	    console.logger.info(f"\n[yellow]💡 Starting instance {instance_id} on port {state.port_base}...[/yellow]")
  2078	
  2079	    # Set environment variables for this process
  2080	    env = os.environ.copy()
  2081	    env.update({
  2082	        "DOPEMUX_INSTANCE_ID": instance_id,
  2083	        "DOPEMUX_WORKSPACE_ID": workspace_id,
  2084	        "DOPEMUX_PORT_BASE": str(state.port_base),
  2085	        "TASK_MASTER_PORT": str(state.port_base + 5),
  2086	        "SERENA_PORT": str(state.port_base + 6),
  2087	        "CONPORT_PORT": str(state.port_base + 7),
  2088	        "INTEGRATION_BRIDGE_PORT": str(state.port_base + 16),
  2089	    })
  2090	
  2091	    # Change to worktree directory if restoring context
  2092	    original_cwd = os.getcwd()
  2093	    if restore_context and state.last_working_directory:
  2094	        try:
  2095	            os.chdir(state.last_working_directory)
  2096	            console.logger.info(f"[green]✅ Changed to working directory: {state.last_working_directory}[/green]")
  2097	        except Exception as e:
  2098	            console.logger.info(f"[yellow]⚠️  Could not change to working directory: {e}[/yellow]")
  2099	            console.logger.info("[dim]Staying in current directory[/dim]")
  2100	
  2101	    console.logger.info(f"\n[green]✅ Instance {instance_id} resumed successfully![/green]")
  2102	    console.logger.info(f"[dim]Services are starting on port {state.port_base}...[/dim]")
  2103	
  2104	    if restore_context:
  2105	        console.logger.info("\n[cyan]📍 Context Restored:[/cyan]")
  2106	        console.logger.info(f"   You were working on: {state.last_focus_context or 'N/A'}")
  2107	        console.logger.info(f"   In directory: {os.getcwd()}")
  2108	
  2109	    console.logger.info(f"\n[dim]💡 Tip: Instance will be marked as 'active' when dopemux start completes[/dim]")
  2110	    console.logger.info(f"[dim]     Run: cd {worktree_path} && dopemux start[/dim]")
  2111	
  2112	    # Mark as active (optimistic - actual start command will confirm)
  2113	    from .instance_state import save_instance_state_sync
  2114	    state.status = 'active'
  2115	    from datetime import datetime
  2116	    state.last_active = datetime.now()
  2117	    save_instance_state_sync(state, workspace_id, conport_port=3004)
  2118

  2120	@instances.command("cleanup")
  2121	@click.argument("instance_id", required=False)
  2122	@click.option("--all", "-a", is_flag=True, help="Clean up all stopped instances")
  2123	@click.option("--force", "-f", is_flag=True, help="Force cleanup without confirmation")
  2124	@click.pass_context
  2125	def instances_cleanup(ctx, instance_id: Optional[str], all: bool, force: bool):
  2126	    """
  2127	    🧹 Clean up stopped instance worktrees
  2128	
  2129	    Removes git worktrees for stopped instances to free up disk space.
  2130	
  2131	    \b
  2132	    Examples:
  2133	        dopemux instances cleanup B          # Remove instance B worktree
  2134	        dopemux instances cleanup --all      # Remove all stopped instances
  2135	    """
  2136	    project_path = Path.cwd()
  2137	    instance_manager = InstanceManager(project_path)
  2138	
  2139	    if not instance_id and not all:
  2140	        console.logger.info("[red]❌ Specify instance ID or use --all flag[/red]")
  2141	        console.logger.info("[dim]Usage: dopemux instances cleanup <ID> or --all[/dim]")
  2142	        sys.exit(1)
  2143	
  2144	    if all:
  2145	        # Get all worktrees
  2146	        worktrees = instance_manager.list_worktrees()
  2147	        running_instances = detect_instances_sync(project_path)
  2148	        running_ids = {inst.instance_id for inst in running_instances}
  2149	
  2150	        # Find stopped instances
  2151	        stopped_instances = [
  2152	            (wt_id, wt_path) for wt_id, wt_path, _ in worktrees
  2153	            if wt_id not in running_ids and wt_id != 'A'
  2154	        ]
  2155	
  2156	        if not stopped_instances:
  2157	            console.logger.info("[green]✅ No stopped instances to clean up[/green]")
  2158	            return
  2159	
  2160	        console.logger.info(f"\n[yellow]⚠️  Found {len(stopped_instances)} stopped instance(s) to clean:[/yellow]")
  2161	        for wt_id, wt_path in stopped_instances:
  2162	            console.logger.info(f"  • Instance {wt_id}: {wt_path}")
  2163	
  2164	        if not force and not click.confirm("\nProceed with cleanup?"):
  2165	            console.logger.info("[yellow]Cleanup cancelled[/yellow]")
  2166	            return
  2167	
  2168	        # Clean up each stopped instance
  2169	        from .instance_state import cleanup_instance_state_sync
  2170	        workspace_id = str(project_path.resolve())
  2171	
  2172	        for wt_id, _ in stopped_instances:
  2173	            if instance_manager.cleanup_worktree(wt_id):
  2174	                console.logger.info(f"[green]✅ Removed worktree for instance {wt_id}[/green]")
  2175	
  2176	                # Also remove instance state from ConPort
  2177	                if cleanup_instance_state_sync(wt_id, workspace_id, conport_port=3004):
  2178	                    console.logger.info(f"[dim]✅ Removed instance state for {wt_id}[/dim]")
  2179	            else:
  2180	                console.logger.error(f"[red]❌ Failed to remove worktree for instance {wt_id}[/red]")
  2181	
  2182	    else:
  2183	        # Clean up specific instance
  2184	        if instance_id == 'A':
  2185	            console.logger.info("[red]❌ Cannot clean up main worktree (instance A)[/red]")
  2186	            sys.exit(1)
  2187	
  2188	        # Check if instance is running
  2189	        running_instances = detect_instances_sync(project_path)
  2190	        if any(inst.instance_id == instance_id for inst in running_instances):
  2191	            console.logger.info(f"[red]❌ Instance {instance_id} is still running[/red]")
  2192	            console.logger.info("[dim]Stop the instance before cleaning up its worktree[/dim]")
  2193	            sys.exit(1)
  2194	
  2195	        worktree_path = instance_manager._get_worktree_path(instance_id)
  2196	        if not worktree_path or not worktree_path.exists():
  2197	            console.logger.info(f"[yellow]⚠️  No worktree found for instance {instance_id}[/yellow]")
  2198	            return
  2199	
  2200	        console.logger.info(f"\n[yellow]⚠️  Removing worktree for instance {instance_id}[/yellow]")
  2201	        console.logger.info(f"[dim]Path: {worktree_path}[/dim]")
  2202	
  2203	        if not force and not click.confirm("Proceed?"):
  2204	            console.logger.info("[yellow]Cleanup cancelled[/yellow]")
  2205	            return
  2206	
  2207	        if instance_manager.cleanup_worktree(instance_id):
  2208	            console.logger.info(f"[green]✅ Removed worktree for instance {instance_id}[/green]")
  2209	
  2210	            # Also remove instance state from ConPort
  2211	            from .instance_state import cleanup_instance_state_sync
  2212	            workspace_id = str(project_path.resolve())
  2213	
  2214	            if cleanup_instance_state_sync(instance_id, workspace_id, conport_port=3004):
  2215	                console.logger.info(f"[dim]✅ Removed instance state from ConPort[/dim]")
  2216	        else:
  2217	            console.logger.error(f"[red]❌ Failed to remove worktree for instance {instance_id}[/red]")
  2218
