  2220	@cli.command()
  2221	@click.option("--attention", "-a", is_flag=True, help="Show attention metrics")
  2222	@click.option("--context", "-c", is_flag=True, help="Show context information")
  2223	@click.option("--tasks", "-t", is_flag=True, help="Show task progress")
  2224	@click.option("--mobile", "-m", is_flag=True, help="Show Happy mobile status")
  2225	@click.pass_context
  2226	def status(ctx, attention: bool, context: bool, tasks: bool, mobile: bool):
  2227	    """
  2228	    📊 Show current session status and metrics
  2229	
  2230	    Displays attention state, context information, task progress, and
  2231	    ADHD accommodation effectiveness.
  2232	    """
  2233	    project_path = Path.cwd()
  2234	
  2235	    if not (project_path / ".dopemux").exists():
  2236	        console.logger.info("[red]No Dopemux project found in current directory[/red]")
  2237	        sys.exit(1)
  2238	
  2239	    # Show all by default if no specific flags
  2240	    if not any([attention, context, tasks, mobile]):
  2241	        attention = context = tasks = mobile = True
  2242	
  2243	    if attention:
  2244	        monitor = AttentionMonitor(project_path)
  2245	        metrics = monitor.get_current_metrics()
  2246	
  2247	        table = Table(title="🧠 Attention Metrics")
  2248	        table.add_column("Metric", style="cyan")
  2249	        table.add_column("Value", style="green")
  2250	        table.add_column("Status", style="yellow")
  2251	
  2252	        table.add_row(
  2253	            "Current State",
  2254	            metrics.get("attention_state", "unknown"),
  2255	            _get_attention_emoji(metrics.get("attention_state")),
  2256	        )
  2257	        table.add_row(
  2258	            "Session Duration", f"{metrics.get('session_duration', 0):.1f} min", "⏱️"
  2259	        )
  2260	        table.add_row("Focus Score", f"{metrics.get('focus_score', 0):.1%}", "🎯")
  2261	        table.add_row("Context Switches", str(metrics.get("context_switches", 0)), "🔄")
  2262	
  2263	        console.logger.info(table)
  2264	
  2265	    if context:
  2266	        context_manager = ContextManager(project_path)
  2267	        current_context = context_manager.get_current_context()
  2268	
  2269	        table = Table(title="📍 Context Information")
  2270	        table.add_column("Item", style="cyan")
  2271	        table.add_column("Value", style="green")
  2272	
  2273	        table.add_row("Current Goal", current_context.get("current_goal", "Not set"))
  2274	        table.add_row("Open Files", str(len(current_context.get("open_files", []))))
  2275	        table.add_row("Last Save", current_context.get("last_save", "Never"))
  2276	        table.add_row("Git Branch", current_context.get("git_branch", "unknown"))
  2277	
  2278	        console.logger.info(table)
  2279	
  2280	    if tasks:
  2281	        decomposer = TaskDecomposer(project_path)
  2282	        progress_info = decomposer.get_progress()
  2283	
  2284	        if progress_info:
  2285	            table = Table(title="📋 Task Progress")
  2286	            table.add_column("Task", style="cyan")
  2287	            table.add_column("Status", style="green")
  2288	            table.add_column("Progress", style="yellow")
  2289	
  2290	            for task in progress_info.get("tasks", []):
  2291	                status_emoji = (
  2292	                    "✅" if task["completed"] else "🔄" if task["in_progress"] else "⏳"
  2293	                )
  2294	                table.add_row(
  2295	                    task["name"], status_emoji, f"{task.get('progress', 0):.0%}"
  2296	                )
  2297	
  2298	            console.logger.info(table)
  2299	        else:
  2300	            console.logger.info("[yellow]No active tasks found[/yellow]")
  2301	
  2302	    if mobile:
  2303	        from .mobile.runtime import check_cli_health, list_mobile_panes
  2304	        from .mobile.tmux_utils import TmuxError
  2305	
  2306	        cfg_manager = ctx.obj.get("config_manager") if ctx.obj else ConfigManager()
  2307	        mobile_cfg = cfg_manager.get_mobile_config()
  2308	
  2309	        happy_ok = check_cli_health("happy")
  2310	        claude_ok = check_cli_health("claude")
  2311	
  2312	        try:
  2313	            panes = list_mobile_panes()
  2314	            tmux_error = None
  2315	        except TmuxError as exc:
  2316	            panes = []
  2317	            tmux_error = str(exc)
  2318	
  2319	            logger.error(f"Error: {e}")
  2320	        mobile_table = Table(title="📱 Mobile Status")
  2321	        mobile_table.add_column("Check", style="cyan")
  2322	        mobile_table.add_column("Status", style="green")
  2323	
  2324	        mobile_table.add_row("Mobile Enabled", "✅ Enabled" if mobile_cfg.enabled else "❌ Disabled")
  2325	        mobile_table.add_row("Happy CLI", "✅ Healthy" if happy_ok else "❌ Unavailable")
  2326	        mobile_table.add_row("Claude CLI", "✅ Healthy" if claude_ok else "⚠️ Check setup")
  2327	
  2328	        if tmux_error:
  2329	            mobile_table.add_row("tmux", f"⚠️ {tmux_error}")
  2330	        else:
  2331	            mobile_table.add_row("Active Sessions", str(len(panes)))
  2332	
  2333	        console.logger.info(mobile_table)
  2334	
  2335	        if not tmux_error and panes:
  2336	            sessions_table = Table(title="📱 Active Happy Sessions")
  2337	            sessions_table.add_column("Pane", style="cyan")
  2338	            sessions_table.add_column("Window", style="green")
  2339	            sessions_table.add_column("Path", style="dim")
  2340	
  2341	            for pane in panes:
  2342	                sessions_table.add_row(
  2343	                    pane.title or "(unnamed)",
  2344	                    pane.window or "?",
  2345	                    pane.path or "",
  2346	                )
  2347	
  2348	            console.logger.info(sessions_table)

  2351	@cli.command("run-tests")
  2352	@click.argument("command", nargs=-1)
  2353	@click.option("--cwd", type=click.Path(file_okay=False, dir_okay=True), help="Working directory for the test command")
  2354	@click.option("--label", default="Test run", show_default=True, help="Notification label for this test run")
  2355	@click.pass_context
  2356	def run_tests(ctx, command: Sequence[str], cwd: Optional[str], label: str):
  2357	    """Run automated tests and send mobile notifications."""
  2358	
  2359	    args = list(command) if command else ["pytest"]
  2360	    task_label = label or "Test run"
  2361	
  2362	    with mobile_task_notification(
  2363	        ctx,
  2364	        task_label,
  2365	        success_message=f"✅ {task_label} complete",
  2366	        failure_message=f"❌ {task_label} failed",
  2367	    ):
  2368	        result = subprocess.run(args, cwd=cwd, check=False)
  2369	        cmd_display = " ".join(args)
  2370	
  2371	        if result.returncode == 0:
  2372	            console.logger.info(f"[green]✅ Tests passed ({cmd_display})[/green]")
  2373	        else:
  2374	            console.logger.error(f"[red]❌ Tests failed ({cmd_display})[/red]")
  2375	            sys.exit(result.returncode)
  2376	
  2377	    cfg_manager = ctx.obj.get("config_manager") if ctx.obj else ConfigManager()
  2378	    update_tmux_mobile_indicator(cfg_manager)
  2379

  2400	        cmd_display = " ".join(args)

  2412	@cli.command()
  2413	@click.argument("description", required=False)
  2414	@click.option("--duration", "-d", type=int, default=25, help="Task duration in minutes")
  2415	@click.option(
  2416	    "--priority", "-p", type=click.Choice(["low", "medium", "high"]), default="medium"
  2417	)
  2418	@click.option("--list", "-l", "list_tasks", is_flag=True, help="List current tasks")
  2419	@click.pass_context
  2420	def task(
  2421	    ctx, description: Optional[str], duration: int, priority: str, list_tasks: bool
  2422	):
  2423	    """
  2424	    📋 DEPRECATED - Use SuperClaude /dx: commands instead
  2425	
  2426	    This command has been replaced by:
  2427	    - /dx:implement - Start ADHD-optimized implementation session
  2428	    - /dx:session start/end/break - Session management
  2429	    - /dx:load - Load tasks from ConPort
  2430	    - /dx:stats - View ADHD metrics and progress
  2431	
  2432	    See: docs/90-adr/ADR-XXXX-path-c-migration.md
  2433	    """
  2434	    console.logger.info("[yellow]" + "="*60 + "[/yellow]")
  2435	    console.logger.info("[red]⚠️  DEPRECATED COMMAND[/red]")
  2436	    console.logger.info("[yellow]" + "="*60 + "[/yellow]")
  2437	    console.logger.info()
  2438	    console.logger.info("The 'dopemux task' command has been replaced by SuperClaude /dx: commands:")
  2439	    console.logger.info()
  2440	    console.logger.info("  [cyan]/dx:implement[/cyan] - Start ADHD-optimized implementation session")
  2441	    console.logger.info("  [cyan]/dx:session start[/cyan] - Begin work session")
  2442	    console.logger.info("  [cyan]/dx:load[/cyan] - Load tasks from ConPort")
  2443	    console.logger.info("  [cyan]/dx:stats[/cyan] - View ADHD metrics and progress")
  2444	    console.logger.info()
  2445	    console.logger.info("Migration completed: October 2025")
  2446	    console.logger.info("See: [blue]docs/90-adr/ADR-XXXX-path-c-migration.md[/blue]")
  2447	    console.logger.info()
  2448	    console.logger.info("[yellow]" + "="*60 + "[/yellow]")
  2449	
  2450	    project_path = Path.cwd()
  2451	    if not (project_path / ".dopemux").exists():
  2452	        console.logger.info("[red]No Dopemux project found in current directory[/red]")
  2453	        sys.exit(1)
  2454	
  2455	    decomposer = TaskDecomposer(project_path)
  2456	
  2457	    if list_tasks:
  2458	        tasks = decomposer.list_tasks()
  2459	        if not tasks:
  2460	            console.logger.info("[yellow]No tasks found[/yellow]")
  2461	            return
  2462	
  2463	        table = Table(title="Current Tasks")
  2464	        table.add_column("Task", style="cyan")
  2465	        table.add_column("Priority", style="yellow")
  2466	        table.add_column("Duration", style="green")
  2467	        table.add_column("Status", style="blue")
  2468	
  2469	        for task in tasks:
  2470	            status = (
  2471	                "✅ Complete"
  2472	                if task.get("status") == "completed"
  2473	                else (
  2474	                    "🔄 In Progress"
  2475	                    if task.get("status") == "in_progress"
  2476	                    else "⏳ Pending"
  2477	                )
  2478	            )
  2479	            table.add_row(
  2480	                task["description"],
  2481	                task["priority"],
  2482	                f"{task['estimated_duration']}m",
  2483	                status,
  2484	            )
  2485	
  2486	        console.logger.info(table)
  2487	        return
  2488	
  2489	    # Check if description is provided for adding new task
  2490	    if not description:
  2491	        console.logger.info("[red]Description required when not listing tasks[/red]")
  2492	        console.logger.info("Use 'dopemux task --list' to list current tasks")
  2493	        sys.exit(1)
  2494	
  2495	    # Add new task
  2496	    task_id = decomposer.add_task(
  2497	        description=description, duration=duration, priority=priority
  2498	    )
  2499	
  2500	    console.logger.info(f"[green]✅ Task added: {description}[/green]")
  2501	    console.logger.info(f"[blue]🆔 ID: {task_id}[/blue]")
  2502	    console.logger.info(f"[yellow]⏱️ Duration: {duration} minutes[/yellow]")
  2503	    console.logger.info(f"[cyan]🎯 Priority: {priority}[/cyan]")
  2504

  2506	@cli.group()
  2507	@click.pass_context
  2508	def autoresponder(ctx):
  2509	    """
  2510	    🤖 Manage Claude Auto Responder integration
  2511	
  2512	    Automatic confirmation responses for Claude Code prompts with
  2513	    ADHD-optimized controls and attention-aware features.
  2514	    """
  2515	
  2516	
  2517	@autoresponder.command("start")
  2518	@click.option(
  2519	    "--terminal-scope",
  2520	    "-t",
  2521	    type=click.Choice(["current", "all", "project"]),
  2522	    help="Terminal scope for monitoring",
  2523	)
  2524	@click.option("--delay", "-d", type=float, help="Response delay in seconds (0-10)")
  2525	@click.option("--timeout", type=int, help="Auto-stop timeout in minutes")
  2526	@click.option(
  2527	    "--whitelist/--no-whitelist", default=None, help="Enable/disable tool whitelisting"
  2528	)
  2529	@click.option("--debug/--no-debug", default=None, help="Enable/disable debug mode")
  2530	@click.pass_context
  2531	def autoresponder_start(ctx, terminal_scope, delay, timeout, whitelist, debug):
  2532	    """
  2533	    🚀 Start Claude Auto Responder
  2534	
  2535	    Begins automatic confirmation of Claude Code prompts with current
  2536	    configuration settings and ADHD optimizations.
  2537	    """
  2538	    config_manager = ctx.obj["config_manager"]
  2539	    project_path = Path.cwd()
  2540	
  2541	    if not (project_path / ".dopemux").exists():
  2542	        console.logger.info("[red]No Dopemux project found in current directory[/red]")
  2543	        sys.exit(1)
  2544	
  2545	    # Update configuration if options provided
  2546	    updates = {}
  2547	    if terminal_scope:
  2548	        updates["terminal_scope"] = terminal_scope
  2549	    if delay is not None:
  2550	        updates["response_delay"] = delay
  2551	    if timeout:
  2552	        updates["timeout_minutes"] = timeout
  2553	    if whitelist is not None:
  2554	        updates["whitelist_tools"] = whitelist
  2555	    if debug is not None:
  2556	        updates["debug_mode"] = debug
  2557	
  2558	    if updates:
  2559	        config_manager.update_claude_autoresponder(**updates)
  2560	
  2561	    from integrations.claude_autoresponder import create_autoresponder_manager
  2562	
  2563	    autoresponder_manager = create_autoresponder_manager(config_manager, project_path)
  2564	
  2565	    with Progress(
  2566	        SpinnerColumn(),
  2567	        TextColumn("[progress.description]{task.description}"),
  2568	        console=console,
  2569	    ) as progress:
  2570	        task = progress.add_task("Starting auto responder...", total=None)
  2571	
  2572	        success = autoresponder_manager.start()
  2573	
  2574	        if success:
  2575	            progress.update(
  2576	                task, description="Auto responder started! 🤖", completed=True
  2577	            )
  2578	            console.logger.info("[green]✅ Claude Auto Responder is now active[/green]")
  2579	            console.print(
  2580	                "[blue]🎯 Monitoring for Claude Code confirmation prompts[/blue]"
  2581	            )
  2582	
  2583	            config = config_manager.get_claude_autoresponder_config()
  2584	            console.logger.info(f"[yellow]📡 Scope: {config.terminal_scope}[/yellow]")
  2585	            if config.response_delay > 0:
  2586	                console.logger.info(f"[cyan]⏱️ Delay: {config.response_delay}s[/cyan]")
  2587	            console.print(
  2588	                f"[dim]💤 Auto-stop after {config.timeout_minutes} minutes of inactivity[/dim]"
  2589	            )
  2590	        else:
  2591	            progress.update(task, description="Failed to start", completed=True)
  2592	            console.logger.error("[red]❌ Failed to start auto responder[/red]")
  2593	            console.print(
  2594	                "[yellow]💡 Try running 'dopemux autoresponder setup' first[/yellow]"
  2595	            )
  2596	            sys.exit(1)

  2602	    """
  2603	    ⏹️ Stop Claude Auto Responder
  2604

  2644	                    f"  📈 Rate: {status['responses_per_minute']:.1f} responses/min"
  2645	                )
  2646	        else:
  2647	            progress.update(task, description="Error stopping", completed=True)
  2648	            console.logger.error("[red]❌ Error stopping auto responder[/red]")

  2749	
  2750	@cli.group()
  2751	@click.pass_context
  2752	def extract(ctx):
  2753	    """
  2754	    📄 Document extraction with ADHD-optimized patterns
  2755	
  2756	    Extract entities, configurations, and patterns from documentation
  2757	    using specialized extractors for markdown, YAML, and ADHD content.
  2758	    """
  2759	    pass
  2760	
  2761	
  2762	@extract.command("docs")
  2763	@click.argument("directory", default=".")
  2764	@click.option(
  2765	    "--mode", "-m",
  2766	    type=click.Choice(["basic", "detailed", "adhd"]),
  2767	    default="basic",
  2768	    help="Extraction mode: basic (key-value), detailed (all patterns), adhd (ADHD-specific)"
  2769	)
  2770	@click.option(
  2771	    "--format", "-f",
  2772	    type=click.Choice(["json", "csv", "markdown", "yaml"]),
  2773	    default="json",
  2774	    help="Output format for extracted entities"
  2775	)
  2776	@click.option("--output", "-o", help="Output file path (default: print to stdout)")
  2777	@click.option("--confidence", "-c", type=float, default=0.5, help="Minimum confidence threshold (0.0-1.0)")
  2778	@click.option("--extensions", help="File extensions to process (default: .md,.yaml,.yml)")
  2779	@click.option("--adhd-profile", "-p", is_flag=True, help="Extract ADHD accommodation profile")
  2780	@click.pass_context
  2781	def extract_docs(
  2782	    ctx,
  2783	    directory: str,
  2784	    mode: str,
  2785	    format: str,
  2786	    output: Optional[str],
  2787	    confidence: float,
  2788	    extensions: Optional[str],
  2789	    adhd_profile: bool
  2790	):
  2791	    """
  2792	    📄 Extract entities from documentation files
  2793	
  2794	    Process markdown and YAML files to extract structured information
  2795	    using ADHD-optimized patterns and confidence scoring.
  2796	    """
  2797	    with mobile_task_notification(
  2798	        ctx,
  2799	        "Documentation extraction",
  2800	        success_message="✅ Documentation extraction complete",
  2801	        failure_message="❌ Documentation extraction failed",
  2802	    ):
  2803	        _run_extract_docs(
  2804	            ctx,
  2805	            directory,
  2806	            mode,
  2807	            format,
  2808	            output,
  2809	            confidence,
  2810	            extensions,
  2811	            adhd_profile,
  2812	        )
  2813	
  2814	
  2815	def _run_extract_docs(
  2816	    ctx,
  2817	    directory: str,
  2818	    mode: str,
  2819	    format: str,
  2820	    output: Optional[str],
  2821	    confidence: float,
  2822	    extensions: Optional[str],
  2823	    adhd_profile: bool,
  2824	) -> None:
  2825	    from pathlib import Path
  2826	    import sys
  2827	    import json
  2828	    import csv
  2829	    from io import StringIO
  2830	
  2831	    # Add extraction package to path
  2832	    sys.path.append(str(Path(__file__).parent.parent.parent / "extraction"))
  2833	
  2834	    try:
  2835	        from document_classifier import DocumentClassifier, extract_from_directory
  2836	    except ImportError as e:
  2837	        console.logger.info(f"[red]❌ Could not import extraction modules: {e}[/red]")
  2838	        console.logger.info("[yellow]💡 Make sure you're in the dopemux-mvp directory[/yellow]")
  2839	        sys.exit(1)
  2840	
  2841	    source_path = Path(directory).resolve()
  2842	    if not source_path.exists():
  2843	        console.logger.info(f"[red]❌ Directory does not exist: {source_path}[/red]")
  2844	        sys.exit(1)
  2845	
  2846	    if not extensions:
  2847	        extensions = ".md,.yaml,.yml,.json"
  2848	
  2849	    with Progress(
  2850	        SpinnerColumn(),
  2851	        TextColumn("[progress.description]{task.description}"),
  2852	        console=console,
  2853	    ) as progress:
  2854	        task = progress.add_task(f"Extracting entities in {mode} mode...", total=None)
  2855	
  2856	        try:
  2857	            results = extract_from_directory(str(source_path))
  2858	
  2859	            progress.update(task, description="Processing results...", total=None)
  2860	
  2861	            filtered_entities = {}
  2862	            total_entities = 0
  2863	            filtered_count = 0
  2864	
  2865	            for entity_type, entity_list in results.get('all_entities', {}).items():
  2866	                filtered_list = []
  2867	                for entity in entity_list:
  2868	                    total_entities += 1
  2869	                    entity_confidence = entity.get('confidence', 0.0)
  2870	                    if entity_confidence >= confidence:
  2871	                        filtered_list.append(entity)
  2872	                        filtered_count += 1
  2873	
  2874	                if filtered_list:
  2875	                    filtered_entities[entity_type] = filtered_list
  2876	
  2877	            if mode == "basic":
  2878	                basic_types = ['section_header', 'project_metadata', 'yaml_properties', 'markdown_headers']
  2879	                filtered_entities = {k: v for k, v in filtered_entities.items() if k in basic_types}
  2880	            elif mode == "adhd":
  2881	                adhd_keywords = ['adhd', 'focus', 'break', 'attention', 'cognitive', 'accommodation']
  2882	                adhd_types = [
  2883	                    k
  2884	                    for k in filtered_entities.keys()
  2885	                    if any(keyword in k.lower() for keyword in adhd_keywords)
  2886	                ]
  2887	                filtered_entities = {k: v for k, v in filtered_entities.items() if k in adhd_types}
  2888	
  2889	            progress.update(task, description="Formatting output...", total=None)
  2890	
  2891	            output_data = {
  2892	                'extraction_summary': {
  2893	                    'mode': mode,
  2894	                    'source_directory': str(source_path),
  2895	                    'documents_processed': results.get('documents_processed', 0),
  2896	                    'total_entities_found': total_entities,
  2897	                    'entities_above_threshold': filtered_count,
  2898	                    'confidence_threshold': confidence,
  2899	                    'entity_types': list(filtered_entities.keys()),
  2900	                },
  2901	                'entities': filtered_entities,
  2902	            }
  2903	
  2904	            if adhd_profile and results.get('metadata', {}).get('adhd_documents'):
  2905	                sys.path.append(str(Path(__file__).parent.parent.parent / "extraction"))
  2906	                from adhd_entities import ADHDEntityExtractor
  2907	
  2908	                extractor = ADHDEntityExtractor()
  2909	                for doc_info in results.get('document_types', {}).get('markdown', []):
  2910	                    if doc_info['filename'] in results['metadata']['adhd_documents']:
  2911	                        output_data['adhd_profile'] = {
  2912	                            'accommodation_categories': ['attention_management', 'energy_management'],
  2913	                            'confidence_note': 'Profile extraction requires document content access',
  2914	                        }
  2915	                        break
  2916	
  2917	            progress.update(task, description="Complete! ✅", completed=True)
  2918	
  2919	        except Exception as e:
  2920	            progress.update(task, description="Error occurred", completed=True)
  2921	            console.logger.error(f"[red]❌ Extraction failed: {e}[/red]")
  2922	            if ctx.obj.get("verbose"):
  2923	                import traceback
  2924	                traceback.print_exc()
  2925	            sys.exit(1)
  2926	
  2927	    if format == "json":
  2928	        output_text = json.dumps(output_data, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)
  2929	    elif format == "yaml":
  2930	        try:
  2931	            import yaml
  2932	
  2933	            output_text = yaml.dump(output_data, default_flow_style=False, allow_unicode=True)
  2934	        except ImportError:
  2935	            console.logger.info("[yellow]⚠️ PyYAML not available, falling back to JSON[/yellow]")
  2936	            output_text = json.dumps(output_data, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)
  2937	    elif format == "csv":
  2938	        output_buffer = StringIO()
  2939	        writer = csv.writer(output_buffer)
  2940	        writer.writerow(['entity_type', 'content', 'value', 'confidence', 'source_file'])
  2941	
  2942	        for entity_type, entity_list in filtered_entities.items():
  2943	            for entity in entity_list:
  2944	                writer.writerow(
  2945	                    [
  2946	                        entity_type,
  2947	                        entity.get('content', ''),
  2948	                        entity.get('value', ''),
  2949	                        entity.get('confidence', 0.0),
  2950	                        entity.get('source_file', ''),
  2951	                    ]
  2952	                )
  2953	        output_text = output_buffer.getvalue()
  2954	    elif format == "markdown":
  2955	        lines = [f"# Extraction Results - {mode.title()} Mode\n"]
  2956	        lines.append(f"**Source**: {source_path}")
  2957	        lines.append(f"**Documents**: {output_data['extraction_summary']['documents_processed']}")
  2958	        lines.append(f"**Entities**: {filtered_count}/{total_entities} (confidence ≥ {confidence})\n")
  2959	
  2960	        for entity_type, entity_list in filtered_entities.items():
  2961	            lines.append(f"## {entity_type.replace('_', ' ').title()}\n")
  2962	            for entity in entity_list:
  2963	                lines.append(f"- **{entity.get('content', 'N/A')}**")
  2964	                if entity.get('value'):
  2965	                    lines.append(f": {entity['value']}")
  2966	                lines.append(f" _(confidence: {entity.get('confidence', 0.0):.2f})_")
  2967	                lines.append("")
  2968	
  2969	        output_text = "\n".join(lines)
  2970	    else:
  2971	        output_text = json.dumps(output_data, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)
  2972	
  2973	    if output:
  2974	        output_path = Path(output)
  2975	        output_path.write_text(output_text, encoding='utf-8')
  2976	        console.logger.info(f"[green]✅ Results written to {output_path}[/green]")
  2977	    else:
  2978	        console.logger.info(output_text)
  2979	
  2980	    console.print(
  2981	        Panel(
  2982	            f"🎯 Extraction Summary:\n\n"
  2983	            f"• Mode: {mode}\n"
  2984	            f"• Documents: {results.get('documents_processed', 0)}\n"
  2985	            f"• Entities: {filtered_count}/{total_entities}\n"
  2986	            f"• Entity types: {len(filtered_entities)}\n"
  2987	            f"• Format: {format}",
  2988	            title="📊 Results",
  2989	            border_style="green",
  2990	        )
  2991	    )
  2992	
  2993	
  2994	@extract.command("pipeline")
  2995	@click.argument("directory", default=".")
  2996	@click.option("--output", "-o", help="Output directory for pipeline results", default="./output")
  2997	@click.option(
  2998	    "--adhd/--no-adhd",
  2999	    default=True,
  3000	    help="Enable/disable ADHD-specific extraction patterns"
  3001	)
  3002	@click.option(
  3003	    "--multi-angle/--no-multi-angle",
  3004	    default=True,
  3005	    help="Enable/disable multi-angle entity extraction"
  3006	)
  3007	@click.option(
  3008	    "--embeddings/--no-embeddings",
  3009	    default=True,
  3010	    help="Enable/disable vector embedding generation"
  3011	)
  3012	@click.option(
  3013	    "--tsv/--no-tsv",
  3014	    default=True,
  3015	    help="Enable/disable TSV registry generation"
  3016	)
  3017	@click.option(
  3018	    "--confidence", "-c",
  3019	    type=float,
  3020	    default=0.5,
  3021	    help="Minimum confidence threshold for entities (0.0-1.0)"
  3022	)
  3023	@click.option(
  3024	    "--embedding-model", "-m",
  3025	    default="voyage-context-3",
  3026	    help="Embedding model to use"
  3027	)
  3028	@click.option("--milvus-uri", help="Milvus database URI for vector storage")
  3029	@click.option("--extensions", help="File extensions to process (default: .md,.yaml,.yml,.json,.txt)")
  3030	@click.option(
  3031	    "--format", "-f",
  3032	    type=click.Choice(["json", "csv", "markdown"]),
  3033	    default="json",
  3034	    help="Output format for extraction results"
  3035	)
  3036	@click.option(
  3037	    "--synthesis/--no-synthesis",
  3038	    default=True,
  3039	    help="Enable/disable document synthesis generation"
  3040	)
  3041	@click.option(
  3042	    "--synthesis-types",
  3043	    multiple=True,

  3045	    default=["executive", "adhd"],
  3046	    help="Types of synthesis to generate (can specify multiple)"
  3047	)
  3048	@click.option(
  3049	    "--synthesis-format",
  3050	    type=click.Choice(["markdown", "json", "both"]),
  3051	    default="markdown",
  3052	    help="Output format for synthesis results"
  3053	)
  3054	@click.pass_context
  3055	def extract_pipeline(
  3056	    ctx,
  3057	    directory: str,
  3058	    output: str,
  3059	    adhd: bool,
  3060	    multi_angle: bool,
  3061	    embeddings: bool,
  3062	    tsv: bool,
  3063	    confidence: float,
  3064	    embedding_model: str,
  3065	    milvus_uri: Optional[str],
  3066	    extensions: Optional[str],
  3067	    format: str,
  3068	    synthesis: bool,
  3069	    synthesis_types: tuple,
  3070	    synthesis_format: str
  3071	):
  3072	    """
  3073	    🚀 Complete document processing pipeline
  3074	
  3075	    Run the full unified pipeline including multi-layer extraction,
  3076	    atomic unit normalization, TSV registry generation, and vector
  3077	    embeddings. Integrates all extraction systems into a single workflow.
  3078	    """
  3079	    with mobile_task_notification(
  3080	        ctx,
  3081	        "Extraction pipeline",
  3082	        success_message="✅ Extraction pipeline complete",
  3083	        failure_message="❌ Extraction pipeline failed",
  3084	    ):
  3085	        _run_extract_pipeline(
  3086	            ctx,
  3087	            directory,
  3088	            output,
  3089	            adhd,
  3090	            multi_angle,
  3091	            embeddings,
  3092	            tsv,
  3093	            confidence,
  3094	            embedding_model,
  3095	            milvus_uri,
  3096	            extensions,
  3097	            format,
  3098	            synthesis,
  3099	            synthesis_types,
  3100	            synthesis_format,
  3101	        )
  3102	
  3103	
  3104	def _run_extract_pipeline(
  3105	    ctx,
  3106	    directory: str,
  3107	    output: str,
  3108	    adhd: bool,
  3109	    multi_angle: bool,
  3110	    embeddings: bool,
  3111	    tsv: bool,
  3112	    confidence: float,
  3113	    embedding_model: str,
  3114	    milvus_uri: Optional[str],
  3115	    extensions: Optional[str],
  3116	    format: str,
  3117	    synthesis: bool,
  3118	    synthesis_types: tuple,
  3119	    synthesis_format: str,
  3120	) -> None:
  3121	    from pathlib import Path
  3122	    import sys
  3123	
  3124	    try:
  3125	        from .extraction import UnifiedDocumentPipeline, PipelineConfig
  3126	    except ImportError as e:
  3127	        console.logger.info(f"[red]❌ Could not import pipeline modules: {e}[/red]")
  3128	        console.logger.info("[yellow]💡 Make sure the extraction package is properly installed[/yellow]")
  3129	        sys.exit(1)
  3130	
  3131	    source_path = Path(directory).resolve()
  3132	    output_path = Path(output).resolve()
  3133	
  3134	    if not source_path.exists():
  3135	        console.logger.info(f"[red]❌ Source directory does not exist: {source_path}[/red]")
  3136	        sys.exit(1)
  3137	
  3138	    file_extensions = None
  3139	    if extensions:
  3140	        file_extensions = [ext.strip() for ext in extensions.split(',')]
  3141	        if not all(ext.startswith('.') for ext in file_extensions):
  3142	            file_extensions = ['.' + ext.lstrip('.') for ext in file_extensions]
  3143	
  3144	    synthesis_types_list = list(synthesis_types)
  3145	    if "all" in synthesis_types_list:
  3146	        synthesis_types_list = ["executive", "adhd", "technical"]
  3147	
  3148	    config = PipelineConfig(
  3149	        source_directory=source_path,
  3150	        output_directory=output_path,
  3151	        enable_adhd_extraction=adhd,
  3152	        enable_multi_angle=multi_angle,
  3153	        file_extensions=file_extensions,
  3154	        confidence_threshold=confidence,
  3155	        generate_tsv_registries=tsv,
  3156	        generate_embeddings=embeddings,
  3157	        embedding_model=embedding_model,
  3158	        milvus_uri=milvus_uri,
  3159	        export_json=(format == "json"),
  3160	        export_csv=(format == "csv"),
  3161	        export_markdown=(format == "markdown"),
  3162	        enable_synthesis=synthesis,
  3163	        synthesis_types=synthesis_types_list,
  3164	        synthesis_format=synthesis_format,
  3165	    )
  3166	
  3167	    console.logger.info(f"[blue]🚀 Starting unified document pipeline...[/blue]")
  3168	    console.logger.info(f"[blue]📁 Source: {source_path}[/blue]")
  3169	    console.logger.info(f"[blue]📤 Output: {output_path}[/blue]")
  3170	
  3171	    with Progress(
  3172	        SpinnerColumn(),
  3173	        TextColumn("[progress.description]{task.description}"),
  3174	        console=console,
  3175	    ) as progress:
  3176	        task = progress.add_task("Initializing pipeline...", total=None)
  3177	
  3178	        try:
  3179	            pipeline = UnifiedDocumentPipeline(config)
  3180	            result = pipeline.process_documents()
  3181	
  3182	            if result.success:
  3183	                progress.update(task, description="Pipeline completed successfully! ✅", completed=True)
  3184	
  3185	                console.print(
  3186	                    Panel(
  3187	                        f"🎯 Pipeline Results:\n\n"
  3188	                        f"• Processing time: {result.processing_time:.2f}s\n"
  3189	                        f"• Documents processed: {result.document_count}\n"
  3190	                        f"• Total entities extracted: {result.total_entities}\n"
  3191	                        f"• TSV registries: {len(result.registry_files or {})}\n"
  3192	                        f"• Vector embeddings: {result.vector_count}\n"
  3193	                        f"• Output files: {len(result.output_files or [])}\n\n"
  3194	                        f"📊 Configuration:\n"
  3195	                        f"• ADHD extraction: {'✅' if adhd else '❌'}\n"
  3196	                        f"• Multi-angle extraction: {'✅' if multi_angle else '❌'}\n"
  3197	                        f"• TSV registries: {'✅' if tsv else '❌'}\n"
  3198	                        f"• Vector embeddings: {'✅' if embeddings else '❌'}\n"
  3199	                        f"• Confidence threshold: {confidence}",
  3200	                        title="🚀 Pipeline Complete",
  3201	                        border_style="green",
  3202	                    )
  3203	                )
  3204	
  3205	                if result.output_files:
  3206	                    console.logger.info("\n[green]📤 Generated files:[/green]")
  3207	                    for file_path in result.output_files:
  3208	                        console.logger.info(f"  • {file_path}")
  3209	
  3210	                if result.registry_files:
  3211	                    console.logger.info("\n[green]📊 TSV registries:[/green]")
  3212	                    for name, path in result.registry_files.items():
  3213	                        count = result.registry_counts.get(name, 0) if result.registry_counts else 0
  3214	                        console.logger.info(f"  • {name}: {path} ({count} entries)")
  3215	
  3216	                if result.embedding_summary:
  3217	                    console.logger.info("\n[green]🔍 Embeddings:[/green]")
  3218	                    console.logger.info(f"  • Model: {result.embedding_summary.get('model', 'N/A')}")
  3219	                    console.logger.info(f"  • Vectors: {result.vector_count}")
  3220	
  3221	            else:
  3222	                progress.update(task, description="Pipeline failed ❌", completed=True)
  3223	                console.logger.error(f"[red]❌ Pipeline failed: {result.error_message}[/red]")
  3224	                sys.exit(1)
  3225	
  3226	        except Exception as e:
  3227	            progress.update(task, description="Error occurred", completed=True)
  3228	            console.logger.error(f"[red]❌ Pipeline execution failed: {e}[/red]")
  3229	            if ctx.obj.get("verbose"):
  3230	                import traceback
  3231	                traceback.print_exc()
  3232	            sys.exit(1)
  3233

  3235	@extract.command("cleanup")

  3245	    type=click.Choice(["temporary", "cache", "outputs", "interim", "all"]),
  3246	    default=["temporary", "cache", "interim"],
  3247	    help="Types of files to clean (can specify multiple)"
  3248	)
  3249	@click.option(
  3250	    "--include-outputs/--preserve-outputs",
  3251	    default=False,
  3252	    help="Include output files in cleanup (default: preserve)"
  3253	)
  3254	@click.option(
  3255	    "--report-format",
  3256	    type=click.Choice(["table", "json", "detailed"]),
  3257	    default="detailed",
  3258	    help="Format for cleanup report"
  3259	)
  3260	@click.option("--report-file", help="Save cleanup report to file")
  3261	@click.pass_context
  3262	def extract_cleanup(
  3263	    ctx,
  3264	    directory: str,
  3265	    dry_run: bool,
  3266	    cleanup_types: tuple,
  3267	    include_outputs: bool,
  3268	    report_format: str,
  3269	    report_file: Optional[str]
  3270	):
  3271	    """
  3272	    🧹 Clean pipeline files and generate activity report
  3273	
  3274	    Remove temporary, cache, and interim files created during pipeline processing.
  3275	    Provides detailed reporting on files removed, created, changed, and output.
  3276	
  3277	    Default behavior preserves output files and runs in dry-run mode for safety.
  3278	    """
  3279	    with mobile_task_notification(
  3280	        ctx,
  3281	        "Pipeline cleanup",
  3282	        success_message="✅ Pipeline cleanup complete",
  3283	        failure_message="❌ Pipeline cleanup failed",
  3284	    ):
  3285	        _run_extract_cleanup(
  3286	            ctx,
  3287	            directory,
  3288	            dry_run,
  3289	            cleanup_types,
  3290	            include_outputs,
  3291	            report_format,
  3292	            report_file,
  3293	        )
  3294	
  3295	
  3296	def _run_extract_cleanup(
  3297	    ctx,
  3298	    directory: str,
  3299	    dry_run: bool,
  3300	    cleanup_types: tuple,
  3301	    include_outputs: bool,
  3302	    report_format: str,
  3303	    report_file: Optional[str],
  3304	) -> None:
  3305	    from pathlib import Path
  3306	    import sys
  3307	    import json
  3308	    from datetime import datetime
  3309	
  3310	    # Import cleanup modules
  3311	    try:
  3312	        from .extraction.cleanup import PipelineCleanup, CleanupConfig
  3313	    except ImportError as e:
  3314	        console.logger.info(f"[red]❌ Could not import cleanup modules: {e}[/red]")
  3315	        console.logger.info("[yellow]💡 Make sure the extraction package is properly installed[/yellow]")
  3316	        sys.exit(1)
  3317	
  3318	    target_path = Path(directory).resolve()
  3319	
  3320	    if not target_path.exists():
  3321	        console.logger.info(f"[red]❌ Target directory does not exist: {target_path}[/red]")
  3322	        sys.exit(1)
  3323	
  3324	    # Configure cleanup
  3325	    cleanup_types_list = list(cleanup_types)
  3326	    if "all" in cleanup_types_list:
  3327	        cleanup_types_list = ["temporary", "cache", "outputs", "interim"]
  3328	    elif include_outputs and "outputs" not in cleanup_types_list:
  3329	        cleanup_types_list.append("outputs")
  3330	
  3331	    config = CleanupConfig(
  3332	        cleanup_types=cleanup_types_list,
  3333	        dry_run=dry_run,
  3334	        preserve_recent_hours=0,  # Clean all matching files
  3335	        include_hidden=False,
  3336	        backup_before_delete=False  # For safety in dry-run mode
  3337	    )
  3338	
  3339	    console.logger.info(f"[blue]🧹 {'Previewing' if dry_run else 'Executing'} pipeline cleanup...[/blue]")
  3340	    console.logger.info(f"[blue]📁 Target: {target_path}[/blue]")
  3341	    console.logger.info(f"[blue]🎯 Cleanup types: {', '.join(cleanup_types_list)}[/blue]")
  3342	
  3343	    if dry_run:
  3344	        console.logger.info("[yellow]⚠️  DRY RUN: No files will actually be removed[/yellow]")
  3345	
  3346	    with Progress(
  3347	        SpinnerColumn(),
  3348	        TextColumn("[progress.description]{task.description}"),
  3349	        console=console,
  3350	    ) as progress:
  3351	        task = progress.add_task("Scanning for cleanup candidates...", total=None)
  3352	
  3353	        try:
  3354	            # Create cleanup system and generate mock activity report
  3355	            cleanup = PipelineCleanup(config)
  3356	
  3357	            # For cleanup command, we simulate an activity report for the target directory
  3358	            mock_activity_report = {
  3359	                "operation_summary": {
  3360	                    "start_time": datetime.now().isoformat(),
  3361	                    "end_time": datetime.now().isoformat(),
  3362	                    "total_operations": 0,
  3363	                    "directories_scanned": [str(target_path)]
  3364	                },
  3365	                "file_operations": {
  3366	                    "created": [],
  3367	                    "modified": [],
  3368	                    "deleted": [],
  3369	                    "moved": []
  3370	                },
  3371	                "size_tracking": {
  3372	                    "total_bytes_created": 0,
  3373	                    "total_bytes_modified": 0,
  3374	                    "total_bytes_deleted": 0
  3375	                },
  3376	                "categorization": {
  3377	                    "by_extension": {},
  3378	                    "by_operation": {},
  3379	                    "by_directory": {}
  3380	                }
  3381	            }
  3382	
  3383	            progress.update(task, description="Performing cleanup analysis...")
  3384	
  3385	            # Perform cleanup
  3386	            result = cleanup.cleanup_pipeline_files(mock_activity_report, target_path)
  3387	
  3388	            if result.success:
  3389	                progress.update(task, description=f"Cleanup {'preview' if dry_run else 'execution'} completed! ✅", completed=True)
  3390	
  3391	                # Generate detailed report
  3392	                if report_format == "detailed":
  3393	                    console.print(
  3394	                        Panel(
  3395	                            f"🧹 Cleanup Results:\n\n"
  3396	                            f"• Files removed: {result.files_removed}\n"
  3397	                            f"• Space freed: {result.space_freed / (1024*1024):.2f} MB\n"
  3398	                            f"• Processing time: {result.processing_time:.2f}s\n"
  3399	                            f"• Errors: {len(result.errors)}\n\n"
  3400	                            f"📊 File Types Cleaned:\n"
  3401	                            + "\n".join([f"• {category}: {count} files"
  3402	                                       for category, count in result.files_by_category.items()]),
  3403	                            title=f"🧹 Cleanup {'Preview' if dry_run else 'Complete'}",
  3404	                            border_style="green" if result.success else "red",
  3405	                        )
  3406	                    )
  3407	
  3408	                    # Show detailed file lists
  3409	                    if result.removed_files:
  3410	                        console.logger.info(f"\n[green]{'📋 Files to be removed:' if dry_run else '🗑️  Files removed:'}[/green]")
  3411	                        for file_path in result.removed_files[:20]:  # Show first 20
  3412	                            file_size = file_path.stat().st_size if file_path.exists() else 0
  3413	                            size_str = f"({file_size / 1024:.1f} KB)" if file_size > 0 else ""
  3414	                            console.logger.info(f"  • {file_path.relative_to(target_path)} {size_str}")
  3415	
  3416	                        if len(result.removed_files) > 20:
  3417	                            console.logger.info(f"  ... and {len(result.removed_files) - 20} more files")
  3418	
  3419	                    # Show errors if any
  3420	                    if result.errors:
  3421	                        console.logger.error(f"\n[red]⚠️  Errors encountered:[/red]")
  3422	                        for error in result.errors[:5]:  # Show first 5 errors
  3423	                            console.logger.error(f"  • {error}")
  3424	                        if len(result.errors) > 5:
  3425	                            console.logger.error(f"  ... and {len(result.errors) - 5} more errors")
  3426	
  3427	                elif report_format == "table":
  3428	                    # Create a summary table
  3429	                    from rich.table import Table
  3430	
  3431	                    table = Table(title=f"Cleanup {'Preview' if dry_run else 'Results'}")
  3432	                    table.add_column("Category", style="cyan")
  3433	                    table.add_column("Files", justify="right", style="magenta")
  3434	                    table.add_column("Size", justify="right", style="green")
  3435	
  3436	                    for category, count in result.files_by_category.items():
  3437	                        # Calculate size for this category
  3438	                        category_size = sum(
  3439	                            f.stat().st_size if f.exists() else 0
  3440	                            for f in result.removed_files
  3441	                            if category.lower() in str(f).lower()
  3442	                        )
  3443	                        size_mb = category_size / (1024 * 1024)
  3444	                        table.add_row(category, str(count), f"{size_mb:.2f} MB")
  3445	
  3446	                    console.logger.info(table)
  3447	
  3448	                elif report_format == "json":
  3449	                    # JSON summary
  3450	                    json_result = {
  3451	                        "cleanup_summary": {
  3452	                            "dry_run": dry_run,
  3453	                            "success": result.success,
  3454	                            "files_removed": result.files_removed,
  3455	                            "space_freed_mb": result.space_freed / (1024*1024),
  3456	                            "processing_time": result.processing_time,
  3457	                            "target_directory": str(target_path),
  3458	                            "cleanup_types": cleanup_types_list
  3459	                        },
  3460	                        "file_categories": result.files_by_category,
  3461	                        "removed_files": [str(f) for f in result.removed_files],
  3462	                        "errors": result.errors,
  3463	                        "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat()
  3464	                    }
  3465	                    console.logger.info(json.dumps(json_result, indent=2))
  3466	
  3467	                # Save report to file if requested
  3468	                if report_file:
  3469	                    report_path = Path(report_file)
  3470	                    report_data = {
  3471	                        "cleanup_summary": {
  3472	                            "dry_run": dry_run,
  3473	                            "success": result.success,
  3474	                            "files_removed": result.files_removed,
  3475	                            "space_freed_mb": result.space_freed / (1024*1024),
  3476	                            "processing_time": result.processing_time,
  3477	                            "target_directory": str(target_path),
  3478	                            "cleanup_types": cleanup_types_list,
  3479	                            "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat()
  3480	                        },
  3481	                        "detailed_results": {
  3482	                            "file_categories": result.files_by_category,
  3483	                            "removed_files": [str(f) for f in result.removed_files],
  3484	                            "errors": result.errors
  3485	                        }
  3486	                    }
  3487	
  3488	                    with open(report_path, 'w') as f:
  3489	                        json.dump(report_data, f, indent=2)
  3490	
  3491	                    console.logger.info(f"\n[green]📄 Report saved to: {report_path}[/green]")
  3492	
  3493	            else:
  3494	                progress.update(task, description="Cleanup failed ❌", completed=True)
  3495	                console.logger.error(f"[red]❌ Cleanup failed: {result.error_message}[/red]")
  3496	                sys.exit(1)
  3497	
  3498	        except Exception as e:
  3499	            progress.update(task, description="Error occurred", completed=True)
  3500	            console.logger.error(f"[red]❌ Cleanup execution failed: {e}[/red]")
  3501	            if ctx.obj.get("verbose"):
  3502	                import traceback
  3503	                traceback.print_exc()
  3504	            sys.exit(1)

  3506	
  3507	@cli.command()
  3508	@click.argument("directory", default=".")
  3509	@click.option("--output", "-o", help="Output directory for analysis results")
  3510	@click.option(
  3511	    "--embedding-model", "-m", default="voyage-context-3", help="Embedding model to use"
  3512	)
  3513	@click.option("--milvus-uri", help="Milvus database URI (file path for Lite mode)")
  3514	@click.option("--max-files", type=int, help="Maximum number of files to process")
  3515	@click.option("--batch-size", type=int, default=10, help="Batch size for processing")
  3516	@click.option("--extensions", help="Comma-separated list of file extensions to include")
  3517	@click.option("--exclude", help="Comma-separated list of patterns to exclude")
  3518	@click.pass_context
  3519	def analyze(
  3520	    ctx,
  3521	    directory: str,
  3522	    output: Optional[str],
  3523	    embedding_model: str,
  3524	    milvus_uri: Optional[str],
  3525	    max_files: Optional[int],
  3526	    batch_size: int,
  3527	    extensions: Optional[str],
  3528	    exclude: Optional[str],
  3529	):
  3530	    """
  3531	    🔍 Analyze codebase with multi-angle document processing
  3532	
  3533	    Processes documents in the specified directory, extracting features,
  3534	    components, subsystems, and research insights with semantic embeddings
  3535	    for intelligent code navigation and ADHD-friendly analysis.
  3536	    """
  3537	    from .analysis import DocumentProcessor, ProcessingConfig
  3538	
  3539	    # Prepare configuration
  3540	    source_path = Path(directory).resolve()
  3541	    if not source_path.exists():
  3542	        console.logger.info(f"[red]❌ Directory does not exist: {source_path}[/red]")
  3543	        sys.exit(1)
  3544	
  3545	    # Set output directory
  3546	    if output:
  3547	        output_path = Path(output).resolve()
  3548	    else:
  3549	        output_path = source_path / ".dopemux" / "analysis"
  3550	
  3551	    output_path.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
  3552	
  3553	    # Parse extensions
  3554	    file_extensions = None
  3555	    if extensions:
  3556	        file_extensions = [
  3557	            f".{ext.strip().lstrip('.')}" for ext in extensions.split(",")
  3558	        ]
  3559	
  3560	    # Parse exclusion patterns
  3561	    exclude_patterns = None
  3562	    if exclude:
  3563	        exclude_patterns = [pattern.strip() for pattern in exclude.split(",")]
  3564	
  3565	    # Create configuration
  3566	    config = ProcessingConfig(
  3567	        source_directory=source_path,
  3568	        output_directory=output_path,
  3569	        max_files=max_files,
  3570	        file_extensions=file_extensions,
  3571	        exclude_patterns=exclude_patterns,
  3572	        embedding_model=embedding_model,
  3573	        milvus_uri=milvus_uri,
  3574	        batch_size=batch_size,
  3575	        show_progress=True,
  3576	        gentle_feedback=True,
  3577	    )
  3578	
  3579	    # Initialize and run processor
  3580	    console.logger.info(f"[blue]🧠 Starting ADHD-optimized analysis of {source_path}[/blue]")
  3581	    console.logger.info(f"[dim]Output: {output_path}[/dim]")
  3582	
  3583	    try:
  3584	        processor = DocumentProcessor(config)
  3585	        results = processor.analyze_directory()
  3586	
  3587	        if results["success"]:
  3588	            console.print(
  3589	                f"[green]✅ Analysis complete! Results saved to {output_path}[/green]"
  3590	            )
  3591	            console.print(
  3592	                f"[blue]📊 Processing time: {results['processing_time']:.1f}s[/blue]"
  3593	            )
  3594	
  3595	            # Show usage suggestions
  3596	            console.print(
  3597	                Panel(
  3598	                    f"🎯 Next steps:\n\n"
  3599	                    f"• Browse results in {output_path}\n"
  3600	                    f"• Use semantic search with embeddings\n"
  3601	                    f"• Explore feature and component registries\n"
  3602	                    f"• Review evidence links for traceability",
  3603	                    title="🚀 Ready to Explore",
  3604	                    border_style="green",
  3605	                )
  3606	            )
  3607	        else:
  3608	            console.logger.error("[red]❌ Analysis failed[/red]")
  3609	            sys.exit(1)
  3610	
  3611	    except Exception as e:
  3612	        console.logger.error(f"[red]❌ Analysis error: {e}[/red]")
  3613	        if ctx.obj.get("verbose"):
  3614	            import traceback
  3615	
  3616	            traceback.print_exc()
  3617	        sys.exit(1)
  3618	
  3619	
  3620	@cli.group()
  3621	def mcp():
  3622	    """Manage MCP Docker servers (start/stop/status/logs)."""
  3623	
  3624	
  3625	@mcp.command("up")
  3626	@click.option("--all", "all_services", is_flag=True, help="Start all MCP servers")
  3627	@click.option("--services", "services", help="Comma-separated services to start")
  3628	def mcp_up_cmd(all_services: bool, services: str):
  3629	    """Start MCP servers via docker-compose."""
  3630	    try:
  3631	        cmd = "cd docker/mcp-servers && "
  3632	        if all_services or not services:
  3633	            cmd += "./start-all-mcp-servers.sh"
  3634	        else:
  3635	            svc_list = " ".join(s.strip() for s in services.split(",") if s.strip())
  3636	            cmd += f"docker-compose up -d --build {svc_list}"
  3637	        console.logger.info(f"[blue]🔌 {cmd}[/blue]")
  3638	        subprocess.run(["bash","-lc", cmd], check=True)
  3639	        console.logger.info("[green]✅ MCP servers started[/green]")
  3640	    except CalledProcessError:
  3641	        console.logger.error("[red]❌ Failed to start MCP servers[/red]")
  3642	        sys.exit(1)
  3643	
  3644	
  3645	@mcp.command("down")
  3646	def mcp_down_cmd():
  3647	    """Stop all MCP servers."""
  3648	    try:
  3649	        subprocess.run(["bash","-lc","cd docker/mcp-servers && docker-compose down"], check=True)
  3650	        console.logger.info("[green]✅ MCP servers stopped[/green]")
  3651	    except CalledProcessError:
  3652	        console.logger.error("[red]❌ Failed to stop MCP servers[/red]")
  3653	        sys.exit(1)
  3654	
  3655	
  3656	@mcp.command("status")
  3657	def mcp_status_cmd():
  3658	    """Show docker-compose status for MCP servers."""
  3659	    try:
  3660	        subprocess.run(["bash","-lc","cd docker/mcp-servers && docker-compose ps"], check=False)
  3661	    except CalledProcessError:
  3662	        sys.exit(1)
  3663	
  3664	
  3665	@mcp.command("logs")
  3666	@click.option("--service", "service", help="Service to tail logs for")
  3667	def mcp_logs_cmd(service: str):
  3668	    """Tail logs for an MCP service or all."""
  3669	    try:
  3670	        if service:
  3671	            cmd = f"cd docker/mcp-servers && docker-compose logs -f {service}"
  3672	        else:
  3673	            cmd = "cd docker/mcp-servers && docker-compose logs -f"
  3674	        console.logger.info(f"[blue]📄 {cmd}[/blue]")
  3675	        subprocess.run(["bash","-lc", cmd], check=False)
  3676	    except CalledProcessError:
  3677	        sys.exit(1)
  3678	
  3679	
  3680	@mcp.command("start-all")
  3681	@click.option("--verify", "-v", is_flag=True, help="Verify service health after starting")
  3682	def mcp_start_all_cmd(verify: bool):
  3683	    """
  3684	    🚀 Start complete Dopemux stack (MCP servers + application services)
  3685	
  3686	    Starts all services including:
  3687	    - 12 MCP servers (ConPort, Zen, Serena, Context7, etc.)
  3688	    - Integration Bridge (event processing, pattern detection)
  3689	    - Task Orchestrator (ADHD task coordination)
  3690	    - All infrastructure (PostgreSQL, Redis, Qdrant)
  3691	
  3692	    \b
  3693	    Examples:
  3694	        dopemux mcp start-all           # Start everything
  3695	        dopemux mcp start-all --verify  # Start + verify health
  3696	
  3697	    \b
  3698	    ADHD Benefit:
  3699	        One command to start the complete event-driven intelligence system.
  3700	        No need to remember which services to start manually.
  3701	    """
  3702	    try:
  3703	        # Run the start-all.sh script
  3704	        script_path = Path(__file__).parent.parent.parent / "scripts" / "start-all.sh"
  3705	
  3706	        if not script_path.exists():
  3707	            console.logger.info(f"[red]❌ start-all.sh not found at {script_path}[/red]")
  3708	            console.logger.info("[yellow]Falling back to manual startup...[/yellow]")
  3709	
  3710	            # Fallback: manual startup
  3711	            console.logger.info("[blue]Starting MCP servers...[/blue]")
  3712	            subprocess.run(["bash","-lc","cd docker/mcp-servers && docker-compose up -d"], check=True)
  3713	
  3714	            console.logger.info("[blue]Starting Integration Bridge...[/blue]")
  3715	            subprocess.run(["bash","-lc","cd docker/conport-kg && docker-compose up -d --no-deps integration-bridge"], check=True)
  3716	
  3717	            console.logger.info("[blue]Starting Task Orchestrator...[/blue]")
  3718	            subprocess.run(["bash","-lc","cd docker/mcp-servers && docker-compose --profile manual up -d task-orchestrator"], check=True)
  3719	
  3720	            console.logger.info("[green]✅ All services started[/green]")
  3721	        else:
  3722	            # Use the script
  3723	            cmd = ["bash", str(script_path)]
  3724	            if verify:
  3725	                cmd.append("--verify")
  3726	
  3727	            subprocess.run(cmd, check=True)
  3728	
  3729	    except CalledProcessError:
  3730	        console.logger.error("[red]❌ Failed to start all services[/red]")
  3731	        console.logger.info("[yellow]💡 Try: docker ps to see running containers[/yellow]")
  3732	        sys.exit(1)
  3733

  3763	@cli.command()
  3764	@click.option("--detailed", "-d", is_flag=True, help="Show detailed health information")
  3765	@click.option("--service", "-s", help="Check specific service only")
  3766	@click.option("--fix", "-f", is_flag=True, help="Attempt to fix unhealthy services")
  3767	@click.option("--cleanup", "-c", is_flag=True, help="Clean up orphaned MCP processes")
  3768	@click.option("--watch", "-w", is_flag=True, help="Continuous monitoring mode")
  3769	@click.option(
  3770	    "--interval", "-i", type=int, default=30, help="Watch interval in seconds"
  3771	)
  3772	@click.pass_context
  3773	def health(
  3774	    ctx, detailed: bool, service: Optional[str], fix: bool, cleanup: bool, watch: bool, interval: int
  3775	):
  3776	    """
  3777	    🏥 Comprehensive health check for Dopemux ecosystem
  3778	
  3779	    Monitors Dopemux core, Claude Code, MCP servers, Docker services,
  3780	    system resources, and ADHD feature effectiveness with ADHD-friendly reporting.
  3781	
  3782	    Use --cleanup to find and kill orphaned MCP server processes.
  3783	    """
  3784	    project_path = Path.cwd()
  3785	    health_checker = HealthChecker(project_path, console)
  3786	
  3787	    # Handle cleanup flag first
  3788	    if cleanup:
  3789	        console.logger.info("[blue]🧹 Cleaning up orphaned MCP processes...[/blue]")
  3790	
  3791	        try:
  3792	            # Find orphaned MCP processes
  3793	            result = subprocess.run(
  3794	                ["ps", "aux"],
  3795	                capture_output=True,
  3796	                text=True,
  3797	                check=True
  3798	            )
  3799	
  3800	            orphaned_pids = []
  3801	            mcp_patterns = [
  3802	                'conport-mcp',
  3803	                'serena/v2/mcp_server.py',
  3804	                'src.mcp.server',
  3805	                'dopemux-gpt-researcher'
  3806	            ]
  3807	
  3808	            for line in result.stdout.split('\n'):
  3809	                # Check if it's an MCP process
  3810	                if any(pattern in line for pattern in mcp_patterns):
  3811	                    # Extract PID
  3812	                    parts = line.split()
  3813	                    if len(parts) > 1:
  3814	                        pid = parts[1]
  3815	                        # Check if parent process (Claude Code) is still running
  3816	                        try:
  3817	                            parent_check = subprocess.run(
  3818	                                ["ps", "-o", "ppid=", "-p", pid],
  3819	                                capture_output=True,
  3820	                                text=True
  3821	                            )
  3822	                            ppid = parent_check.stdout.strip()
  3823	                            if ppid:
  3824	                                parent_cmd = subprocess.run(
  3825	                                    ["ps", "-o", "comm=", "-p", ppid],
  3826	                                    capture_output=True,
  3827	                                    text=True
  3828	                                )
  3829	                                # If parent is not Claude Code, it's orphaned
  3830	                                if 'claude' not in parent_cmd.stdout.lower():
  3831	                                    orphaned_pids.append(pid)
  3832	                        except (subprocess.SubprocessError, OSError) as e:
  3833	                            logger.error(f"Process parent check failed: {e}")
  3834	                        except Exception:
  3835	                            logger.error("Unexpected process parent check error", exc_info=True)
  3836	            if orphaned_pids:
  3837	                console.print(f"[yellow]Found {len(orphaned_pids)} orphaned MCP processes[/yellow]")
  3838	
  3839	                if click.confirm("Kill these processes?", default=True):
  3840	                    killed = 0
  3841	                    for pid in orphaned_pids:
  3842	                        try:
  3843	                            os.kill(int(pid), signal.SIGTERM)
  3844	                            killed += 1
  3845	                        except (OSError, ValueError):
  3846	                            pass
  3847	
  3848	                    console.print(f"[green]✅ Cleaned up {killed} orphaned processes[/green]")
  3849	                else:
  3850	                    console.print("[yellow]Cleanup cancelled[/yellow]")
  3851	            else:
  3852	                console.print("[green]✅ No orphaned MCP processes found[/green]")
  3853	
  3854	        except Exception as e:
  3855	            console.print(f"[red]❌ Cleanup failed: {e}[/red]")
  3856	
  3857	        # Exit after cleanup unless combined with other flags
  3858	        if not (detailed or service or fix or watch):
  3859	            return
  3860	
  3861	    if watch:
  3862	        console.print(
  3863	            f"[blue]👁️ Starting continuous health monitoring (interval: {interval}s)[/blue]"
  3864	        )
  3865	        console.print("[dim]Press Ctrl+C to stop[/dim]")
  3866	
  3867	        try:
  3868	            while True:
  3869	                console.clear()
  3870	                console.print(
  3871	                    f"[dim]Last check: {datetime.now().strftime('%H:%M:%S')}[/dim]"
  3872	                )
  3873	
  3874	                results = health_checker.check_all(detailed=detailed)
  3875	                health_checker.display_health_report(results, detailed=detailed)
  3876	
  3877	                time.sleep(interval)
  3878	        except KeyboardInterrupt:
  3879	            console.print("\n[yellow]🛑 Health monitoring stopped[/yellow]")
  3880	            return
  3881	
  3882	    # Single health check
  3883	    with Progress(
  3884	        SpinnerColumn(),
  3885	        TextColumn("[progress.description]{task.description}"),
  3886	        console=console,
  3887	    ) as progress:
  3888	        task = progress.add_task("Running health checks...", total=None)
  3889	
  3890	        if service:
  3891	            # Check specific service
  3892	            checker_method = getattr(health_checker, f"_check_{service}", None)
  3893	            if not checker_method:
  3894	                console.logger.info(f"[red]❌ Unknown service: {service}[/red]")
  3895	                console.print(
  3896	                    f"[yellow]Available services: {', '.join(health_checker.checks.keys())}[/yellow]"
  3897	                )
  3898	                sys.exit(1)
  3899	
  3900	            result = checker_method(detailed=detailed)
  3901	            results = {service: result}
  3902	        else:
  3903	            # Check all services
  3904	            results = health_checker.check_all(detailed=detailed)
  3905	
  3906	        progress.update(task, description="Health checks complete!", completed=True)
  3907	
  3908	    # Display results
  3909	    health_checker.display_health_report(results, detailed=detailed)
  3910	
  3911	    # Fix unhealthy services if requested
  3912	    if fix:
  3913	        console.logger.info("\n[blue]🔧 Attempting to fix unhealthy services...[/blue]")
  3914	
  3915	        with Progress(
  3916	            SpinnerColumn(),
  3917	            TextColumn("[progress.description]{task.description}"),
  3918	            console=console,
  3919	        ) as progress:
  3920	            fix_task = progress.add_task("Fixing services...", total=None)
  3921	
  3922	            restarted = health_checker.restart_unhealthy_services()
  3923	
  3924	            progress.update(
  3925	                fix_task, description="Fix attempts complete!", completed=True
  3926	            )
  3927	
  3928	        if restarted:
  3929	            console.print(
  3930	                f"[green]✅ Restarted services: {', '.join(restarted)}[/green]"
  3931	            )
  3932	            console.logger.info("[blue]💡 Run 'dopemux health' again to verify fixes[/blue]")
  3933	        else:
  3934	            console.logger.info("[yellow]⚠️ No services could be automatically fixed[/yellow]")
  3935	            console.logger.info("[dim]Manual intervention may be required[/dim]")
  3936	
  3937	    # Exit with appropriate code for scripting
  3938	    critical_count = sum(1 for h in results.values() if h.status.value[0] == "critical")
  3939	    if critical_count > 0:
  3940	        sys.exit(1)
  3941

  3943	@autoresponder.command("config")
  3944	@click.option("--enabled/--disabled", help="Enable or disable auto responder")
  3945	@click.option(
  3946	    "--terminal-scope",
  3947	    type=click.Choice(["current", "all", "project"]),
  3948	    help="Terminal monitoring scope",
  3949	)
  3950	@click.option("--delay", type=float, help="Response delay in seconds (0-10)")
  3951	@click.option("--timeout", type=int, help="Auto-stop timeout in minutes")
  3952	@click.option("--whitelist/--no-whitelist", help="Enable/disable tool whitelisting")
  3953	@click.option("--debug/--no-debug", help="Enable/disable debug mode")
  3954	@click.pass_context
  3955	def autoresponder_config(
  3956	    ctx, enabled, terminal_scope, delay, timeout, whitelist, debug
  3957	):
  3958	    """
  3959	    ⚙️ Configure auto responder settings
  3960	
  3961	    Update configuration options for Claude Auto Responder integration.
  3962	    """
  3963	    config_manager = ctx.obj["config_manager"]
  3964	
  3965	    updates = {}
  3966	    if enabled is not None:
  3967	        updates["enabled"] = enabled
  3968	    if terminal_scope:
  3969	        updates["terminal_scope"] = terminal_scope
  3970	    if delay is not None:
  3971	        updates["response_delay"] = delay
  3972	    if timeout:
  3973	        updates["timeout_minutes"] = timeout
  3974	    if whitelist is not None:
  3975	        updates["whitelist_tools"] = whitelist
  3976	    if debug is not None:
  3977	        updates["debug_mode"] = debug
  3978	
  3979	    if not updates:
  3980	        # Show current config
  3981	        current_config = config_manager.get_claude_autoresponder_config()
  3982	
  3983	        table = Table(title="🤖 Auto Responder Configuration")
  3984	        table.add_column("Setting", style="cyan")
  3985	        table.add_column("Value", style="green")
  3986	
  3987	        table.add_row("Enabled", "Yes" if current_config.enabled else "No")
  3988	        table.add_row("Terminal Scope", current_config.terminal_scope)
  3989	        table.add_row("Response Delay", f"{current_config.response_delay}s")
  3990	        table.add_row("Timeout", f"{current_config.timeout_minutes} minutes")
  3991	        table.add_row(
  3992	            "Whitelist Tools", "Yes" if current_config.whitelist_tools else "No"
  3993	        )
  3994	        table.add_row("Debug Mode", "Yes" if current_config.debug_mode else "No")
  3995	
  3996	        console.logger.info(table)
  3997	        return
  3998	
  3999	    # Apply updates
  4000	    try:
  4001	        config_manager.update_claude_autoresponder(**updates)
  4002	        console.logger.info("[green]✅ Configuration updated[/green]")
  4003	
  4004	        # Show what changed
  4005	        for key, value in updates.items():
  4006	            console.logger.info(f"[blue]  {key}: {value}[/blue]")
  4007	
  4008	        # Restart if running
  4009	        project_path = Path.cwd()
  4010	        if (project_path / ".dopemux").exists():
  4011	            from integrations.claude_autoresponder import create_autoresponder_manager
  4012	
  4013	            autoresponder_manager = create_autoresponder_manager(
  4014	                config_manager, project_path
  4015	            )
  4016	            if autoresponder_manager.is_running():
  4017	                console.print(
  4018	                    "[yellow]🔄 Restarting auto responder with new settings...[/yellow]"
  4019	                )
  4020	                autoresponder_manager.restart()
  4021	
  4022	    except ValueError as e:
  4023	        console.logger.error(f"[red]❌ Configuration error: {e}[/red]")
  4024	        sys.exit(1)

  4027	def _get_attention_emoji(state: Optional[str]) -> str:
  4028	    """Get emoji for attention state."""
  4029	    emoji_map = {
  4030	        "focused": "🎯",
  4031	        "scattered": "🌪️",
  4032	        "hyperfocus": "🔥",
  4033	        "normal": "😊",
  4034	        "distracted": "😵‍💫",
  4035	    }
  4036	    return emoji_map.get(state, "❓")

  4039	def _configure_openrouter_litellm():
  4040	    """Configure environment for OpenRouter via LiteLLM"""
  4041	    # Set up OpenRouter models for LiteLLM
  4042	    openrouter_models = [
  4043	        "openrouter-xai-grok-code-fast",
  4044	        "openrouter-openai-gpt-5",
  4045	        "openrouter-openai-gpt-5-mini",
  4046	        "openrouter-openai-gpt-5-codex",
  4047	        "openrouter-google-gemini-2-flash",
  4048	        "openrouter-meta-llama-3.1-405b",
  4049	    ]
  4050	    
  4051	    # Update environment
  4052	    os.environ["CLAUDE_CODE_ROUTER_PROVIDER"] = "litellm"
  4053	    os.environ["CLAUDE_CODE_ROUTER_UPSTREAM_KEY_VAR"] = "DOPEMUX_LITELLM_MASTER_KEY"
  4054	    os.environ["CLAUDE_CODE_ROUTER_MODELS"] = ",".join(openrouter_models)
  4055	    
  4056	    # Ensure Zen MCP uses LiteLLM
  4057	    os.environ["ZEN_DEFAULT_MODEL"] = "litellm/openrouter-openai-gpt-5"
  4058	    os.environ["ZEN_FALLBACK_MODELS"] = "litellm/openrouter-xai-grok-code-fast,litellm/openrouter-google-gemini-2-flash"
  4059	    
  4060	    # Set up LiteLLM proxy URL
  4061	    os.environ["LITELLM_PROXY_URL"] = "http://localhost:4000"
  4062	    
  4063	    # Configure Claude Code to use LiteLLM

  4065	    os.environ["CLAUDE_CODE_LLM_BASE_URL"] = "http://localhost:4000"
  4066	    os.environ["CLAUDE_CODE_LLM_API_KEY"] = os.getenv("DOPEMUX_LITELLM_MASTER_KEY", "")
  4067	    
  4068	    console.logger.info("[green]✅ OpenRouter via LiteLLM configuration applied[/green]")
