  4073	def _start_mcp_servers_with_progress(project_path: Path, instance_env: Optional[dict] = None):
  4074	    """
  4075	    Start MCP servers with real-time output streaming and health check waiting.
  4076	
  4077	    CRITICAL: Passes instance environment variables to MCP servers for workspace isolation.
  4078	    Without this, all instances share the same workspace = broken ADHD context preservation!
  4079	
  4080	    Args:
  4081	        project_path: Project root path
  4082	        instance_env: Instance-specific environment variables (DOPEMUX_WORKSPACE_ID, etc.)
  4083	
  4084	    ADHD-optimized:
  4085	    - Real-time visual feedback reduces anxiety
  4086	    - Clear status updates maintain engagement
  4087	    - Health check waiting ensures everything is ready
  4088	    """
  4089	    if os.getenv("DOPEMUX_SKIP_MCP_START", "0").lower() in {"1", "true", "yes"}:
  4090	        console.logger.info("[yellow]⏭️ Skipping MCP server startup (DOPEMUX_SKIP_MCP_START)[/yellow]")
  4091	        return
  4092	
  4093	    import requests
  4094	
  4095	    mcp_dir = project_path / "docker" / "mcp-servers"
  4096	
  4097	    # CRITICAL FIX: Merge instance env with current environment
  4098	    # This ensures MCP servers get DOPEMUX_WORKSPACE_ID and other instance vars
  4099	    env_for_subprocess = os.environ.copy()
  4100	    if instance_env:
  4101	        env_for_subprocess.update(instance_env)
  4102	
  4103	    # Critical servers to health check
  4104	    critical_servers = [
  4105	        ("Context7", "http://localhost:3002/health"),
  4106	        ("Zen", "http://localhost:3003/health"),
  4107	        ("LiteLLM", "http://localhost:4000/health/readiness"),
  4108	    ]
  4109	
  4110	    console.logger.info("\n[bold blue]🔌 Starting MCP Servers[/bold blue]")
  4111	    console.logger.info("[dim]This may take 30-60 seconds for first-time setup...[/dim]\n")
  4112	
  4113	    # Start docker-compose with real-time output
  4114	    status_text = Text()
  4115	    status_text.append("🚀 ", style="bold blue")
  4116	    status_text.append("Launching containers...")
  4117	
  4118	    startup_successful = False
  4119	    output_lines = []
  4120	    
  4121	    try:
  4122	        with Live(status_text, console=console, refresh_per_second=4) as live:
  4123	            # Start the containers with instance environment
  4124	            # CRITICAL FIX: Pass env_for_subprocess so docker-compose gets DOPEMUX_WORKSPACE_ID
  4125	            process = subprocess.Popen(
  4126	                ["bash", "-c", f"cd {mcp_dir} && ./start-all-mcp-servers.sh"],
  4127	                stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
  4128	                stderr=subprocess.STDOUT,
  4129	                text=True,
  4130	                bufsize=1,
  4131	                env=env_for_subprocess  # ← THE FIX! Passes instance vars to MCP servers
  4132	            )
  4133	
  4134	            # Stream output line by line
  4135	            for line in process.stdout:
  4136	                line = line.rstrip()
  4137	                if line:
  4138	                    # Update status with last meaningful line
  4139	                    if "Starting" in line:
  4140	                        status_text = Text()
  4141	                        status_text.append("🔨 ", style="bold blue")
  4142	                        status_text.append(line)
  4143	                        live.update(status_text)
  4144	                    elif "✅" in line or "Healthy" in line:
  4145	                        status_text = Text()
  4146	                        status_text.append("✅ ", style="bold green")
  4147	                        status_text.append(line)
  4148	                        live.update(status_text)
  4149	                    elif "⚡" in line:
  4150	                        status_text = Text()
  4151	                        status_text.append("⚡ ", style="bold yellow")
  4152	                        status_text.append(line)
  4153	                        live.update(status_text)
  4154	
  4155	                    output_lines.append(line)
  4156	
  4157	            process.wait()
  4158	
  4159	            if process.returncode != 0:
  4160	                console.logger.error("\n[red]❌ MCP server startup failed[/red]")
  4161	                console.logger.info("[dim]Last 10 lines of output:[/dim]")
  4162	                for line in output_lines[-10:]:
  4163	                    console.logger.info(f"[dim]{line}[/dim]")
  4164	                raise CalledProcessError(process.returncode, process.args)
  4165	        
  4166	        # Mark startup as successful only after the first Live context has fully exited
  4167	        startup_successful = True
  4168	
  4169	    except CalledProcessError as e:
  4170	        console.logger.error("[yellow]⚠️  Failed to start MCP servers (continuing with reduced functionality)[/yellow]")
  4171	        console.logger.info("[dim]   Tip: Run 'dopemux start --no-mcp' to skip this step[/dim]")
  4172	        return  # Exit early to avoid starting the second Live context
  4173	    except Exception as e:
  4174	        console.logger.error(f"[yellow]⚠️  Error during MCP startup: {e}[/yellow]")
  4175	        console.logger.info("[dim]   Continuing with reduced functionality...[/dim]")
  4176	        return  # Exit early to avoid starting the second Live context
  4177	
  4178	    # Only proceed with health checks if startup was successful
  4179	    if startup_successful:
  4180	        # Wait for health checks
  4181	        console.logger.info("\n[bold blue]🏥 Waiting for services to become healthy...[/bold blue]")
  4182	
  4183	        max_wait = 45  # seconds
  4184	        start_time = time.time()
  4185	        all_healthy = False
  4186	
  4187	        health_status = {name: False for name, _ in critical_servers}
  4188	
  4189	        try:
  4190	            with Live(console=console, refresh_per_second=2) as live:
  4191	                while time.time() - start_time < max_wait:
  4192	                    status_text = Text()
  4193	                    all_healthy = True
  4194	
  4195	                    for name, url in critical_servers:
  4196	                        is_healthy = False
  4197	                        try:
  4198	                            response = requests.get(url, timeout=2)
  4199	                            is_healthy = response.status_code == 200
  4200	                        except requests.RequestException:
  4201	                            is_healthy = False
  4202	
  4203	                        health_status[name] = is_healthy
  4204	                        if is_healthy:
  4205	                            status_text.append("✅ ", style="bold green")
  4206	                        else:
  4207	                            status_text.append("⏳ ", style="bold yellow")
  4208	                            all_healthy = False
  4209	                        status_text.append(f"{name}\n")
  4210	
  4211	                    # Add elapsed time
  4212	                    elapsed = int(time.time() - start_time)
  4213	                    status_text.append(f"\n[dim]⏱️  {elapsed}s / {max_wait}s[/dim]")
  4214	
  4215	                    live.update(Panel(status_text, title="[bold]Health Check Status[/bold]", border_style="blue"))
  4216	
  4217	                    if all_healthy:
  4218	                        break
  4219	
  4220	                    time.sleep(2)
  4221	
  4222	            if all_healthy:
  4223	                console.logger.info("\n[bold green]✅ All MCP servers are healthy and ready![/bold green]\n")
  4224	            else:
  4225	                # Show which services failed
  4226	                console.logger.info("\n[yellow]⚠️  Some services are not healthy (continuing anyway):[/yellow]")
  4227	                for name, is_healthy in health_status.items():
  4228	                    if not is_healthy:
  4229	                        console.logger.info(f"  [red]❌ {name}[/red]")
  4230	                    else:
  4231	                        console.logger.info(f"  [green]✅ {name}[/green]")
  4232	                console.logger.info("[dim]Tip: Check docker logs with: docker-compose -f docker/mcp-servers/docker-compose.yml logs[/dim]\n")
  4233	        
  4234	        except Exception as e:
  4235	            console.logger.error(f"[yellow]⚠️  Error during health checks: {e}[/yellow]")
  4236	            console.logger.info("[dim]   Continuing anyway...[/dim]")
  4237

  4239	def _activate_dangerous_mode():
  4240	    """
  4241	    Activate dangerous mode with proper security safeguards.
  4242	
  4243	    This temporarily overrides the default safe mode settings for the current
  4244	    session only. Changes are not persisted to the .env file.
  4245	
  4246	    Security Features:
  4247	    - Time-limited session (1 hour max)
  4248	    - Explicit user confirmation required
  4249	    - Clear warnings about risks
  4250	    - Environment isolation
  4251	    """
  4252	    # Check if already in dangerous mode
  4253	    if os.getenv("DOPEMUX_DANGEROUS_MODE") == "true":
  4254	        expires_str = os.getenv("DOPEMUX_DANGEROUS_EXPIRES", "0")
  4255	        expires_timestamp = float(expires_str) if expires_str.isdigit() else 0
  4256	
  4257	        if time.time() < expires_timestamp:
  4258	            console.logger.info("[yellow]⚠️  Dangerous mode already active[/yellow]")
  4259	            remaining_minutes = int((expires_timestamp - time.time()) / 60)
  4260	            console.logger.info(f"[dim]Expires in {remaining_minutes} minutes[/dim]")
  4261	            return
  4262	        else:
  4263	            # Expired, clear old settings
  4264	            _deactivate_dangerous_mode()
  4265	
  4266	    # Show serious warning
  4267	    console.print(Panel(
  4268	        "[red bold]⚠️  DANGER: This will disable ALL security restrictions![/red bold]\n\n"
  4269	        "[yellow]This mode will:[/yellow]\n"
  4270	        "• Skip all permission checks\n"
  4271	        "• Disable role enforcement\n"
  4272	        "• Bypass budget limits\n"
  4273	        "• Allow unrestricted tool access\n\n"
  4274	        "[red]Use ONLY in isolated, trusted environments![/red]\n"
  4275	        "[yellow]Session will expire automatically in 1 hour.[/yellow]",
  4276	        title="🚨 Security Warning",
  4277	        border_style="red"
  4278	    ))
  4279	
  4280	    # Require explicit confirmation
  4281	    if not click.confirm("\nDo you understand the risks and want to proceed?", default=False):
  4282	        console.logger.info("[green]Dangerous mode cancelled. Staying in safe mode.[/green]")
  4283	        return
  4284	
  4285	    if not click.confirm("Are you in an isolated, trusted environment?", default=False):
  4286	        console.logger.info("[green]Dangerous mode cancelled for security.[/green]")
  4287	        return
  4288	
  4289	    # Set time-limited dangerous mode (1 hour)
  4290	    expiry_time = time.time() + 3600  # 1 hour
  4291	
  4292	    os.environ["DOPEMUX_DANGEROUS_MODE"] = "true"
  4293	    os.environ["DOPEMUX_DANGEROUS_EXPIRES"] = str(expiry_time)
  4294	    os.environ["DOPEMUX_DANGEROUS_PID"] = str(os.getpid())  # Track process
  4295	
  4296	    # Set security bypass flags
  4297	    os.environ["HOOKS_ENABLE_ADAPTIVE_SECURITY"] = "0"
  4298	    os.environ["CLAUDE_CODE_SKIP_PERMISSIONS"] = "true"
  4299	    os.environ["METAMCP_ROLE_ENFORCEMENT"] = "false"
  4300	    os.environ["METAMCP_APPROVAL_REQUIRED"] = "false"
  4301	    os.environ["METAMCP_BUDGET_ENFORCEMENT"] = "false"
  4302	
  4303	    # Traditional dangerous flags for compatibility
  4304	    os.environ["CLAUDE_DANGEROUS"] = "true"
  4305	    os.environ["SKIP_PERMISSIONS"] = "true"
  4306	
  4307	    # Log for audit trail (but not sensitive info)
  4308	    expiry_str = datetime.fromtimestamp(expiry_time).strftime("%H:%M:%S")
  4309	    console.logger.info(f"[red bold]⚠️  DANGEROUS MODE ACTIVE until {expiry_str}[/red bold]")
  4310	
  4311	
  4312	def _deactivate_dangerous_mode():
  4313	    """Deactivate dangerous mode and clean up environment."""
  4314	    dangerous_vars = [
  4315	        "DOPEMUX_DANGEROUS_MODE",
  4316	        "DOPEMUX_DANGEROUS_EXPIRES",
  4317	        "DOPEMUX_DANGEROUS_PID",
  4318	        "HOOKS_ENABLE_ADAPTIVE_SECURITY",
  4319	        "CLAUDE_CODE_SKIP_PERMISSIONS",
  4320	        "METAMCP_ROLE_ENFORCEMENT",
  4321	        "METAMCP_APPROVAL_REQUIRED",
  4322	        "METAMCP_BUDGET_ENFORCEMENT",
  4323	        "CLAUDE_DANGEROUS",
  4324	        "SKIP_PERMISSIONS"
  4325	    ]
  4326	
  4327	    for var in dangerous_vars:
  4328	        os.environ.pop(var, None)
  4329	
  4330	    console.logger.info("[green]✅ Dangerous mode deactivated[/green]")
  4331	
  4332	
  4333	def _check_dangerous_mode_expiry():
  4334	    """Check if dangerous mode has expired and clean up if needed."""
  4335	    if os.getenv("DOPEMUX_DANGEROUS_MODE") == "true":
  4336	        expires_str = os.getenv("DOPEMUX_DANGEROUS_EXPIRES", "0")
  4337	        expires_timestamp = float(expires_str) if expires_str.isdigit() else 0
  4338	
  4339	        if time.time() >= expires_timestamp:
  4340	            console.logger.info("[yellow]⏰ Dangerous mode expired, returning to safe mode[/yellow]")
  4341	            _deactivate_dangerous_mode()
  4342	            return True
  4343	    return False

  4345	
  4346	@cli.command("backup")
  4347	@click.option("--dest", help="Destination directory for tar backups (defaults to docker/mcp-servers/backups/volumes_<timestamp>)")
  4348	@click.option("--pattern", help="Regex to filter volume names (default: ^(mcp_|dopemux_))")
  4349	@click.option("--no-pull", is_flag=True, help="Do not pull alpine image if missing")
  4350	@click.option("--schedule", type=click.Choice(["daily", "weekly"]), help="Print a cron entry to run backups on a schedule")
  4351	@click.option("--apply", is_flag=True, help="Attempt to install the cron entry into your crontab")
  4352	@click.pass_context
  4353	def backup(ctx, dest: Optional[str], pattern: Optional[str], no_pull: bool, schedule: Optional[str], apply: bool):
  4354	    """
  4355	    📦 Back up all Docker named volumes used by Dopemux (mcp_*/dopemux_*).
  4356	
  4357	    Creates .tgz archives and a SHA256SUMS.txt manifest in the destination.
  4358	    Use --schedule to print or install a cron job for daily/weekly backups.
  4359	    """
  4360	    from .workspace_utils import get_workspace_root
  4361	    import hashlib, re
  4362	
  4363	    # Scheduling path only
  4364	    if schedule:
  4365	        _print_or_apply_cron(schedule, apply)
  4366	        return
  4367	
  4368	    with mobile_task_notification(
  4369	        ctx,
  4370	        "Docker volume backup",
  4371	        success_message="✅ Docker volume backup complete",
  4372	        failure_message="❌ Docker volume backup failed",
  4373	    ):
  4374	        _run_volume_backup(dest, pattern, no_pull, get_workspace_root)
  4375	
  4376	
  4377	def _run_volume_backup(dest: Optional[str], pattern: Optional[str], no_pull: bool, get_workspace_root):
  4378	    import hashlib
  4379	    import re
  4380	
  4381	    workspace = get_workspace_root()
  4382	    ts = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d_%H%M%S")
  4383	    default_dest = workspace / "docker" / "mcp-servers" / "backups" / f"volumes_{ts}"
  4384	    dest_path = Path(dest).expanduser().resolve() if dest else default_dest
  4385	    dest_path.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
  4386	
  4387	    vol_pattern = re.compile(pattern or r"^(mcp_|dopemux_)")
  4388	
  4389	    try:
  4390	        result = subprocess.run(["docker", "volume", "ls", "--format", "{{.Name}}"], capture_output=True, text=True, check=True)
  4391	    except Exception as e:
  4392	        console.logger.info(f"[red]❌ Docker not available: {e}[/red]")
  4393	        sys.exit(1)
  4394	
  4395	    volumes = [v.strip() for v in result.stdout.splitlines() if v.strip() and vol_pattern.search(v.strip())]
  4396	    if not volumes:
  4397	        console.logger.info("[yellow]No matching volumes found[/yellow]")
  4398	        return
  4399	
  4400	    console.logger.info(f"[blue]== Backing up {len(volumes)} volumes to {dest_path} ==[/blue]")
  4401	
  4402	    if not no_pull:
  4403	        try:
  4404	            subprocess.run(["docker", "image", "inspect", "alpine:latest"], capture_output=True, text=True, check=True)
  4405	        except subprocess.CalledProcessError:
  4406	            console.logger.info("[dim]Pulling alpine:latest ...[/dim]")
  4407	            subprocess.run(["docker", "pull", "alpine:latest"], check=False)
  4408	
  4409	    ok = 0
  4410	    fail = 0
  4411	    for vol in volumes:
  4412	        console.logger.info(f"Backing up [cyan]{vol}[/cyan] ...")
  4413	        cmd = [
  4414	            "docker", "run", "--rm",
  4415	            "-v", f"{vol}:/data:ro",
  4416	            "-v", f"{str(dest_path)}:/backup",
  4417	            "alpine", "sh", "-lc",
  4418	            f"cd /data 2>/dev/null || mkdir -p /data; tar czf '/backup/{vol}.tgz' -C /data ."
  4419	        ]
  4420	        try:
  4421	            subprocess.run(cmd, check=True)
  4422	            console.logger.info(f"[green]✓ {vol}[/green] → {dest_path / (vol + '.tgz')}")
  4423	            ok += 1
  4424	        except subprocess.CalledProcessError:
  4425	            console.logger.error(f"[red]✗ Failed to back up {vol}[/red]")
  4426	            fail += 1
  4427	
  4428	    try:
  4429	        sums_path = dest_path / "SHA256SUMS.txt"
  4430	        with sums_path.open("w") as f:
  4431	            for tgz in sorted(dest_path.glob("*.tgz")):
  4432	                h = hashlib.sha256()
  4433	                with tgz.open("rb") as tf:
  4434	                    for chunk in iter(lambda: tf.read(1024 * 1024), b""):
  4435	                        h.update(chunk)
  4436	                f.write(f"{h.hexdigest()}  {tgz.name}\n")
  4437	        console.logger.info(f"[green]Manifest written:[/green] {sums_path}")
  4438	    except Exception as e:
  4439	        console.logger.info(f"[yellow]⚠️  Could not write checksum manifest: {e}[/yellow]")
  4440	
  4441	    console.logger.error(f"\n[bold]Summary[/bold]: Backed up {ok} volumes, {fail} failed")
  4442	
  4443	
  4444	def _print_or_apply_cron(frequency: str, apply: bool) -> None:
  4445	    """Print or install a cron job to run 'dopemux backup' on the desired schedule."""
  4446	    # Defaults: run at 02:30 local time
  4447	    cron_time = "30 2 * * *" if frequency == "daily" else "30 2 * * 1"
  4448	
  4449	    backup_cmd = "dopemux backup"
  4450	    cron_entry = (
  4451	        f"# dopemux-backup ({frequency})\n"
  4452	        f"{cron_time} cd $HOME/code/dopemux-mvp && {backup_cmd} >> $HOME/.dopemux/backup.log 2>&1\n"
  4453	    )
  4454	
  4455	    if not apply:
  4456	        console.logger.info("\n[bold]Cron suggestion[/bold] (add via 'crontab -e'):\n")
  4457	        console.logger.info(cron_entry)
  4458	        console.logger.info("\n[dim]Tip: Adjust path and time as needed.[/dim]")
  4459	        return
  4460	
  4461	    try:
  4462	        current = subprocess.run(["crontab", "-l"], capture_output=True, text=True)
  4463	        content = current.stdout if current.returncode == 0 else ""
  4464	        if "# dopemux-backup" in content:
  4465	            console.logger.info("[yellow]⚠️  A dopemux-backup entry already exists in your crontab[/yellow]")
  4466	            return
  4467	        new_content = content + ("\n" if content and not content.endswith("\n") else "") + cron_entry
  4468	        p = subprocess.run(["crontab", "-"], input=new_content, text=True)
  4469	        if p.returncode == 0:
  4470	            console.logger.info("[green]✅ Installed dopemux backup cron job[/green]")
  4471	        else:
  4472	            console.logger.info("[yellow]⚠️  Could not install cron job. Printing entry instead:[/yellow]")
  4473	            console.logger.info(cron_entry)
  4474	    except Exception as e:
  4475	        console.logger.error(f"[yellow]⚠️  Failed to install cron job: {e}[/yellow]")
  4476	        console.logger.info("\nAdd this entry manually via 'crontab -e':\n")
  4477	        console.logger.info(cron_entry)
  4478	
  4479	
  4480	@cli.command("extract-chatlog")
  4481	@click.argument("directory", default=".")
  4482	@click.option("--output", "-o", help="Output directory for extraction results")
  4483	@click.option("--confidence", "-c", type=float, default=0.5, help="Minimum confidence threshold (0.0-1.0)")
  4484	@click.option("--batch-size", "-b", type=int, default=10, help="Number of files to process per batch")
  4485	@click.option("--max-workers", "-w", type=int, default=4, help="Maximum parallel workers")
  4486	@click.option("--archive", "-a", help="Archive directory for processed files")
  4487	@click.option("--workspace-id", help="ConPort workspace ID for persistence")
  4488	@click.pass_context
  4489	def extract_chatlog(
  4490	    ctx,
  4491	    directory: str,
  4492	    output: Optional[str],
  4493	    confidence: float,
  4494	    batch_size: int,
  4495	    max_workers: int,
  4496	    archive: Optional[str],
  4497	    workspace_id: Optional[str]
  4498	):
  4499	    """
  4500	    📄 Extract structured data from chatlog conversations (Basic Mode)
  4501	
  4502	    Process chatlog files using core extractors (decisions, features, research)
  4503	    with adaptive document synthesis. Includes batch processing with phase
  4504	    synchronization and automatic archiving of processed files.
  4505	
  4506	    Basic extractors:
  4507	    • Decision extraction (conclusions, agreements, next steps)
  4508	    • Feature extraction (requirements, user stories, acceptance criteria)
  4509	    • Research extraction (findings, references, methodologies)
  4510	    """
  4511	    with mobile_task_notification(
  4512	        ctx,
  4513	        "Chatlog extraction",
  4514	        success_message="✅ Chatlog extraction complete",
  4515	        failure_message="❌ Chatlog extraction failed",
  4516	    ):
  4517	        _run_extract_chatlog(
  4518	            ctx,
  4519	            directory,
  4520	            output,
  4521	            confidence,
  4522	            batch_size,
  4523	            max_workers,
  4524	            archive,
  4525	            workspace_id,
  4526	        )
  4527

  4529	def _run_extract_chatlog(
  4530	    ctx,
  4531	    directory: str,
  4532	    output: Optional[str],
  4533	    confidence: float,
  4534	    batch_size: int,
  4535	    max_workers: int,
  4536	    archive: Optional[str],
  4537	    workspace_id: Optional[str],
  4538	) -> None:
  4539	    import sys
  4540	    from pathlib import Path
  4541	
  4542	    backend_path = Path(__file__).parent.parent.parent / "services" / "dopemux-gpt-researcher" / "backend"
  4543	    sys.path.insert(0, str(backend_path))
  4544	
  4545	    try:
  4546	        from extraction_pipeline import ExtractionPipeline, PipelineConfig
  4547	    except ImportError as e:
  4548	        console.logger.info(f"[red]❌ Could not import extraction pipeline: {e}[/red]")
  4549	        console.logger.info("[yellow]💡 Make sure you're in the dopemux-mvp directory[/yellow]")
  4550	        sys.exit(1)
  4551	
  4552	    source_path = Path(directory).resolve()
  4553	    if not source_path.exists():
  4554	        console.logger.info(f"[red]❌ Directory does not exist: {source_path}[/red]")
  4555	        sys.exit(1)
  4556	
  4557	    if output:
  4558	        output_path = Path(output).resolve()
  4559	    else:
  4560	        output_path = source_path / ".dopemux" / "extraction"
  4561	
  4562	    archive_path = Path(archive).resolve() if archive else None
  4563	
  4564	    if not workspace_id:
  4565	        workspace_id = str(source_path)
  4566	
  4567	    config = PipelineConfig(
  4568	        source_directory=source_path,
  4569	        output_directory=output_path,
  4570	        archive_directory=archive_path,
  4571	        batch_size=batch_size,
  4572	        max_workers=max_workers,
  4573	        confidence_threshold=confidence,
  4574	        include_basic_extractors=True,
  4575	        include_pro_extractors=False,
  4576	        enable_synthesis=True,
  4577	        max_documents=4,

  4579	        persist_to_conport=True,
  4580	        workspace_id=workspace_id,
  4581	    )

  4592	    ) as progress:

  4597

  4599	            files = pipeline.discover_files()
  4600

  4602	                progress.update(task, description="No files found to process", completed=True)
  4603	                console.logger.info("[yellow]⚠️ No unprocessed chatlog files found[/yellow]")
  4604	                return
  4605	
  4606	            progress.update(task, description=f"Processing {len(files)} files...")
  4607	            result = pipeline.run_extraction()
  4608

  4610	                progress.update(task, description="Extraction completed successfully! ✅", completed=True)
  4611

  4614	                    Panel(

  4618	                        f"• Fields extracted: {stats['total_fields']}\n"
  4619	                        f"• High confidence fields: {stats['high_confidence_fields']}\n"
  4620	                        f"• Documents generated: {stats['documents_generated']}\n"
  4621	                        f"• Processing time: {stats['processing_time']:.2f}s\n\n"
  4622	                        f"📊 Field Types:\n"
  4623	                        + "\n".join(
  4624	                            [f"• {field_type}: {count}" for field_type, count in stats['fields_by_type'].items()]

  4627	                        border_style="green",
  4628	                    )

  4633

  4635	                progress.update(task, description="Extraction failed ❌", completed=True)
  4636	                console.logger.error(f"[red]❌ Extraction failed[/red]")
  4637	                if result.get('errors'):
  4638	                    console.logger.error(f"[red]Errors: {len(result['errors'])}[/red]")
  4639	                    for error in result['errors'][:3]:
  4640	                        console.logger.error(f"[red]  • {error}[/red]")
  4641	                sys.exit(1)
  4642	
  4643	        except Exception as e:
  4644	            progress.update(task, description="Error occurred", completed=True)
  4645	            console.logger.error(f"[red]❌ Extraction pipeline failed: {e}[/red]")
  4646	            if ctx.obj.get("verbose"):
  4647	                import traceback
  4648	                traceback.print_exc()
  4649	            sys.exit(1)

  4652	@cli.command()

  4654	@click.option("--output", "-o", help="Output directory for extraction results")

  4660	@click.option("--max-documents", "-d", type=int, default=8, help="Maximum documents to generate")
  4661	@click.pass_context
  4662	def extractPro(
  4663	    ctx,
  4664	    directory: str,
  4665	    output: Optional[str],
  4666	    confidence: float,
  4667	    batch_size: int,
  4668	    max_workers: int,
  4669	    archive: Optional[str],
  4670	    workspace_id: Optional[str],
  4671	    max_documents: int
  4672	):
  4673	    """
  4674	    🔬 Extract comprehensive data from chatlog conversations (Pro Mode)
  4675	
  4676	    Process chatlog files using ALL extractors with advanced analysis capabilities.
  4677	    Includes full synthesis suite, knowledge graph construction, and comprehensive
  4678	    reporting with pre-commit review integration.
  4679	
  4680	    Pro extractors include ALL basic extractors PLUS:
  4681	    • Constraint extraction (technical/business limitations, dependencies)
  4682	    • Stakeholder extraction (roles, responsibilities, decision makers)
  4683	    • Risk extraction (threats, mitigations, impact assessments)
  4684	    • Security extraction (auth requirements, compliance, vulnerabilities)
  4685	
  4686	    Pro features:
  4687	    • Lower confidence threshold for broader coverage
  4688	    • More parallel processing power
  4689	    • Advanced document synthesis (8+ document types)
  4690	    • Knowledge graph with relationship mapping
  4691	    • Comprehensive quality metrics and reporting
  4692	    """
  4693	    with mobile_task_notification(
  4694	        ctx,
  4695	        "Pro chatlog extraction",
  4696	        success_message="✅ Pro chatlog extraction complete",
  4697	        failure_message="❌ Pro chatlog extraction failed",
  4698	    ):
  4699	        _run_extract_pro(
  4700	            ctx,
  4701	            directory,
  4702	            output,
  4703	            confidence,
  4704	            batch_size,
  4705	            max_workers,
  4706	            archive,
  4707	            workspace_id,
  4708	            max_documents,
  4709	        )

  4713	    ctx,

  4717	    batch_size: int,
  4718	    max_workers: int,
  4719	    archive: Optional[str],
  4720	    workspace_id: Optional[str],
  4721	    max_documents: int,
  4722	) -> None:
  4723	    import sys
  4724	    from pathlib import Path
  4725	
  4726	    # Add the gpt-researcher backend to the path
  4727	    backend_path = Path(__file__).parent.parent.parent / "services" / "dopemux-gpt-researcher" / "backend"
  4728	    sys.path.insert(0, str(backend_path))
  4729	
  4730	    try:
  4731	        from extraction_pipeline import ExtractionPipeline, PipelineConfig
  4732	    except ImportError as e:
  4733	        console.logger.info(f"[red]❌ Could not import extraction pipeline: {e}[/red]")
  4734	        console.logger.info("[yellow]💡 Make sure you're in the dopemux-mvp directory[/yellow]")
  4735	        sys.exit(1)
  4736	
  4737	    source_path = Path(directory).resolve()
  4738	    if not source_path.exists():
  4739	        console.logger.info(f"[red]❌ Directory does not exist: {source_path}[/red]")
  4740	        sys.exit(1)
  4741	
  4742	    # Set output directory
  4743	    if output:
  4744	        output_path = Path(output).resolve()
  4745	    else:
  4746	        output_path = source_path / ".dopemux" / "extraction-pro"
  4747	
  4748	    # Set archive directory
  4749	    archive_path = None
  4750	    if archive:
  4751	        archive_path = Path(archive).resolve()
  4752	
  4753	    # Set workspace ID for ConPort
  4754	    if not workspace_id:
  4755	        workspace_id = str(source_path)
  4756

  4758	    config = PipelineConfig(
  4759	        source_directory=source_path,
  4760	        output_directory=output_path,
  4761	        archive_directory=archive_path,
  4762	        batch_size=batch_size,
  4763	        max_workers=max_workers,
  4764	        confidence_threshold=confidence,
  4765	        include_basic_extractors=True,
  4766	        include_pro_extractors=True,  # Pro mode includes ALL extractors
  4767	        enable_synthesis=True,
  4768	        max_documents=max_documents,
  4769	        verbose=ctx.obj.get("verbose", False),
  4770	        persist_to_conport=True,
  4771	        workspace_id=workspace_id
  4772	    )
  4773	
  4774	    console.logger.info("[blue]🔬 Starting Pro Chatlog Extraction Pipeline[/blue]")
  4775	    console.logger.info(f"[blue]📁 Source: {source_path}[/blue]")
  4776	    console.logger.info(f"[blue]📤 Output: {output_path}[/blue]")
  4777	    console.logger.info(f"[blue]🎯 Extractors: All 7 (Decision, Feature, Research, Constraint, Stakeholder, Risk, Security)[/blue]")
  4778	
  4779	    with Progress(
  4780	        SpinnerColumn(),
  4781	        TextColumn("[progress.description]{task.description}"),
  4782	        console=console,
  4783	    ) as progress:
  4784	        task = progress.add_task("Initializing Pro extraction pipeline...", total=None)
  4785	
  4786	        try:
  4787	            # Create and run pipeline
  4788	            pipeline = ExtractionPipeline(config)
  4789	
  4790	            progress.update(task, description="Discovering files...")
  4791	            files = pipeline.discover_files()
  4792	
  4793	            if not files:
  4794	                progress.update(task, description="No files found to process", completed=True)
  4795	                console.logger.info("[yellow]⚠️ No unprocessed chatlog files found[/yellow]")
  4796	                return
  4797

  4799	            result = pipeline.run_extraction()
  4800	
  4801	            if result['success']:
  4802	                progress.update(task, description="Pro extraction completed successfully! ✅", completed=True)
  4803

  4814	                        f"📊 Field Types:\n" +
  4815	                        "\n".join([f"• {field_type}: {count}"
  4816	                                 for field_type, count in stats['fields_by_type'].items()]) +
  4817	                        f"\n\n⏱️ Phase Times:\n" +
  4818	                        "\n".join([f"• {phase}: {time:.2f}s"
  4819	                                 for phase, time in stats['phase_times'].items()]),
  4820	                        title="🚀 Pro Extraction Complete",

  4823	                )

  4848	@cli.group()
  4849	def update():
  4850	    """🔄 Update and upgrade dopemux system components."""
  4851	    pass
  4852	
  4853	
  4854	@update.command()
  4855	@click.option(
  4856	    "--check",
  4857	    is_flag=True,
  4858	    help="Check for updates without applying them (dry run)"
  4859	)
  4860	@click.option(
  4861	    "--minimal",
  4862	    is_flag=True,
  4863	    help="Skip Docker rebuilds if possible (faster update)"
  4864	)
  4865	@click.option(
  4866	    "--skip-backups",
  4867	    is_flag=True,
  4868	    help="Skip backup creation (not recommended)"
  4869	)
  4870	@click.option(
  4871	    "--skip-docker",
  4872	    is_flag=True,
  4873	    help="Skip Docker image updates"
  4874	)
  4875	@click.option(
  4876	    "--timeout",
  4877	    type=int,
  4878	    default=30,
  4879	    help="Timeout in minutes for update operations"
  4880	)
  4881	@click.pass_context
  4882	def run(ctx, check: bool, minimal: bool, skip_backups: bool, skip_docker: bool, timeout: int):
  4883	    """
  4884	    🚀 Run comprehensive system update
  4885	
  4886	    Updates all dopemux components including:
  4887	    - Git repository (with local change preservation)
  4888	    - Docker containers and images
  4889	    - Python and Node.js dependencies
  4890	    - Database migrations
  4891	    - Configuration updates
  4892	
  4893	    Includes automatic backup, rollback capability, and ADHD-friendly progress tracking.
  4894	    """
  4895	    import asyncio
  4896	    from .update import UpdateManager, UpdateConfig
  4897	
  4898	    try:
  4899	        # Configure update
  4900	        config = UpdateConfig(
  4901	            dry_run=check,
  4902	            minimal=minimal,
  4903	            skip_backups=skip_backups,
  4904	            skip_docker=skip_docker,
  4905	            timeout_minutes=timeout
  4906	        )
  4907	
  4908	        # Create update manager
  4909	        manager = UpdateManager(config=config, project_root=Path.cwd())
  4910	
  4911	        if check:
  4912	            console.logger.info("[cyan]🔍 Checking for available updates...[/cyan]")
  4913	            # Run dry run
  4914	            plan = asyncio.run(manager.dry_run())
  4915	
  4916	            # Display update plan
  4917	            _show_update_plan(plan)
  4918	
  4919	        else:
  4920	            # Run actual update
  4921	            console.logger.info("[cyan]🚀 Starting dopemux update...[/cyan]")
  4922	            result = asyncio.run(manager.run_update())
  4923	
  4924	            # Show result
  4925	            if result.value == "success":
  4926	                console.logger.info("[green]✅ Update completed successfully![/green]")
  4927	            elif result.value == "rolled_back":
  4928	                console.logger.error("[yellow]🔄 Update failed but rollback successful[/yellow]")
  4929	            elif result.value == "interrupted":
  4930	                console.logger.info("[yellow]⏸️ Update interrupted - resume with 'dopemux update resume'[/yellow]")
  4931	            else:
  4932	                console.logger.error("[red]❌ Update failed[/red]")
  4933	                sys.exit(1)
  4934	
  4935	    except Exception as e:
  4936	        console.logger.error(f"[red]❌ Update command failed: {e}[/red]")
  4937	        if ctx.obj and ctx.obj.get('verbose'):
  4938	            import traceback
  4939	            traceback.print_exc()
  4940	        sys.exit(1)
  4941

  4943	@update.command()
  4944	@click.pass_context
  4945	def resume(ctx):
  4946	    """
  4947	    ▶️ Resume interrupted update from last checkpoint
  4948	
  4949	    Continues an update that was interrupted by user or system failure.
  4950	    Uses automatic checkpointing to resume from the exact point of interruption.
  4951	    """
  4952	    import asyncio
  4953	    from .update import UpdateManager, UpdateConfig
  4954	
  4955	    try:
  4956	        # Create manager with resume configuration
  4957	        config = UpdateConfig(checkpoint_saves=True)
  4958	        manager = UpdateManager(config=config, project_root=Path.cwd())
  4959	
  4960	        console.logger.info("[cyan]🔄 Resuming interrupted update...[/cyan]")
  4961	        result = asyncio.run(manager.run_update())
  4962	
  4963	        if result.value == "success":
  4964	            console.logger.info("[green]✅ Update resumed and completed successfully![/green]")
  4965	        else:
  4966	            console.logger.error(f"[red]❌ Update resume failed: {result.value}[/red]")
  4967	            sys.exit(1)
  4968	
  4969	    except Exception as e:
  4970	        console.logger.error(f"[red]❌ Resume command failed: {e}[/red]")
  4971	        if ctx.obj and ctx.obj.get('verbose'):
  4972	            import traceback
  4973	            traceback.print_exc()
  4974	        sys.exit(1)

  4977	@update.command()
  4978	@click.option(
  4979	    "--backup-name",
  4980	    help="Specific backup to rollback to (interactive selection if not provided)"
  4981	)
  4982	@click.option(
  4983	    "--list-backups",
  4984	    is_flag=True,
  4985	    help="List available backups and exit"
  4986	)
  4987	@click.pass_context
  4988	def rollback(ctx, backup_name: Optional[str], list_backups: bool):
  4989	    """
  4990	    ⏪ Rollback to previous system state
  4991	
  4992	    Safely restore the system to a previous working state using automatic backups.
  4993	    Includes database restoration, configuration rollback, and service restart.
  4994	    """
  4995	    import asyncio
  4996	    from .update import RollbackManager
  4997	
  4998	    try:
  4999	        manager = RollbackManager(project_root=Path.cwd())
  5000	
  5001	        if list_backups:
  5002	            # List available backups
  5003	            backups = manager.list_available_backups()
  5004	
  5005	            if not backups:
  5006	                console.logger.info("[yellow]No backups available[/yellow]")
  5007	                return
  5008	
  5009	            console.logger.info("\n[bold]Available Backups:[/bold]")
  5010	            table = Table(show_header=True, header_style="bold magenta")
  5011	            table.add_column("Name", style="cyan")
  5012	            table.add_column("Created", style="dim")
  5013	            table.add_column("Version", style="green")
  5014	            table.add_column("Size", style="blue")
  5015	
  5016	            for backup in backups:
  5017	                backup_path = Path(backup['path'])
  5018	                created = backup['created_at'][:19].replace('T', ' ')
  5019	                version = backup.get('version_from', 'unknown')
  5020	                size = backup.get('size', 'unknown')
  5021	
  5022	                table.add_row(backup_path.name, created, version, size)
  5023	
  5024	            console.logger.info(table)
  5025	            return
  5026	
  5027	        # Perform rollback
  5028	        console.logger.info("[yellow]🔄 Initiating system rollback...[/yellow]")
  5029	        success = asyncio.run(manager.manual_rollback(backup_name))
  5030	
  5031	        if success:
  5032	            console.logger.info("[green]✅ Rollback completed successfully![/green]")
  5033	        else:
  5034	            console.logger.error("[red]❌ Rollback failed[/red]")
  5035	            sys.exit(1)
  5036	
  5037	    except Exception as e:
  5038	        console.logger.error(f"[red]❌ Rollback command failed: {e}[/red]")
  5039	        if ctx.obj and ctx.obj.get('verbose'):
  5040	            import traceback
  5041	            traceback.print_exc()
  5042	        sys.exit(1)
  5043

  5046	@click.pass_context

  5048	    """

  5050	
  5051	    Displays current version, available updates, system health,
  5052	    and update history.
  5053	    """
  5054	    import asyncio
  5055	    from .update import UpdateManager
  5056	    from .update.health import HealthChecker
  5057	
  5058	    try:
  5059	        manager = UpdateManager(project_root=Path.cwd())
  5060	        health_checker = HealthChecker(project_root=Path.cwd())
  5061	
  5062	        console.logger.info("[cyan]📊 Dopemux System Status[/cyan]\n")
  5063	
  5064	        # Version information
  5065	        version_info = manager.check_for_updates()
  5066	        console.logger.info(f"[bold]Current Version:[/bold] {version_info.current}")
  5067	        console.logger.info(f"[bold]Latest Version:[/bold] {version_info.target}")
  5068	
  5069	        if version_info.current != version_info.target:
  5070	            console.logger.info(f"[yellow]📦 Update available: {version_info.current} → {version_info.target}[/yellow]")
  5071	        else:
  5072	            console.logger.info("[green]✅ System is up to date[/green]")
  5073	
  5074	        # Health status
  5075	        console.logger.info("\n[bold]System Health:[/bold]")
  5076	        health_results = asyncio.run(health_checker.check_all_services())
  5077	
  5078	        healthy_count = sum(health_results.values())
  5079	        total_count = len(health_results)
  5080	
  5081	        if healthy_count == total_count:
  5082	            console.logger.info(f"[green]✅ All services healthy ({healthy_count}/{total_count})[/green]")
  5083	        else:
  5084	            console.logger.info(f"[yellow]⚠️ {total_count - healthy_count} services need attention ({healthy_count}/{total_count})[/yellow]")
  5085	
  5086	            # Show unhealthy services
  5087	            unhealthy = [service for service, healthy in health_results.items() if not healthy]
  5088	            for service in unhealthy:
  5089	                console.logger.info(f"  [red]❌ {service}[/red]")
  5090	
  5091	    except Exception as e:
  5092	        console.logger.error(f"[red]❌ Status command failed: {e}[/red]")
  5093	        if ctx.obj and ctx.obj.get('verbose'):
  5094	            import traceback
  5095	            traceback.print_exc()
  5096	        sys.exit(1)
  5097

  5099	def _show_update_plan(plan):
  5100	    """Show update plan in user-friendly format."""
  5101	    version_info = plan['version_info']
  5102	
  5103	    console.logger.info(f"\n[bold]📋 Update Plan: v{version_info['current']} → v{version_info['target']}[/bold]")
  5104	
  5105	    if version_info['current'] == version_info['target']:
  5106	        console.logger.info("[green]✅ Already up to date![/green]")
  5107	        return
  5108	
  5109	    # Show what will be updated
  5110	    table = Table(show_header=True, header_style="bold cyan")
  5111	    table.add_column("Component", style="cyan")
  5112	    table.add_column("Action", style="yellow")
  5113	    table.add_column("Details")
  5114	
  5115	    table.add_row("Code", "🔄 Update", "Pull latest changes from git")
  5116	    table.add_row("Dependencies", "📦 Update", "Python and Node.js packages")
  5117	    table.add_row("Docker", "🐳 Rebuild", "Update container images")
  5118	    table.add_row("Configuration", "⚙️ Merge", "Preserve local customizations")
  5119	
  5120	    if version_info.get('requires_migration'):
  5121	        table.add_row("Database", "🔄 Migrate", "Apply schema changes")
  5122	
  5123	    console.logger.info(table)
  5124	
  5125	    # Show estimates
  5126	    console.logger.info(f"\n[dim]⏱️ Estimated time: {plan.get('estimated_time', '15-20 minutes')}[/dim]")
  5127	    console.logger.info(f"[dim]💾 Backup size: {plan.get('backup_size', '~250 MB')}[/dim]")
  5128	
  5129	    # Show phases
  5130	    phases = plan.get('phases', [])
  5131	    if phases:
  5132	        console.logger.info(f"\n[bold]Phases:[/bold] {' → '.join(phases)}")

  5150

  5239	@profile.command("auto-enable")

  5241	@click.option("--threshold", "-t", type=float, help="Confidence threshold (default: 0.85)")
  5242	@click.pass_context
  5243	def profile_auto_enable_cmd(ctx, check_interval: Optional[int], threshold: Optional[float]):
  5244	    """🔍 Enable auto-detection with gentle profile suggestions."""

  5246	        from .auto_detection_service import AutoDetectionService, create_default_settings
  5247

  5254	        service = AutoDetectionService(config_file=config_file)
  5255	
  5256	        if check_interval:
  5257	            service.config.check_interval_seconds = check_interval
  5258	        if threshold:
  5259	            service.config.confidence_threshold = threshold
  5260

  5262	        service.config.save(config_file)

  5267	        console.logger.info(f"   Quiet hours: {service.config.quiet_hours_start}-{service.config.quiet_hours_end}")
  5268	        console.logger.info(f"\n[dim]💡 Service will suggest profile switches when confidence >{service.config.confidence_threshold:.0%}[/dim]")
  5269	        console.logger.info(f"[dim]💡 Edit settings: {config_file}[/dim]")

  5271	    except Exception as e:

  5338	@profile.command("stats")
  5339	@click.option("--days", "-d", type=int, default=30, help="Days of history to analyze (default: 30)")
  5340	@click.pass_context
  5341	def profile_stats_cmd(ctx, days: int):
  5342	    """📊 Show profile usage analytics and trends."""
  5343	    try:
  5344	        from .profile_analytics import get_stats_sync, display_stats
  5345	
  5346	        workspace_id = str(Path.cwd())
  5347	
  5348	        # Get stats from ConPort
  5349	        console.logger.info(f"[cyan]📊 Analyzing profile usage (last {days} days)...[/cyan]\n")
  5350	        stats = get_stats_sync(workspace_id, days_back=days)
  5351	
  5352	        # Display with visual dashboard
  5353	        display_stats(stats, days_back=days)
  5354	
  5355	        # Optimization suggestions (if enough data)
  5356	        if stats.total_switches >= 10:
  5357	            console.logger.info(f"\n[bold]💡 Optimization Suggestions:[/bold]")
  5358	
  5359	            # Suggest based on patterns
  5360	            if stats.switch_accuracy < 70:
  5361	                console.logger.info(f"   • [yellow]Low accuracy ({stats.switch_accuracy:.0f}%)[/yellow]: Consider refining auto-detection rules")
  5362	
  5363	            if stats.auto_switches == 0 and stats.total_switches > 20:
  5364	                console.logger.info(f"   • [cyan]All manual switches[/cyan]: Try 'dopemux profile auto-enable' for suggestions")
  5365	
  5366	            if stats.suggestion_declined > stats.suggestion_accepted * 2:
  5367	                console.logger.info(f"   • [yellow]Many declined suggestions[/yellow]: Lower confidence threshold or adjust profile rules")
  5368	
  5369	            # Suggest creating a new profile for common patterns
  5370	            if stats.most_used_profile and stats.usage_by_profile.get(stats.most_used_profile, 0) > stats.total_switches * 0.7:
  5371	                console.logger.info(f"   • [green]Stable workflow detected[/green]: Your '{stats.most_used_profile}' profile is well-matched!")
  5372	
  5373	    except Exception as e:
  5374	        console.logger.error(f"[red]Error: {e}[/red]")
  5375	        if ctx.obj.get("verbose"):
  5376	            raise
  5377	        sys.exit(1)

  5411	@profile.command("show")
  5412	@click.argument("profile_name")
  5413	@click.option("--profile-dir", "-d", help="Profile directory path", type=click.Path(exists=True))
  5414	@click.option("--raw", "-r", is_flag=True, help="Show raw YAML content")
  5415	@click.pass_context
  5416	def profile_show_cmd(ctx, profile_name: str, profile_dir: Optional[str], raw: bool):
  5417	    """📄 Show detailed profile information."""
  5418	    try:
  5419	        parser = ProfileParser(Path(profile_dir) if profile_dir else None)
  5420	        profile_paths = parser.discover_profiles()
  5421	
  5422	        # Find matching profile
  5423	        profile_path = None
  5424	        for path in profile_paths:
  5425	            if path.stem == profile_name:
  5426	                profile_path = path
  5427	                break
  5428	
  5429	        if not profile_path:
  5430	            console.logger.info(f"[red]Profile '{profile_name}' not found[/red]")
  5431	            console.logger.info(f"\nAvailable profiles in {parser.profile_dir}:")
  5432	            for path in profile_paths:
  5433	                console.logger.info(f"  • {path.stem}")
  5434	            sys.exit(1)
  5435	
  5436	        # Show raw YAML if requested
  5437	        if raw:
  5438	            console.logger.info(f"\n[cyan]Profile: {profile_name}[/cyan]")
  5439	            console.logger.info(f"[dim]Path: {profile_path}[/dim]\n")
  5440	            with open(profile_path, 'r') as f:
  5441	                console.logger.info(f.read())
  5442	            return
  5443	
  5444	        # Load and validate profile
  5445	        p = parser.load_profile(profile_path)
  5446	
  5447	        # Display formatted profile info
  5448	        console.logger.info(f"\n[bold cyan]Profile: {p.display_name}[/bold cyan]")
  5449	        console.logger.info(f"[dim]Name: {p.name}[/dim]")
  5450	        console.logger.info(f"[dim]File: {profile_path}[/dim]\n")
  5451	
  5452	        console.logger.info(f"[bold]Description:[/bold] {p.description}\n")
  5453	
  5454	        # MCP Servers
  5455	        console.logger.info("[bold]MCP Servers:[/bold]")
  5456	        for mcp in p.mcps:
  5457	            console.logger.info(f"  • {mcp}")
  5458	
  5459	        # ADHD Config (if present)
  5460	        if p.adhd_config:
  5461	            console.logger.info("\n[bold]ADHD Configuration:[/bold]")
  5462	            console.logger.info(f"  Energy preference: {p.adhd_config.energy_preference}")
  5463	            console.logger.info(f"  Attention mode: {p.adhd_config.attention_mode}")
  5464	            console.logger.info(f"  Session duration: {p.adhd_config.session_duration} minutes")
  5465	
  5466	        # Auto-detection rules (if present)
  5467	        if p.auto_detection:
  5468	            console.logger.info("\n[bold]Auto-Detection Rules:[/bold]")
  5469	            if p.auto_detection.git_branches:
  5470	                console.logger.info("  Git branches:")
  5471	                for branch in p.auto_detection.git_branches:
  5472	                    console.logger.info(f"    • {branch}")
  5473	            if p.auto_detection.directories:
  5474	                console.logger.info("  Directories:")
  5475	                for dir in p.auto_detection.directories:
  5476	                    console.logger.info(f"    • {dir}")
  5477	            if p.auto_detection.file_patterns:
  5478	                console.logger.info("  File patterns:")
  5479	                for pattern in p.auto_detection.file_patterns:
  5480	                    console.logger.info(f"    • {pattern}")
  5481	            if p.auto_detection.time_windows:
  5482	                console.logger.info("  Time windows:")
  5483	                for window in p.auto_detection.time_windows:
  5484	                    console.logger.info(f"    • {window}")
  5485	
  5486	        console.logger.info(f"\n[green]✓ Profile is valid[/green]")
  5487	
  5488	    except ProfileValidationError as e:
  5489	        console.logger.error(f"[red]Validation Error:[/red] {e.reason}")
  5490	        if e.fix_suggestion:
  5491	            console.logger.info(f"[yellow]Suggestion:[/yellow] {e.fix_suggestion}")
  5492	        sys.exit(1)
  5493	    except FileNotFoundError as e:
  5494	        console.logger.error(f"[red]Error: {e}[/red]")
  5495	        sys.exit(1)
  5496	    except Exception as e:
  5497	        console.logger.error(f"[red]Unexpected error: {e}[/red]")
  5498	        if ctx.obj.get("verbose"):
  5499	            raise
  5500	        sys.exit(1)

  5503	@profile.command("validate")
  5504	@click.argument("profile_name", required=False)
  5505	@click.option("--profile-dir", "-d", help="Profile directory path", type=click.Path(exists=True))
  5506	@click.option("--all", "-a", is_flag=True, help="Validate all profiles")
  5507	@click.pass_context
  5508	def profile_validate_cmd(ctx, profile_name: Optional[str], profile_dir: Optional[str], all: bool):
  5509	    """✅ Validate profile YAML and configuration."""
  5510	    try:
  5511	        parser = ProfileParser(Path(profile_dir) if profile_dir else None)
  5512	
  5513	        if all:
  5514	            # Validate all profiles
  5515	            console.logger.info("[cyan]Validating all profiles...[/cyan]\n")
  5516	            profile_set = parser.load_all_profiles(fail_fast=False)
  5517	
  5518	            # Show results
  5519	            table = Table(title="Validation Results", show_header=True, header_style="bold cyan")
  5520	            table.add_column("Profile", style="cyan")
  5521	            table.add_column("Status", style="white")
  5522	            table.add_column("Message", style="white", no_wrap=False)
  5523	
  5524	            for p in profile_set.profiles:
  5525	                table.add_row(p.name, "[green]✓ Valid[/green]", f"{len(p.mcps)} MCP servers")
  5526	
  5527	            for path, error in profile_set.errors:
  5528	                error_msg = str(error)
  5529	                if isinstance(error, ProfileValidationError):
  5530	                    error_msg = f"{error.reason}"
  5531	                table.add_row(path.stem, "[red]✗ Invalid[/red]", error_msg)
  5532	
  5533	            console.logger.info(table)
  5534	
  5535	            # Summary
  5536	            total = len(profile_set.profiles) + len(profile_set.errors)
  5537	            valid = len(profile_set.profiles)
  5538	            console.logger.info(f"\n[bold]Summary:[/bold] {valid}/{total} profiles valid")
  5539	
  5540	            if profile_set.errors:
  5541	                sys.exit(1)
  5542	
  5543	        else:
  5544	            # Validate single profile
  5545	            if not profile_name:
  5546	                console.logger.error("[red]Error: Provide a profile name or use --all[/red]")
  5547	                console.logger.info("Usage: dopemux profile validate <profile_name>")
  5548	                console.logger.info("   or: dopemux profile validate --all")
  5549	                sys.exit(1)
  5550	
  5551	            profile_paths = parser.discover_profiles()
  5552	            profile_path = None
  5553	            for path in profile_paths:
  5554	                if path.stem == profile_name:
  5555	                    profile_path = path
  5556	                    break
  5557	
  5558	            if not profile_path:
  5559	                console.logger.info(f"[red]Profile '{profile_name}' not found[/red]")
  5560	                sys.exit(1)
  5561	
  5562	            console.logger.info(f"[cyan]Validating profile: {profile_name}[/cyan]\n")
  5563	
  5564	            # Load and validate
  5565	            p = parser.load_profile(profile_path)
  5566	
  5567	            console.logger.info(f"[green]✓ YAML syntax is valid[/green]")
  5568	            console.logger.info(f"[green]✓ Profile schema is valid[/green]")
  5569	            console.logger.info(f"[green]✓ All {len(p.mcps)} MCP servers are configured[/green]")
  5570	            if p.adhd_config:
  5571	                console.logger.info(f"[green]✓ ADHD configuration is valid[/green]")
  5572	            if p.auto_detection:
  5573	                console.logger.info(f"[green]✓ Auto-detection rules are valid[/green]")
  5574	
  5575	            console.logger.info(f"\n[bold green]Profile '{profile_name}' is valid ✓[/bold green]")
  5576	
  5577	    except ProfileValidationError as e:
  5578	        console.logger.error(f"[red]✗ Validation failed:[/red] {e.reason}")
  5579	        if e.fix_suggestion:
  5580	            console.logger.info(f"[yellow]💡 Suggestion:[/yellow] {e.fix_suggestion}")
  5581	        sys.exit(1)
  5582	    except FileNotFoundError as e:
  5583	        console.logger.error(f"[red]Error: {e}[/red]")
  5584	        sys.exit(1)
  5585	    except Exception as e:
  5586	        console.logger.error(f"[red]Unexpected error: {e}[/red]")
  5587	        if ctx.obj.get("verbose"):
  5588	            raise
  5589	        sys.exit(1)
  5590	
  5591

  5704	@worktrees.command("switch")
  5705	@click.argument("branch")
  5706	@click.option("--no-fuzzy", is_flag=True, help="Disable fuzzy matching")
  5707	@click.pass_context
  5708	def worktrees_switch_cmd(ctx, branch: str, no_fuzzy: bool):
  5709	    """[DEPRECATED] Use shell integration instead - see 'dopemux shell-setup'."""
  5710	    click.secho("\n⚠️  WARNING: This command cannot change your shell's directory", fg="yellow", bold=True)
  5711	    click.secho("This is a fundamental POSIX limitation, not a bug.\n", fg="yellow")
  5712	
  5713	    click.secho("Why it doesn't work:", fg="cyan")
  5714	    click.echo("  • Python runs in a subprocess")
  5715	    click.echo("  • Subprocesses cannot modify the parent shell's working directory")
  5716	    click.echo("  • This affects ALL programming languages, not just Python\n")
  5717	
  5718	    # Offer automated shell integration installation (Phase 3: UX Polish)
  5719	    click.secho("✅ Solution: Install shell integration", fg="green", bold=True)
  5720	
  5721	    from .shell_integration_installer import ShellIntegrationInstaller
  5722	
  5723	    installer = ShellIntegrationInstaller()
  5724	
  5725	    if installer.is_supported() and not installer.is_installed():
  5726	        click.echo("\n[Option 1] Automated installation (recommended):")
  5727	        click.echo("  We can install shell integration automatically right now!")
  5728	
  5729	        if click.confirm("  Install automatically?", default=True):
  5730	            success, message = installer.install(auto_confirm=True)
  5731	
  5732	            if success:
  5733	                click.secho(f"\n🎉 {message}", fg="green", bold=True)
  5734	                click.echo(f"\nActivate now: source ~/{'.' + installer.shell_name + 'rc'}")
  5735	                click.echo(f"Then try: dwt {branch}\n")
  5736	                ctx.exit(0)
  5737	            else:
  5738	                click.secho(f"\n❌ {message}", fg="red")
  5739	                click.echo("Falling back to manual instructions...\n")
  5740	        else:
  5741	            click.echo("\n[Option 2] Manual installation:")
  5742	    else:
  5743	        click.echo("\n[Manual installation]:")
  5744	
  5745	    click.echo("  1. Run: dopemux shell-setup bash >> ~/.bashrc")
  5746	    click.echo("  2. Run: source ~/.bashrc")
  5747	    click.echo(f"  3. Use: dwt {branch}\n")
  5748	
  5749	    click.secho("Alternative: Use the workaround command", fg="cyan")
  5750	    click.echo(f"  cd $(dopemux worktrees switch-path {branch})\n")
  5751	
  5752	    ctx.exit(1)

  5766	# Shell Integration Command
  5767	# =============================================================================
  5768	
  5769	@cli.command("shell-setup")
  5770	@click.argument("shell_type", type=click.Choice(["bash", "zsh"], case_sensitive=False))
  5771	@click.pass_context
  5772	def shell_setup_cmd(ctx, shell_type: str):
  5773	    """🐚 Output shell integration code for worktree switching.
  5774	
  5775	    This command outputs shell functions that enable proper worktree switching.
  5776	    Python subprocesses cannot change the parent shell's directory, so we provide
  5777	    shell functions that execute 'cd' in the shell's context.
  5778	
  5779	    Usage:
  5780	        dopemux shell-setup bash >> ~/.bashrc && source ~/.bashrc
  5781	        dopemux shell-setup zsh >> ~/.zshrc && source ~/.zshrc
  5782	
  5783	    Then use:
  5784	        dwt <branch>   # Switch to worktree with fuzzy matching
  5785	        dwtls          # List all worktrees
  5786	        dwtcur         # Show current worktree
  5787	    """
  5788	    import importlib.resources
  5789	
  5790	    # Read the shell integration script
  5791	    script_path = Path(__file__).parent.parent.parent / "scripts" / "shell_integration.sh"
  5792	
  5793	    if not script_path.exists():
  5794	        click.secho(f"❌ Shell integration script not found: {script_path}", fg="red", err=True)
  5795	        ctx.exit(1)
  5796	
  5797	    try:
  5798	        content = script_path.read_text()
  5799	
  5800	        # Output header
  5801	        click.echo(f"\n# Dopemux Shell Integration ({shell_type})")
  5802	        click.echo(f"# Generated: {datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')}")
  5803	        click.echo("# Source: dopemux shell-setup\n")
  5804	
  5805	        # Output the integration code
  5806	        click.echo(content)
  5807	
  5808	        # Usage instructions to stderr so they don't pollute the output
  5809	        click.echo("\n# Installation complete! Restart your shell or run:", err=True)
  5810	        if shell_type == "bash":
  5811	            click.echo("#   source ~/.bashrc", err=True)
  5812	        else:
  5813	            click.echo("#   source ~/.zshrc", err=True)
  5814	        click.echo("#", err=True)
  5815	        click.echo("# Then use:", err=True)
  5816	        click.echo("#   dwt <branch>   - Switch to worktree", err=True)
  5817	        click.echo("#   dwtls          - List worktrees", err=True)
  5818	        click.echo("#   dwtcur         - Current worktree", err=True)
  5819	
  5820	    except Exception as e:
  5821	        click.secho(f"❌ Error reading shell integration: {e}", fg="red", err=True)
  5822	        ctx.exit(1)
  5823	
  5824	
  5825	        logger.error(f"Error: {e}")
  5826	# Worktree Diagnostics Command
  5827	# =============================================================================
  5828	
  5829	@cli.command("doctor")
  5830	@click.option("--worktree", is_flag=True, help="Run worktree-specific diagnostics")
  5831	@click.option("--verbose", "-v", is_flag=True, help="Show detailed information")
  5832	@click.pass_context
  5833	def doctor_cmd(ctx, worktree: bool, verbose: bool):
  5834	    """🏥 Run system diagnostics and health checks.
  5835	
  5836	    Comprehensive health check for Dopemux configuration, workspace detection,
  5837	    MCP servers, and worktree system.
  5838	
  5839	    Examples:
  5840	        dopemux doctor                # General health check
  5841	        dopemux doctor --worktree     # Worktree system check
  5842	        dopemux doctor --worktree -v  # Detailed worktree diagnostics
  5843	    """
  5844	    if worktree:
  5845	        # Phase 1-3 worktree diagnostics
  5846	        from .worktree_diagnostics import run_diagnostics
  5847	
  5848	        success = run_diagnostics(verbose=verbose)
  5849	        sys.exit(0 if success else 1)
  5850	    else:
  5851	        # General Dopemux health check
  5852	        console.logger.info("\n[bold cyan]🏥 Dopemux System Diagnostics[/bold cyan]\n")
  5853	        console.logger.info("[yellow]Use --worktree flag for worktree-specific checks[/yellow]\n")
  5854	
  5855	        # Basic checks
  5856	        checks = []
  5857	
  5858	        config_manager: ConfigManager = ctx.obj.get("config_manager") if ctx.obj else ConfigManager()
  5859	        mobile_cfg = config_manager.get_mobile_config()
  5860	
  5861	        # 1. Check if dopemux is initialized
  5862	        workspace = Path.cwd()
  5863	        dopemux_dir = workspace / ".dopemux"
  5864	        checks.append(("Dopemux initialized", dopemux_dir.exists()))
  5865	
  5866	        # 2. Check environment variables
  5867	        checks.append(("ANTHROPIC_API_KEY set", bool(os.getenv("ANTHROPIC_API_KEY"))))
  5868	        checks.append(("VOYAGE_API_KEY set", bool(os.getenv("VOYAGE_API_KEY"))))
  5869	
  5870	        # 3. Check Docker (for MCP servers)
  5871	        try:
  5872	            subprocess.run(["docker", "version"], capture_output=True, check=True, timeout=5)
  5873	            checks.append(("Docker available", True))
  5874	        except Exception as e:
  5875	            checks.append(("Docker available", False))
  5876	
  5877	            logger.error(f"Error: {e}")
  5878	        # 4. Mobile prerequisites
  5879	        happy_present = shutil.which("happy") is not None
  5880	        checks.append(("Happy CLI available", happy_present))
  5881	
  5882	        claude_present = shutil.which("claude") is not None
  5883	        checks.append(("Claude CLI available", claude_present))
  5884	
  5885	        if mobile_cfg.happy_server_url:
  5886	            parsed = urlparse(mobile_cfg.happy_server_url)
  5887	            host = parsed.hostname
  5888	            port = parsed.port or (443 if parsed.scheme == "https" else 80)
  5889	            reachable = False
  5890	            if host:
  5891	                try:
  5892	                    with socket.create_connection((host, port), timeout=3):
  5893	                        reachable = True
  5894	                except Exception as e:
  5895	                    reachable = False
  5896	                    logger.error(f"Error: {e}")
  5897	            checks.append((f"Happy relay reachable ({mobile_cfg.happy_server_url})", reachable))
  5898	
  5899	        # Print results
  5900	        from rich.table import Table
  5901	        table = Table(show_header=False)
  5902	        table.add_column("Check", style="bold")
  5903	        table.add_column("Status")
  5904	
  5905	        passed = 0
  5906	        for check_name, result in checks:
  5907	            status = "[green]✅ Pass[/green]" if result else "[red]❌ Fail[/red]"
  5908	            table.add_row(check_name, status)
  5909	            if result:
  5910	                passed += 1
  5911	
  5912	        console.logger.info(table)
  5913	
  5914	        # Summary
  5915	        console.logger.info(f"\n[bold]Result:[/bold] {passed}/{len(checks)} checks passed")
  5916	
  5917	        if passed == len(checks):
  5918	            console.logger.info("[green]🎉 System healthy![/green]")
  5919	        else:
  5920	            console.logger.error("[yellow]⚠️  Some checks failed. See above for details.[/yellow]")
  5921	
  5922	        sys.exit(0 if passed == len(checks) else 1)
  5923

  6057	# Code command group - dedicated vanilla agent interface
  6058	@cli.group()
  6059	@click.pass_context
  6060	def code(ctx):
  6061	    """
  6062	    🧠 AI Code Repair - Vanilla Agent
  6063	
  6064	    Quick and reliable code fixes using traditional LLM-based iterative repair.
  6065	    Best for straightforward bugs and rapid development cycles.
  6066	
  6067	    Examples:
  6068	        dopemux code repair "undefined variable error" --file script.py
  6069	        dopemux code analyze "null pointer issue" --file app.py
  6070	        dopemux code status
  6071	    """
  6072	    pass
  6073	
  6074	
  6075	@code.command()
  6076	@click.argument('bug_description')
  6077	@click.option('--file', '-f', 'file_path', help='Path to file containing the bug')
  6078	@click.option('--line', '-l', type=int, help='Line number where bug occurs')
  6079	@click.option('--verbose', '-v', is_flag=True, help='Enable verbose output')
  6080	@click.option('--dry-run', is_flag=True, help='Show what would be done without making changes')
  6081	@click.pass_context
  6082	def repair(ctx, bug_description, file_path, line, verbose, dry_run):
  6083	    """
  6084	    Repair code using the vanilla agent.
  6085	
  6086	    BUG_DESCRIPTION: Description of the bug to fix
  6087	
  6088	    Examples:
  6089	        dopemux code repair "variable not defined" --file script.py --line 42
  6090	        dopemux code repair "null pointer exception" --file app.py --verbose
  6091	    """
  6092	    # Import here to avoid circular dependencies
  6093	    try:
  6094	        # Add services to Python path if needed
  6095	        import sys
  6096	        from pathlib import Path
  6097	        services_path = Path(__file__).resolve().parent.parent / 'services'
  6098	        if str(services_path) not in sys.path:
  6099	            sys.path.insert(0, str(services_path))
  6100	
  6101	        from genetic_agent.vanilla.vanilla_agent import VanillaAgent
  6102	        from genetic_agent.core.config import AgentConfig
  6103	        import asyncio
  6104	
  6105	        async def run_repair():
  6106	            config = AgentConfig()
  6107	            agent = VanillaAgent(config)
  6108	
  6109	            task = {
  6110	                "bug_description": bug_description,
  6111	                "file_path": file_path or "",
  6112	                "line_number": line or 0
  6113	            }
  6114	
  6115	            if dry_run:
  6116	                console.logger.info("[yellow]🔍 Dry run mode - analyzing bug without repair[/yellow]")
  6117	                analysis = await agent._analyze_bug(bug_description, file_path or "", line or 0)
  6118	                console.logger.info("Analysis Results:")
  6119	                console.logger.info(f"  Description: {analysis.get('description', 'N/A')}")
  6120	                console.logger.info(f"  Complexity: {analysis.get('complexity', {}).get('score', 'N/A')}")
  6121	                console.logger.info(f"  Similar patterns: {len(analysis.get('similar_patterns', {}).get('results', []))}")
  6122	                return
  6123	
  6124	            result = await agent.process_task(task)
  6125	
  6126	            if result.get('success'):
  6127	                console.logger.info("[green]✅ Repair successful![/green]")
  6128	                console.logger.info(f"Confidence: {result.get('confidence', 0):.2f}")
  6129	                console.logger.info(f"Iterations: {result.get('iterations', 0)}")
  6130	                if result.get('repair'):
  6131	                    console.logger.info("\n[blue]Generated Repair:[/blue]")
  6132	                    console.logger.info(result['repair'])
  6133	                if result.get('explanation'):
  6134	                    console.logger.info(f"\n[yellow]Explanation:[/yellow] {result['explanation']}")
  6135	            else:
  6136	                console.logger.error("[red]❌ Repair failed[/red]")
  6137	                console.logger.error(f"Reason: {result.get('explanation', 'Unknown error')}")
  6138	                if verbose:
  6139	                    console.logger.debug(f"Debug: Iterations attempted: {result.get('iterations', 0)}")
  6140	
  6141	        asyncio.run(run_repair())
  6142	
  6143	    except Exception as e:
  6144	        console.logger.error(f"[red]❌ Code repair failed: {e}[/red]")
  6145	        if verbose:
  6146	            import traceback
  6147	            traceback.print_exc()
  6148

  6232	                "ConPort": "http://localhost:3004",
  6233	                "Serena": "http://localhost:3006",
  6234	                "Dope-Context": "http://localhost:3010"

  6239	                for service, url in host_urls.items():
  6240	                    reachable = False

  6245	                        async with session.get(health_url) as response:
  6246	                            if response.status == 200:
  6247	                                reachable = True
  6248	                            else:
  6249	                                error_msg = f"Health check failed with status {response.status}"
  6250	                    except Exception as e:
  6251	                        error_msg = f"Connection failed: {str(e)}"
  6252	
  6253	                        logger.error(f"Error: {e}")
  6254	                    status_icon = "✅" if reachable else "❌"
  6255	                    console.logger.info(f"  {status_icon} {service}")
  6256	                    if not reachable:
  6257	                        console.logger.error(f"    Error: {error_msg}")
  6258	
  6259	            console.logger.info("\n[dim]Note: Container uses Docker network names, host uses localhost[/dim]")
  6260	
  6261	        asyncio.run(show_status())
  6262	
  6263	    except Exception as e:
  6264	        console.logger.error(f"[red]❌ Status check failed: {e}[/red]")
  6265	        if verbose:
  6266	            import traceback

  6295	@memory.group()
  6296	def rollup():
  6297	    """📊 Global rollup index operations."""
  6298	    pass
  6299	
  6300	
  6301	@rollup.command()
  6302	@click.option(
  6303	    "--projects-file",
  6304	    type=click.Path(exists=True, path_type=Path),
  6305	    help="File containing list of project roots (newline or JSON)",
  6306	)
  6307	@click.option(
  6308	    "--index-path",
  6309	    type=click.Path(path_type=Path),
  6310	    help="Global index path (default: ~/.dopemux/global_index.sqlite)",
  6311	)
  6312	def build(projects_file: Optional[Path], index_path: Optional[Path]):
  6313	    """Build global rollup index from project ledgers (read-only)."""
  6314	    from dopemux.memory.global_rollup import (
  6315	        GlobalRollupIndexer,
  6316	        resolve_rollup_projects,
  6317	        GlobalRollupError,
  6318	    )
  6319	
  6320	    try:
  6321	        roots = resolve_rollup_projects(projects_file=projects_file)
  6322	        console.logger.info(f"[cyan]Resolved {len(roots)} project(s)[/cyan]")
  6323	
  6324	        indexer = GlobalRollupIndexer(index_path=index_path)
  6325	        result = indexer.build(roots)
  6326	
  6327	        console.logger.info(f"[green]✓[/green] Projects registered: {result['projects_registered']}")
  6328	        console.logger.info(f"[green]✓[/green] Pointers indexed: {result['pointers_upserted']}")
  6329	        console.logger.info(f"[green]✓[/green] Index: {result['index_path']}")
  6330	
  6331	    except GlobalRollupError as e:
  6332	        console.logger.error(f"[red]✗ Rollup error:[/red] {e}")
  6333	        raise click.Abort()
  6334	
  6335	
  6336	@rollup.command()
  6337	@click.option(
  6338	    "--index-path",
  6339	    type=click.Path(path_type=Path),
  6340	    help="Global index path (default: ~/.dopemux/global_index.sqlite)",
  6341	)
  6342	def list(index_path: Optional[Path]):
  6343	    """List registered projects in global rollup index."""
  6344	    from dopemux.memory.global_rollup import GlobalRollupIndexer
  6345	    from rich.table import Table
  6346	
  6347	    indexer = GlobalRollupIndexer(index_path=index_path)
  6348	
  6349	    projects = indexer.list_projects()
  6350	
  6351	    if not projects:
  6352	        console.logger.info("[yellow]No projects registered in global index[/yellow]")
  6353	        return
  6354	
  6355	    table = Table(title="Registered Projects")
  6356	    table.add_column("Project ID", style="cyan")
  6357	    table.add_column("Repo Root", style="green")
  6358	    table.add_column("Last Seen", style="yellow")
  6359	
  6360	    for proj in projects:
  6361	        table.add_row(
  6362	            proj["project_id"],
  6363	            proj["repo_root"],
  6364	            proj["last_seen_at"],
  6365	        )
  6366	
  6367	    console.logger.info(table)
  6368	
  6369	
  6370	@rollup.command()
  6371	@click.argument("query")
  6372	@click.option(
  6373	    "--limit",
  6374	    type=int,
  6375	    default=10,
  6376	    help="Max results (default: 10, max: 100)",
  6377	)
  6378	@click.option(
  6379	    "--index-path",
  6380	    type=click.Path(path_type=Path),
  6381	    help="Global index path (default: ~/.dopemux/global_index.sqlite)",
  6382	)
  6383	def search(query: str, limit: int, index_path: Optional[Path]):
  6384	    """Search global rollup index for promoted work log entries."""
  6385	    from dopemux.memory.global_rollup import GlobalRollupIndexer
  6386	    from rich.table import Table
  6387	
  6388	    indexer = GlobalRollupIndexer(index_path=index_path)
  6389	
  6390	    results = indexer.search(query, limit=limit)
  6391	
  6392	    if not results:
  6393	        console.logger.info(f"[yellow]No results for: {query}[/yellow]")
  6394	        return
  6395	
  6396	    table = Table(title=f"Search Results: {query}")
  6397	    table.add_column("Timestamp", style="cyan")
  6398	    table.add_column("Type", style="yellow")
  6399	    table.add_column("Summary", style="green")
  6400	    table.add_column("Project", style="blue", overflow="fold")
  6401	
  6402	    for row in results:
  6403	        table.add_row(
  6404	            row["ts_utc"],
  6405	            row["event_type"],
  6406	            row["summary"][:80] + ("..." if len(row["summary"]) > 80 else ""),
  6407	            row["project_id"][-40:],  # Last 40 chars of path
  6408	        )
  6409	
  6410	    console.logger.info(table)
  6411	    console.logger.info(f"\n[dim]Showing {len(results)} of up to {limit} results[/dim]")
  6412
